Nanso, asaana a Aparahamu, Isaki ni Sumayili, yahaavithaca athumwanaya nnikhukuni no Makipela, vakhiviru ni uManree, nthala na Eforomi, mwana a Suwari, nHitita,
nenne nthala, Aparahamu nathumanannyawe maHitita. Vaavale phivithiyawe Aparahamu wamoca ni Asaara amwaarawe.
Nanso nakhwileene Aparahamu, Nluku ahonreeriha Isaki. Vano Isaki aakhala vakhiviru ni Iluusi yo Lahayi-Royi.
Vano ula phu ucuulu wa Sumayili, mwana annyanryawe Aparahamu ni Akaari o Wiciipitu, ipottha ya Asaara.
Ala phi macina a asaana a Sumayili, yantikhaciye ittharihiyaka eyareelo aya: Nepawoti, mwana omuulupale a Sumayili, Ketari, Apeteli, Mipisamu,
Misima, Tumaa, Masaa,
Hattatti, Temaa, Yeturi, Nafisi ni Ketemaa.
Ala phaari asaana a Sumayili, yakhalacile ahooleli o mahimo, mmawaani mwaya ni mmapuroni mwamakiya yeehaneliya yaala macina ala. Ahooleli ayo yaari khumi nuuwa eeli.
Sumayili ahokhala myakha iminya wo talathiini na saapa (137) ceyarelo. Ahokhwa ni watthara mayathumwane okhalayi.
Ucuulu awe wahokhala nttetthe unkhuma o Havila urwaka o Suuri, vakhiviru ni mwiinano wo Wiciipitu, mphantte unrwaa o Siiriya. Ni yaheeserana mpika na asunnaya.
Ala phi mayaranacelo o nrukulu na Isaki, mwana Aparahamu: Aparahamu ahonnyara Isaki.
Isaki narina myakha arupayini ceyarelo, ahonthela Repeka, mwana a Petuweli, Nramewu o Patan-Aramu, aari mwanrokorawe Lapanu, ni uyo ciicammo Nramewu.
Vano Isaki ahonlepela Nluku, kontha amwaarawe ayo yari mwali eekupa. Phimaana Mwaneene Nluku ahaakhula iswali cawe nnyo ni Repeka ahorupala irukulu.
Urupala wawe, asaana ayo munthukwani mmo yaanawaanaca, ni Repeka aheera: Nlattuni ikikhumelelaka ila itthu ila? Ni ahorwaa unkoha Mwaneene Nluku.
Vano Mwaneene Nluku ahomwaakhula: Ilapo piili phiriwo munthuukwani mwaa mmo, phimaana anakhuma mommo atthu eeli ni anaahala umwalana: Mmoca uyo nokookhala okuru oompwaha nkhwawe, nanso omuulupale uyo naahala unvarela nteko omwankani uyo.
Vaavale, waphiilyaya ukati wooyara, khweeli ahorumelelihiya wiira yaari mavatta munthukwani mwawe mmwe.
Oopacera uyariya uyo aari okharari cookhwiila, ni irutthu awe yothene yaari yo mapururu; phimaana ahovahiya ncina na Isawu.
Wahoolo ahoyarya mwanhimaawe, ntata nawe naavarenle ikottokottho ya Isawu; phimaana ahovahiya ncina na Yakopi. Ukati waayarawe Repeka, Isaki aarina myakha sitiini ceyarelo.
Asaana ale yahonuwaca. Isawu aari nlupa oocuwela utotha ni aari nantakhwani. Nanso Yakopi waari nteko awe paahi uhakhela imope ni aakhala mmaheemani.
Isaki anfenta Isawu, kontha cancivela ukhura inama ceevawe; ni ciicammo Repeka anfenta Yakopi.
Nanso ikwaha imoca, Yakopi aapyaacaka yoolya, ahowa Isawu navoliye itala, akhumaka utakhwani,
ni ahommekela eeraka: Ukimeele vakani nhuci woserya uyo. Ukivola itala! Phimaana eehaninyaka ciicammo Eetomu.
Vano Yakopi ahomwaakhula eeraka: Woopacera ukitumihereke iyuulupale aa.
Vaavale Isawu aheera: Nna vaa kihanle vakani ukhwa. Kimphurela isiyani iyuulupale eyo?
Wahoolo Yakopi ahonkhanyereriha Isawu eeraka: Woopacera unlamuliya ulupela. Ni ule aholupela untumihera Yakopi iyuulupale eyo.
Vano Yakopi ahonvaha Isawu isima ni maruru. Ule aholya nuwurerya, ahonwa nurwaa. Commo Isawu ahovyavyeeha iyuulupale awe.
Yahovola itala yeele ilapo ele, toko weracilyaya ukati wa Aparahamu. Phimaana Isaki ahorwaa ilapo yo Kerari, wonwo Apimeleke waaryawe mwene o mafilisitiya.
Vano Mwaneene Nluku ahomphwanya Isaki ni ahomwiirela: Uhikhuruwele Wiciipitu. Urwee wakhale ilapo inhalaka wuthoonyera.
Ukhale ila ilapo ela, mi kinaakhala ni we ni kinawureeriha. Kontha we nuucuulu aa uyo kinaahala wuuvahani ila ilapo ela, ni kinarwa uttharihelela yolumacenryaka athumwaninyu aneehaniya Aparahamu.
Kinaahala wuncerera ucuulu aa toko itthoottwa co wirimu ni waavaha nnya ilapo nnya cothene; ni nhina wo ucuulu aa atthu othene omwiilaponi anaahala ureerihiya,
kontha Aparahamu hosunka malamulo aka inrumilyaka ni isariya caka.
Commo Isaki ahokhala o Kerari.
Vano alopwana o nenno nipuro nno ukati waankohilyaya wiira ala phamwaaraa, ule ahaakhula eeraka: Mwanrokoraka. Anawoova uhimyaca wiira amwaaraka, kontha oopuwela wiira, alopwana o yeela ilapo ela anaahala ukiiva nlattu wa Repeka, kontha ahotepa ooreera.
Isaki ahokhala o Kerari ukati mwinci. Nihuku nimoca, Apimeleke, mwene o mafilisitiya, anawehecesa wacanelani yaari uculu, phuukati wamonnyawe Isaki anthwelanaka Repeka amwaarawe.
Vano Apimeleke ahomwiihana Isaki ni ahomwiirela: Khweeli, uhirune. Ale amwaaraa. Vano weerelani mwanrokoraka? Isaki ahaakhula eeraka: Kontha kineenre amwaaraka kanawoova wiiviya.
Apimeleke aheera: Unipankenleni commo? Kontha nlopwana phi nlopwana uyo aanawaarupana amwaaraa ayo, ni wananiwiihera ikoosi.
Vaavale Apimeleke ahaahimyacera atthu othene eeraka: Ntthu nohala umwiiriha itthu ula nlopwana ula atthuna amwaarawe ala, naahala ukhwa!
Vano Isaki ahotthimpula imatta ni yooyo mwakha uyo ahoruwerya venci, kontha Mwaneene Nluku ahonreeriha.
Ule ahothaciri ni nhakhu awe wahoncererya mpaka ahothacireeha.
Ahaana ikhontwaa ni imope cinci ni ipottha cinci mpaka mafilisitiya upacera unrama.
Phimaana, mafilistiya yahotthunttuwanihaca nuuwuhelelaca iluusi cothene cathipiye ni ipottha ukati wa Aparahamu, athumwane Isaki.
Vano Apimeleke ahomwiirela Isaki: Ukhume mwilaponi mwihu mu, kontha uri ntthu oonhakhu cinenne woonipwaha hi.
Phimaana Isaki ahokhuma nuthamela wuuthakoni wo Kerari waakhalawe khalayi.
Wahoolo Isaki ahowuhulaca iluusi caathipiye ukati wathumwane. Nnye cawuhelelaciye ni mafilisitiya ukhwa wawe Aparahamu ni ahovaha macina yavahilyaya athumwane.
Vano ipottha ca Isaki cahothipaca muuthakoni mmwe ni cahottenla maasi menci oociva.
Vano ahakheli o Kerari yahonyakulihana na ahakheli a Isaki, yiirelanaka: Maasi ala awihu! Phimaana Isaki ahovaha iluusi ile ncina na Eseke, nlattu woonyakuliheraninya.
Vano ipottha nnye cahothipaca iluusi ikina, ni ile yahonyakuliheraniya. Phimaana aheehana Sitina.
Wahoolo Isaki ahothama nne nipuro nne ni ahothipa iluusi ikina ni khayanyakuliheraniye tho. Phimaana ahovaha ncina na Riyopoti, eeraka: Vano Mwaneene Nluku honihulela ikhato ninaahala wiithawala yeela ilapo ela.
Ukhuma vaavale Isaki ahorwaa o Peresepa.
Yoole uhiyu ule, Mwaneene Nluku ahomphwanya ni ahomwiirela: Mi kiri Nluku a Aparahamu athumwanaa. Uhoove, kontha kiri ni we. Mi kinaahala wureeriha ni wuncerera ucuulu aa mwanlattu woofenta karumeya aka Aparahamu.
Isaki ahoteka ikhilompi ni aholapela ncina na Mwaneene Nluku. Vaavale ahomaka ni ipottha cawe yahothipaca iluusi ikina.
Yoole ukati ule, Apimeleki ahowa akhumaka o Kerari wamoca ni Awusate nlakakano awe ni Fikoli, muulupale aanakhotto awe.
Vaavale Isaki ahaakohaca eeraka: Nlattuni mmwaaka ukiweha, mi mwahokipanka mwiinani ni mwahokoomola?
Ale yahomwaakhulaca yiiracaka: Kontha nihowoona weekhweeli wiira Mwaneene Nluku ri ni we, phimaana niiraka: Nrwee nilupelace we ni hi. Nimphavela waatana ni we.
We uhinipanke yoonanara, toko hi cihupankileehu itthu, nanso nihoopanka ratta ni wuleeha wo mpuha. Vano nihocuwela wiira Mwaneene Nluku hooreeriha.
Vano Isaki ahaavahaca yoolya ni ale yaholyaca nuuwuryaca.
Usa waya oyeeli yaholupelihana. Isaki ahaalehaca ni ale yahorwaca ni mpuha.
Nenno nihuku nno ipottha ca Isaki cahowaaca unhimerya ciiraka: Iluusi yathipehu iyo nihottenla maasi!
Isaki ahovaha iluusi ile ncina na Sepa, phimaana mpaka nihuku nolelo, ile iparasa ile icuweliyaka ncina no Peresepa.
Isawu naphihenrene myakha arupayini ceyarelo ahonthela Yutiti, mwana a Peeri, nhitita, ni ciicammo ahonthela Pasimati, mwana a Elomi, nhitita.
Ale asithiyana ale yahaacukulihaca Isaki ni Repeka.
Ukati wooluvanlyawe Isaki wiitho wawe wahonripela ni khoona. Vano ahomwiihana mwanawe omuulupale eehaniya Isawu, eeraka: Mwanaka. Ni ule ahomwaakhula eeraka: Kiri va.
Ule ahomwiirela: Mi kihooluvala ni akincuwela nihuku ninkhwaka.
Nna va, ukuse myuupa, muura ni nivaka naa nno, urwee utakhwani wakaaverye inama.
Vano waakaapyele sankanya ookicivela ni ukiwiihere kaanlye wiira kuuvahe iparakha kihinakhwa.
Ukati woolumacawe Isaki anhimeryaka mwanawe Isawu, moolumo ale Repeka eera eewaka. Vano Isawu ahorwaa utakhwani wiiva inama wiira aawiihere athumwane.
Phimaana Repeka ahonhimerya mwanawe eehaninya Yakopi eeraka: Kiheewa athumwana ayo amwiirelaka munnaa Isawu:
Wakilupatthele inama ni wakaapyeele sankanya oociva wiira kinlye ni kuuvahe iparakha wamiithoni wa Mwaneene Nluku kihinakhwa.
Nna vaa mwanaka, uviriyane inoohimeryaka ila.
Urwee muncicini mmo wakuse ipuri piili. Mi kinnowaapyela sankanya oociva toko athumwana cinaacivelaya,
ni waarwehele athumwana yanlye wiira yuvahe iparakha ahinakhwa.
Nanso Yakopi aheerela anumwane: Kinawoona amunna Isawu irutthu aya iyo iri yo mapururu. Mi kiri oohimapururu.
Pooti apaapa ayo ankokapaapela ni wamiithoni waya kinkokhala mayowootha. Commo kinawiiwaanela mahusi woohikhala iparakha.
Anumwane yahomwiirela: Mwanaka, nihusi naa nno ninhala ukhala nawaka. Wiiwelele paahi nuulumo naka. Urwele ni ukiwaanele.
Vano ule ahorwela ni waawiihera anumwane, ni ale yahomwaapyela sankanya oociva, toko athumwane caacivelaya.
Wahoolo, Repeka ahokusa coowara comaana ca Isawu, mwana omuulupale, carinawe uwaani ni ahommwariha Yakopi, mwana omwankani.
Vano ahommwariha nrapala nopuri nsiko ni mmatatani,
ni ahonvaha mmatatani mwa Yakopi, mwana omwankani, sankanya oociva ni nkatthe watthenkacilyawe.
Vano Yakopi ahorwaa woolumana athumwane ni aheerela: Paapa! Athumwane yahomwaakhula yiiraka: Kiri va. We tupani mwanaka?
Yakopi ahaakhula athumwane eeraka: Mi Isawu mwaninyu oontthaara. Kihopanka toko caakirenlenyu. Vano, munkome ni nlye ilupatthilyaka wiira nkireerihe.
Isaki ahonkoha mwanawe eeraka: Weeraceele cani wakuvaka ulupattha? Ule ahaakhula: Mwaneene Nluku, Nluku inyu ahokaakuvyehera umphwanya mwannama.
Vaavale Isaki ahomwiirela Yakopi: Mwanaka, ukaattamerye wiira kiwaapaapele ni kuucuwelele wakhala wiira we khweeli mwanaka Isawu.
Yakopi ahaattamerya athumwane ni ale yahomwapapela ni yaheera: Ncu nno na Yakopi nanso myoono nnyo ca Isawu.
Isaki khaancuwelenle Yakopi kontha myoono cawe caari co mapururu toko ca Isawu munnaawe, phimaana ahonreeriha.
Wahoolo Isaki ahonkoha tho eeraka: We khweeli mwanaka Isawu? Ni ule ahaakhula eeraka: Phi yeemi.
Vaavale Isaki ahomwiirela: Mwanaka, ukiwiihere ilupatthilyaa eyo wiira kilye ni kuureerihe. Yakopi ahaawiihera ni athumwane yaholya, ni ciicammo ahaawiihera ivinyu ni ale yahowurya.
Vano Isaki ahomwiirela Yakopi: Nkaawe woono mwanaka ni ukivahe alaahuma.
Ule ahaattamerya ni ahaavaha alaahuma. Ukati wonnyawe ikuwo cawe nnyo nhiriri wonama, Isaki ahonreeriha eeraka: Nhiriri wa mwanaka uri toko inukhelelo yotakhwa ireerihilyawe Mwaneene Nluku.
Nluku oovahe ukame wo wirimu, uruwerye vathi va, itiriku yinci ni malaaso menci.
Wiira atthu othene waarume, ni ilapo cuulemelihe, ni ukhale nkunya a asihimaa, na asaana a anumwane yuulemelihe we, natakhaliya ule nohala wuulapha, ni nareeriya ule nohala wureeriha.
Isaki umaliha wawe unreeriha Yakopi ni nakhumileene wamiithoni wa athumwane, phawawe Isawu akhumaka wulupatthani.
Ni ule ahomwaapya sankanya oociva ni ahaawiihera athumwane ni aheerela: Paapa, munnwe ni nkhuureke inama ilupatthilyaka wiira nkireerihe.
Vano athumwane yahonkoha yiiraka: We tupani? Ule ahaakhula: Mi Isawu, mwaninyu oontthara.
Vaavale Isaki ahothukumela venci cinenne ni aheera: Tupani ule kiwiihenre inama yoolupatthiya? Mi kihokhuura yothene we uhinaya uwa. Yooyo ntthu uyo, mi kihonvaha iparakha ni ciicammo nakhala ooreerihiya.
Vano Isawu weewilyawe moolumo athumwane ale, ahothulana ni unlaka ahokhuwa wowirunya eerelaka athumwane: Nkireerihe ni mi, paapa.
Isaki ahomwaakhula phimwiirelaka: Mwanhimaa ahowa va mmirukuni, ni hokusa iparakha caa nnyo.
Vaavale Isawu ahopwaherera eeraka: Khweeli ule uhomphwanela wavahiyawe ncina na Yakopi, kontha imaara piili nnya akithepyaka. Woopacera hokaakha iyuulupale aka, nna va hokaakha iparakha caka. Vano Isawu aheera tho: Khankihalihenre tho mi iparakha?
Vano Isaki ahomwaakhula Isawu eeraka: Kinawoona kihompanka ukhala owulamula we, ni asunnaa ayo othene kihonvaha ukhala ananrumiya awe; mpaka itiriku ni malaaso kihomuncerera. Vano we mwanaka kiwiiriheke cani?
Vano Isawu aheerela athumwane: Nrina iparakha imoca paahi? Paapa, nkireerihe ni mi ciicammo. Vaavale Isawu ahokhuwa ni wunla.
Vano Isaki, athumwane, yahomwaakhula yiiraka: We unkookhala uttayi ni mapuro oocayira ni oohikhuruwa ukame.
Malelyo aa ankokhala okhotto, ni unhala ukhala nanrumiya a nhimaa. Nanso we wooryaka wiicopola phinhalaa urula nipisi niri nsiko mwaa mmo.
Vano Isawu ahoncukula Yakopi mwanlattu womwakha iparakha yavahiyawe na athumwane. Phimaana ahoopuwela wanrimani wawe eeraka: Anaphiya mahuku ookhwa apaapa. Kimwomwiiva nhimaka Yakopi.
Vano Repeka ahohimerya yalakenlyawe Isawu, mwana omuulupale, ahomwiihana Yakopi mwanawe omwankani, phimwiirelaka: Munnaa Isawu neepisiha nrima ni hoolakela uwiiva.
Nna vaa, mwanaka, wiiwe inhalaka wuuhimerya: Wunwe ni urwee wamwanrokoraka Lapanu, ilapo yo Harani,
wakhale wonwo mahuku vakani, mpaka uvire uviruwa wa munnaa,
mpaka uvire urusiya wa munnaa, ni aliyale itthu impankilyaa. Mi kinaahala uleehera ni wuhokolosiha. Isiyani inhalaka wuhalelacerani oyeeli nihuku nimoca?
Phimaana Repeka ahomwiirela Isaki coo: Ahokitosa asaana a Heeti, kontha Yakopi aathelaka athiyana o yeela ilapo ela, mi phatari kikhwe.
Vano Isaki ahomwiihana Yakopi, ahonreeriha nunhimerya eeraka: Uhaathele athiyana o Nkanani mu.
Ukhume ni urwee uPatan-Aramu, wa Petuweli, athumwanaya anumwana ni wanthele mwana a Lapanu, mwanrokoraya anumwana.
Ni Nluku Okuru Cothene ureerihe, upanke mayoyara ni awuncereryanihe wiira nkhale atthu enci,
ni uvahe iparakha ca Aparahamu, we ni ucuulu aa uyo, wiira uhalane ilapo iryaa nletto, Nluku invahilyawe Aparahamu.
Phimaana Isaki ahonveleeliha Yakopi ilapo yo Patan-Aramu, wa Lapanu, mwana a Petuweli Nramewu, mwanrokorawe Repeka, anumwane Yakopi ni Isawu.
Vano Isawu woonyawe wiira Isaki honreeriha Yakopi ni honveleeliha uPatan-Aramu wiira anthele nthiyana wonwo ni waanreerihawe va ahomwiirela: Uhaathele athiyana o Nkanani mu.
Yakopi aheewelela athumwane na anumwane ni ahorwaa uPatan-Aramu.
Isawu woonyawe athumwane wiira khayatteeliye nrima na athiyana o Nkanaa,
ule ahorwaa wa Sumayili ni ahonthela nthiyana, eehaninya Malati, mwana a Sumayili, mwana a Aparahamu, mwanrokorawe Nepakoti, woohatakanihera athiyana yarinawe akina.
Yooyo ukati uyo Yakopi ahokhuma uPerisepa arwaka uHarani
ni ahophiya nipuro narupilyawe kontha waheela. Nenno nipuro nno ahokusa nluku nimoca, aheesa wiimuru ni aheecatalela.
Vano aholoha nttora woonyawe makwantta aneemesiye vathi mpaka ukwanya irimu ni phoonawe ancelo a Nluku awelaka ni akhuruwaka makwantta ayo.
Mwaneene Nluku phaari uculu waya makwantta ni aheera: Mi kiri Mwaneene Nluku, Nluku a Aparahamu, athumwana, ni Nluku a Isaki; yeela ilapo irupilyaa ila kinawuvaha we ni ucuulu aa uyo.
Ucuulu aa unhala ukhala toko ntthupi no vathi, ni unhala umwaryeela urwaka unkhuma ncuwa mpaka unkela ncuwa, urwaka uculu mpaka uhitto, ni mwanlattu wawaa we ni ucuulu aa uyo, unkophwanya iparakha uneethi wothene wo mwiilaponi.
Phi mi kiri ni we. Kinawusunka mapuro othene ankela uvira, kinawuturusela tho ila ilapo ela, kontha akinhala wuuhiya mpaka kipankeke itthu yukhuluvelihilyaka.
Vano Yakopi wunwa wawe nkhoveni aheera: Khweeli Mwaneene Nluku ri nna nipuro nna. Mi akaacuwela.
Ni uvaka aheera: Wopihilyaya nna nipuro nna! Nna khaninakhala nipuro nikina; iri inupa ya Nluku. Ula nkhora wo wirimu.
Paahi, Yakopi ahonwa wicisuru, ahokusa nluku neesilyawe wiimuru nne, aheemesa, ni ahomiinela makhura waculu waya va.
Phimaana ahovaha ncina nenno nipuro nno Peteli, nanso yeeyo iparasa eyo ncina naya nokhalayi neehaniya Luusi.
Ni Yakopi ahomoopa natiri eeraka: Nluku akhalaka ni mi ni akisunkaka ila ikwaha ila, akivahaka yoolya, ni ikuwo coowara,
ni kituruwelaka wosalama uwaani wa apaapa, Mwaneene Nluku nahala ukhala Nluku aka.
Ni nenna nluku neemesilyaka nna ninwa ukhala inupa ya Nluku ni cothene cinhalaa ukivaha, khweeli kinawuvaha mphantte wonakhumi.
Vaavale Yakopi ahokhuma arwaka ilapo iri mphantte unkhuma ncuwa.
Nanaanoru ahoona iluusi mmathalani ni mihuwo miraru cokhontwaa cinarupile nceresere mmo, kontha yeeyo iluusi iyo phawuryaya ikhontwaa nnyo. Nahaawo nluku nuulupale nakhuneliya iluusi iyo.
Nenne nipuro nne canthukumana mihuwo, ahakheli yantamiha nluku nakhuneliya iluusi iyo nuurika maasi wiira avahe mihuwo caya nuukhunela tho iluusi iyo.
Vano Yakopi ahaakohaca eeraka: Asunnnaka nnokhumaca vayi? Ni ale yahaakhulaca yiiraka: Ninkhuma uHarani.
Ni uyo aheerelaca: Nnancuwela Lapanu, mwana a Nahori? Nale yahaakhulaca yiiraka: Ninancuwela.
Ahaakohaca tho eeraka: Haawo nkumi? Ni ale yahomwaakhulaca: Haawo nkumi, ni mwanawe mwanthiyana neehaniya Rakeli phuula wiihile nnya ikhontwaa nnya.
Ule aheera tho: Nanlelo uthana, khunaphiya ukati wothukumaniha ikhontwaa nnyo. Nvahe maasi ciwurye ni nvira nliha.
Vano ale yaheeraca coo: Khaninoorya, mpaka cithukumanihiyeke ikhontwaa cothene ni nluku nikhuneeliye iluusi iyo nitamihiye wiira nivahe ratta maasi oowurya.
Nanlelo oolumacaka nale, ahowa Rakeli ni ikhontwaa ca athumwane kontha uyo aari nhakheli.
Ni waakhumelenle coo, Yakopi umoona wawe Rakeli mwana a Lapanu arokoraya anumwane, ni ikhontwaa ca Lapanu, Yakopi ahorwaa walusi ni ahotamiha nluku nakhuneleliye nuuvaha uwurya ikhontwaa ca Lapanu, mwanrokoraya anumwane.
Vaavale Yakopi ahonsalameeha Rakeli, mpaka upacera wunla.
Yakopi ahonhimerya Rakeli wiira ule mwamunnaya athumwane ni ari mwana a Repeka. Vano Rakeli ahokhuma atthawaka urwaa wahimyacera athumwane.
Ukati weewilyawe Lapanu ihapari ca Yakopi, mwana a mwanrokorawe, ahomwiikamela nuunkapatta nuunsalameeha mpaka umpiiha uwaanyawe, ni ule ahonttonkacera Lapanu citthu cothene caankhumelenle munkwahani mwawe.
Vano Lapanu ahomwiirela: Khweeli we uri nikhuva ni irutthu aka. Ni ahokhala ni ule mweeri mmoca.
Wahoolo Lapanu ahomwiirela Yakopi: Kamana we uri nhimaaka unaakivarela nteko wo mahala? Ukihimerye ihisapu yowuliva.
Lapanu ahaana asaana eeli asithiyana. Omuulupale uyo ncina nawe Leya ni omwankani uyo ncina nawe Rakeli.
Vano Leya arina miitho oolocwaca nanso Rakeli arina irutthu yooreera ni ikhove yomaana.
Ni Yakopi anancivela venci Rakeli ni aheera: Kinaawuvarela nteko myakha saapa nlattu wa Rakeli, mwanaa oomwankani.
Vano Lapanu ahaakhula eeraka: Wanaareera wuvaha we woohikhala wumvaha nlopwana nkina. Ukhale va ni mi.
Yakopi ahovara nteko myakha saapa amphavelaka Rakeli, cenyo myakha nnyo oonne ukhala mahuku vakani kontha anancivela cineene.
Wahoolo Yakopi ahomwiirela Lapanu: Ukivahe amwaaraka, kontha kihomalihera mahuku aka ayo ni kimphavela waathela.
Vano Lapanu ahaathukumaniha alopwana othene o yoole nttetthe ole ni ahopanka isikuhuulu.
Vaavale uhiyu, Lapanu ahonkusa Leya ni ahommwiihera Yakopi. Ni ahonthukumanana.
Vano Lapanu ahokumiha ipottha awe yeehaniya Silipa ni ahonvaha mwanawe wiira arumeke.
Nanso usa waya amoone Leya. Vano Yakopi ahomwiirela Lapanu: We ukipankile cani? Mi akivanre nteko kimphavelaka Rakeli? Nlattuni we ukithepyacaka?
Lapanu ahaakhula: Uno khinakhalaka ilemalelo upacera utheliya mwana omwankani, omuulupale hinaya utheliya.
Vano uhiye umala isumana ithenlyaa ila, ninaahala wuuvaha tho omwankani uyo, nanso uvareke tho nteko myakha saapa.
Vaavale Yakopi ahokupali. Yahovira isumana yanthenlyawe Leya ni Lapanu ahonvaha Rakeli ukhala amwaarawe.
Lapanu ahonvaha Rakeli ipottha awe yeehaninya Piila wiira arumeke.
Yakopi ahonthukumanana Rakeli. Yoole aancivenle wompwaha Leya ni ahonvarela nteko Lapanu myakha saapa.
Ukati woonnyawe Mwaneene Nluku wiira Leya anavyavyehiya, ahonvaha asaana, nanso Rakeli ari mwali eekupa.
Leya ahorupala irukulu, ni ahonnyara mwana ni ahonvaha ncina na Rupeni, kontha eera: Mwaneene Nluku hoona icuku caka. Vano, weekhweeli awannyaka anaahala ukifenta.
Leya ahorupala tho irukulu, ni unnyara wawe mwana nkina aheera: Kontha Mwaneene Nluku heewa wiira kinavyavyehiya, hokivaha tho ula, ni yahonvaha ncina na Simeyoni.
Ahorupala tho irukulu ikina ni wannyanryawe mwana, aheera: Paahi, awannyaka anaahala waatana ni mi, kontha kihaayarana asaana araru. Phimaana yahonvaha ncina na Levi.
Ahorupala tho irukulu ni unnyara wawe mwana aheera: Ula nkwaha ola kinamunnuwiha Mwaneene Nluku. Commo yahonvaha ncina na Yutta. Ni ahohiya uyara.
Vano ukati woonnyawe Rakeli wiira khannyaranne asaana Yakopi, ahopacera unrama munnaawe ni ahomwiirela Yakopi: Ukiyarane asaana, atthuna phatari kikhwe.
Yakopi ahorusiya ni Rakeli ni aheera: Kinokhala Nluku, watelihile uyara?
Vano ule ahaakhula: Haawo Piila ula, ipottha aka, unthukumananeke wiira aayare asaana toko waahalaka waayara mi, wiira nhina mwa yaayo kaakhalane asaana.
Phimaana ule ahonvaha Yakopi uthela ipottha awe yeehaninya Piila, ni ahonthukumanana.
Piila ahorupala irukulu ni ahonnyarana Yakopi mwana.
Vano Rakeli aheera: Nluku hooluma, heewa ncu naka ni hokivaha mwana. Phimaana ahonvaha ncina na Tani.
Piila, ipottha ya Rakeli, ahorupala tho irukulu ni ahonnyarana Yakopi mwana onayeeli.
Vaavale Rakeli aheera: Kaari ni ikhotto yuulupale ni munnaka ni kihotthema. Phimaana ahonvaha ncina na Nafitalii.
Ukati woonnyawe Leya wiira hohiya uyara, ahonkusa Siilipa ipottha awe ni ahonvaha uthela Yakopi.
Siilipa, ipottha ya Leya, ahoyarana Yakopi mwana mmoca.
Vano Leya aheera: Ila iparakha! Phimaana ahomwiihana Kaate.
Wahoolo, Siilipa, ipottha ya Leya ahonnyarana tho Yakopi mwana onayeeli.
Vano Leya aheera: Kihotteeliya! Athiyana ayo ankokiirela kiri ootteeliya, ni aahonvaha ncina na Aseri.
Ukati woohephiya itiriku, Rupeni ahorwaa umattani ni ahophwanya mirette cooyariha ni ahaawiihera anumwane. Vano Rakeli ahomwiirela Leya: Ukivahe mirette cooyariha ca mwanaa nnyo.
Nanso ule ahomwaakhula: Khawutosile wakaakhilyaa alopwana ayo? Umphavela ukaakha tho mirette ciwiihilyawe mwanaka nnyo? Vano Rakeli ahaakhula: Ula uhiyu ula Yakopi naahala wuthukumanana. Naakakhanihaka ni mirette ciwiihilyawe mwanaa nnyo.
Ucoocilo, ukati waturuwilyawe Yakopi umattani, Leya ahomwiikamela numwiirela: Ilelo we unaahala ukithukumanana, kontha kihowuthumani ni mirette ca mwanaka. Ni yoole uhiyu ule ahonthukumanana.
Nluku ahomwiiwa Leya. Ule ahorupala irukulu ni ahonnyarana Yakopi mwana oneethanu.
Vano Leya aheera: Nluku hokiliva wammahilyaka ipottha aka waathukumanana awannyaka. Phimaana ahonvaha ncina na Isakari.
Leya ahorupala tho irukulu ni ahonnyarana Yakopi mwana onasiita.
Leya aheera: Nluku hokitthuva itthuvo yomaana. Ula nkwaha ula awannyaka anakunkomana, kontha kihaayarana asaana siita. Phimaana ahonvaha ncina na Sepulomi.
Ukati vakani tho, ule ahonnyara mwana mwanthiyana ammahilyawe ncina na Tina.
Vano Nluku ahomuupuwela Rakeli. Nluku aheewa ukhuwela wawe ni ahompanka mayooyara.
Ule ahorupala irukulu nuunnyara mwana ni aheera: Nluku hotamiha ihaaya caka nnyo.
Ahonvaha ncina na Yusufu ni aheera: Mwaneene Nluku akivahe tho mwana nkina.
Rakeli nannyanreene Yusufu, Yakopi ahomwiirela Lapanu: Ukihiye kituruwele uwaani, ilapo aka.
Ukivahe asaaraka ayo yuvarenlyaka nteko, na asaanaka ayo, kontha mi kimphavela urwaa uwaani. We uhocuwela ciinryaka wowuuvarela nteko.
Nanso Lapanu ahomwiirela: Wakhala wiira kihophwanya iparakha wa miithoni waa kinawulepela wiira ukhale ni mi. Kihoona wiira Mwaneene Nluku hokivaha iparakha nlattu wawaa we.
Ni ahopwahera eeraka: Ukihimerye ihisapu yowuuliva; mi kinaahala wuuliva.
Yakopi ahomwaakhula: We uhocuwela cuvarenlyaka nteko, ni mihuwo caa cihoncererya nlattu wowehaweha mi.
Ni citthu vakani caarinaa kihinawa, cihoncererya venci, kontha Mwaneene Nluku hovaha iparakha ukati uwilyaka uno. Vano mi kinhala upanka yakhani itthu yowakavihera alokwaka?
Vano Lapanu ahonkoha: Untthuna kuuvaheke isiyani? Yakopi ahaakhula eeraka: Uhikivahe itthu. Kinaahokoleela uwacawaca nuuhakhela mihuwo cinyu wakhala wiira nnakupali imphavelaka.
Ilelo kinaahala uvira mmihuwoni mwinyu ni kimmothanla ikhontwaa co manepa ni co mitthottwe, ni asikhontwaa othene ooripa, ni ipuri co manepa ni co mitthottwe, cole phinhalaka ukhala mpokerero aka.
Ni isariya aka inkowuvaha uhoolo usaahiti, ukati unhalaa uwehaweha mapokerero aka. Yakhalaka mmatatani mwaka ipuri yohimanepa ni yohimitthottwe, ikhontwaa cohiripa, pooti wiira cowiinyinya.
Lapanu aheera: Nihotthukelana, weerannyee toko cihimilyaa.
Nanso, nenno nihuku nno Lapanu ahaakawaniha apeperu o mitthottwe ni o manepa ni ipuri cothene co mitthottwe ni co manepa cothene cari cotteelatteela ni asikhontwaa othene ooripa ni ahohiya mmatatani mwa asaanawe.
Vano Yakopi ahokhuma nipuro nne arwaka ncoko woweettiya mahuku mararu. Wahoolo Yakopi ahopwaherera uliha mihuwo ca Lapanu.
Vaavale Yakopi ahokusa miri cikithi co mphari, ntholo ni rokoci ni ahokhava apankaka mitthottwe.
Wakhavaawe, aheesa uhoolo waya mihuwo, mmakuwani, mawureryoni ni mapuro yarupaya ni canapepheryana ukati wawaya uwurya.
Ni campepheryana uhoolo waya miritta, cantotholiya co marephurephu, co manepa ni co mitthottwe.
Vano Yakopi anawawayaniha cikani nnyo, ni aanapanka wiira cennyo cikhale wamoca ni inama co marephurephu ni cooripa ca Lapanu. Commo antthonkomaniha mihuwo cawe woohitakanihera ca Lapanu.
Ukati warupalaya ikhontwaa coonenevaca nnye, Yakopi anaweesa uhoolo waya nwo miritta, cineemelacilene mmasepani, wiira citotholele mmirittani mmo.
Nanso kheesa miritta nnye uhoolo waya inama cokenkennya, kontha cokenkennya nnyo caakhala ca Lapanu ni cooneneva nnyo cakhala ca Yakopi.
Phimaana Yakopi ahothaciri venci mpaka ahaana mihuwo cinci, ipottha cithiyana ni cilopwana, inkamira ni apuuru.
Yakopi aheewa wiira, asaana a Lapanu yanawuulumaca yiiraka: Yakopi howyaa citthu ni mihakhu cothene carinaya apaapa ehu, phimaana athaciriki.
Yakopi ahoona wiira makhalelo a Lapanu ni uyo khayari toko khalayi.
Vano Mwaneene Nluku ahomwiirela Yakopi: Uturuwele ilapo yo mayathumwanaa ni wamucyaa. Mi kinkokhala ni we.
Vaavale Yakopi ahoruma wiihaninya Rakeli ni Leya wiira arwace utakhwani yoone mihuwo cawe.
Uwaca waya aheerelaca coo: Kinawoona makhalelo athumwaninyu ayo ni miyano khaanakhala toko khalayi. Nanso Nluku Apaapa ari ni mi.
Nyu nnaacuwela wiira kihaavarela ratta nteko athumwaninyu,
nanso ayo ankipanka mi ntirikhi, avirikanihacaka mpokerero aka imaara khumi. Nanso Nluku khaatthunihenre wiira akipanke yoonanara.
Yakiirelaka wiira inama co manepa nnyo cikhaleke cawaa, phuupokera waa; vano mihuwo cothene cakhala co manepa. Ni yakiirelaka coorephuwaca nnyo cothene cikhaleke cawaa, wonwo phuupokera waa, vano mihuwo cothene caatothola asaana oorephuwaca.
Nluku ala mananna ala phipankilyawe wowaakha mihuwo athumwaninyu akivahaka mi.
Weeracele coo: Ukati warupalaya mihuwo nnyo, mi kahoweha ni kahoona munttorani mmo anapinkula athukumananaka ikhontwaa cithiyana nnyo cari co manepa, co marephurephu ni co mitthottwe.
Vano ncelo a Nluku ahokiirela munttorani: Yakopi, mi kahomwaakhula kiiraka: Kiri va.
Ni ule ahomwiirela tho: Uwuse miitho aa ayo, ni unawoona anapinkula othene anthukumanana ikhontwaa cithiyana nnyo, ari o manepa, o marephurephu ni o mitthottwe, kontha kihoona cothene cuupankilyawe Lapanu.
Mi phi mi Nluku o Peeteli wonwe wemeesilyaa nluku uttikitthelaka makhura ni ukoopelaka natiri. Wunwe nna va, ukhume ila ilapo ela ni uturuwele ilapo ya alokwaa.
Vano Rakeli ni Leya yahonkoha Yakopi yiiraka: Wapaapa nwo uhaawo mphantte wonhakhu unnaaca?
Khannalikelela ukhala amalaponi? Maana ahonitumiha ni aholya ncurukhu uyo.
Kontha nhakhu wothene Nluku ukumihilyawe wathumwanihu uri wawihu ni wa asaanehu. Nna vaa upanke cothene cinoohimeryawe Nluku.
Vano Yakopi ahaaweliha asaarawe na asaanawe ayo mmankamirani.
Ahokusa mihuwo cawe cothene ni mihakhu caphwanyilyawe uPatan-Arami, wiira arwee ilapo yo Kanaa, uri Isaki athumwane.
Ukati Lapanu warwelyawe uthikila mapururu okhontwaa, Rakeli aheennya ananttuntta a athumwane.
Ni Yakopi ahomwiita Lapanu nramewu wohinhimerya itthu kontha anatthawa.
Ahonwa nuutthawana cothene carinawe ni aholapuwa mooloko awehaka muru mwaako wo Kiliyati.
Nihuku noneeraru Lapanu ahohimerya wiira Yakopi hotthawa.
Vano ahaakusa asunnawe ni ahontthimakela mahuku saapa eettaka ni ahomphwanya nari mwaako wo Kiliyati.
Vano Lapanu Nramewu ahophwanyinya ni Nluku, uhiyu munttorani phimwiirelaka: Wiisunke, uhuulume itthu ni Yakopi, hata ikhale itthu yooreera atthuna yoonanara.
Lapanu ahomphwanya Yakopi naakhurutunle aheema awe umyakoni co Kiliyati. Ciicammo Lapanu na asunnawe ahaakhurutula aheema awe umwaakoni.
Vano Lapanu ahonkoha Yakopi eeraka: Ukipankile cani? Yokiita iyo wakusaka asaana ayo toko ipottha coovariya ukhottoni?
Nlattuni ukitthawaka womwiitiho ni ukisempaka, wohikihimyacera itthu? Hapo mi kanawuveleliha wootteeliya ni icipo, ikoma ni ceece.
Ciicammo khukihile kavahaka alaahuma asaanaka nu ucuulu aka wiira kaaleehe. Uheetta wootirikhi.
Kahaana ikuru cooreera wuuttarusa, nanso Nluku athumwaninyu, hokuulumana ncana uhiyu eeraka: Wiisunke uhimuulumele itthu hata ikhale yooreera atthuna yoonanara.
Vano we wapheela urwaa, kontha wahoonukhela uturuwela waathumwanaa, kahiki wennyerani anluku aka ayo?
Yakopi ahomwaakhula Lapanu eeraka: Kanawoova. Kontha kooniha wiira unakaakha asaanaa ayo.
Ule nohalaa umphwanyana anluku aa ayo umwiive. Unikukhuryace mi na asunnaka ayo waphwanya itthu yawaa ukuse. Kontha Yakopi khaacuwela wiira Rakeli pheennyile anluku ayo.
Vano ahokela Lapanu nheemani mwa Yakopi, nheemani mwa Leya, nheemani mwa ipottha cithiyana piili nanso wohaphwanya anluku ayo. Ni ukhuma wawe nheemani mwa Leya, ahokela nheemani mwa Rakeli.
Nanso Rakeli ahaakusa ananttuntta ayo ni wattukhunyera munhukhoni yonkamira ni ahonkomela. Vano Lapanu ahaakukhurya nheemani mothene, ni khaaphwanyile.
Rakeli aheerela athumwane: Paapa, nhikiviruwele akinlamuliya wunwa kontha kiri ni nteko wathiyana. Lapanu ahaawehaweha ananttunntta ayo, nanso khaaphwanyile.
Vaavale Yakopi ahorusiya nunviruwela Lapanu amwiirelaka: Kitthekileni? Kukosenre isiyani yooreera we uviruwa ni ukoomolanihaca?
We uhokukhuryaca mirintti caka cothene wakhala wiira uhophwanya itthu yawaa, uwiihe va yoonaka alokwaa ayo ni alokwaka wiira anihukhumu.
Myakha sirini kihoovarela nteko. Ikhontwaa ni ipuri cinyu akinarihakaciha ni akinakhura inama yo nhuwo enyu.
Kakinowiiherani inama yoorakalaca. Nkilivihaka inama cothene cenyinya uhiyu atthuna uthana.
Uthana kaakhwa nttukuttha ni uhiyu kaakhwa uriiriya ni nkaarupa.
Kihokhala myakha sirini, kuuvarelakani nteko. Myakha khumi na micese kihovarelani nteko wiira kaathele asaanaa eeli, ni myakha siita kihovarelani nteko nkipokerihaka inama, nanso nyu nhorukunusaca mapokerero aka imaara khumi.
Ahaari Nluku a apaapa, Nluku a Aparahamu, Nluku ri ihisima ya Isaki, khweeli nyu mwankoomola wohiitthu. Nluku heewa icuku caka ni hoona nteko uvanryaka, phimaana hookuphulani uhiyu wo ncana.
Vaavale Lapanu ahomwaakhula Yakopi eeraka: Ala asithiyana ala asaanaka ni asilopwana ayo ucuulu aka, nnya mihuwo caka ni cothene cinoonaa nnyo ciri cawaka. Ilelo kinhala weeriha cani asaanaka ala ni asaana yayanryaya ayo?
Nna va nileehane wiira ukhale usaahiti we ni mi.
Vano Yakopi ahokusa nluku ni aheemesa upanka nivatta.
Ni Yakopi aheerela asunnawe: Mpanke nikuttha no maluku. Ni ale yahopankaca nikuttha no maluku ni othene yaholelyaca wanikutthani vale.
Lapanu aheehana nipuro nno Yekar-Saatuta, nanso Yakopi eehane Kaleeti.
Vano Lapanu aheera: Nna nikuttha nna nikhale saahiti ehu we ni mi. Phimaana wiihaninyaka uKaleeti
ni Misipa, kontha heera: Mwaneene Nluku nniwehawehe we ni mi ni anihukhumu hata nimwalane ntthu ni nkhwawe.
Waahuvihaka asaanaka ala, waathelaka athiyana akina mi hata kihikhale, ucuwele wiira Nluku nawoona.
Lapanu ahomwiirela tho Yakopi: Nikuttha phi nna, ni nivatta neemesilyaka iriyari yo we ni mi phi nna.
Nikuttha nna nikhale saahiti. Ciicammo nivatta nna nikhale saahiti wiira yakhala yoonanara kihitupihe nikuttha nna kiwanaka nwo, ni we yakhala yoonanara uhituphane nikuttha nna ni nivatta nna uwaka uno.
Nluku a Aparahamu, Nluku a Nahori, Nluku o mayathumwanaya anihukhumu. Ni Yakopi, mwanlattu wo ihisima ya Isaki athumwane, aholupela.
Yakopi ahopanka isataka umwaakoni, ni aheehana asilokwawe yaari wonwo wiira alye. Yaholyaca ni yarupacile umwaakoni wonwo.
Wahoolo Yakopi ahokhuma ni ahaakumanana ancelo a Nluku.
Vano woona wawe, Yakopi aheera: Ala anakhotto a Nluku! Ni ahovaha nipuro nno ncina na Manayimu.
Vaavale, Yakopi ahaaveleliha mayanhupi awe wa Isawu munnaawe, akhala uSeyiri ilapo yo Eetomu.
Ni aheerela mwanhimerye nkunyaka Isawu wiira: Mi karumeya enyu Yakopi kari wamoca ni Lapanu, kihaawo mpaka ilelo.
Kihaana imope na apuuru, ikhontwaa, ipuri, ipottha cithiyana ni cilopwana. Nkunya, kinovelelihera ula nhupi ula, wiira ukakhelele wosalaama.
Vano mayanhupi yahoturuwela wa Yakopi phimwiirelaka: Nihomphwanya munnaa Isawu ni uyo nowa wonwo, nawuphavela, ni haana alopwana iminya cese.
Vano Yakopi ahoova venci ni ahocukula. Phimaana ahaakawaniha atthu ayo miphwinko miili, ciicammo ahokawaniha ikhontwaa, ipuri, imope ni inkamira miphwinko miili,
kontha oopuwela coo: Isawu awaaka na anakhotto awe aatuphelaka mphwinko mmoca nkina uyo unkohala.
Vano Yakopi ahoswali eeraka: Nluku a paapa Aparahamu, Nluku a paapa Isaki, we Mwaneene Nluku ukireenle wiira: Uturuwele uwannyaa waalokwaa kinawupanka yooreera.
Mi kinacuwela wiira khaninkiphwanela nifento neekhweeli ninkipankaa mi karumeyaa. Kilapuwile mooloko Yortani ni nttontto aka paahi, nanso nna va kihaana miphwinko miili.
Sontte ukoopole mmatatani mwa munnaka Isawu, kontha mi kinamoova, wiira hiiwe ukiiva mi, asaana wamoca na anumwanaya.
Kontha we uheera: Kinaweettiha ratta. Kinawuvaha ucuulu mwinci toko nhava wo mpharyaa ni mphwinko wa atthu wohaalikelyaa.
Yoole uhiyu ule Yakopi ahorupa nenne nipuro nne ni ahothanla mihuwo commaha munnaawe Isawu:
ipuri cithiyana iminya piili ni anapinkula sirini, ikhontwaa cithiyana iminya piili ni anapinkula sirini okhontwaa,
inkamira talathini cithiyana co wamwinya na asaana aya, imope cithiyana arupayini ni imope khumi cilopwana, apuuru onthiyana sirini ni apuuru onlopwana khumi.
Ahaakawela mihuwo nnyo ipottha cawe wiira awacawace, ni wo khula nhuwo wari mphantte aya, ni aheerela: Nhoolelaceke ni nhiye ikhato nhuwo ni nhuwo nkhwaya.
Ahonlamulela oopacera ole: Munnaka Isawu oophwanyaka, ni ookohaka wiira: We uri naani, unrwa vayi ni nhuwo urinaa ula wawani?
Vano umwakhuleke wiira ca karumeya enyu Yakopi. Ciri itthuvo cinonveleliherawe nkunya awe Isawu ni uyo neera awaka uttuli wihu.
Ciicammo ahonlamulela onayeeli, oneeraru nale othene yawa uttuli mihuwo eeraka: Uphwanyakani Isawu othene munhimyacere nuulumo nimoca nenna.
Munhimerye tho wiira: Karumeya aa Yakopi nawa uttuli uno. Kontha Yakopi hoopuwela coo: Kahoolihaka itthuvo caka nnyo, kinattipiha urusiya wawe nwo, vano nakumanacaka ni mi uyo, atthunaka nakakhelela wooreera.
Phimaana inama cotthuvo nnye cahohoolihiya, nanso ule ahohala veekhawe nipuro nomakiya nne ni ahorupa uhiyu wothene.
Yoole uhiyu ule ahonwa ni ahaakusa asaarawe eeli, na asaarawe eeli oohitteeliheraninya, wamoca na asaanawe khumi na mmoca, ni yaholapuwaca nsepa no Yappoko.
Ahaalapusaca nsepa nno asaarawe ayo ni citthu cothene carinawe.
Vano Yakopi ahohala veekhawe ni ahomwanana nlopwana mmoca uhiyu wothene mpaka usa.
Nlopwana ule, woona wawe wiira khamoorya untthema, ahomwaatta wakumanacile makhuva oonatara, ni Yakopi ahorepenyuwa wakumanacile makhuva ni amwananaka ono.
Nlopwana ule aheera ukihiye kirwee kontha uhosa. Nanso Yakopi ahomwaakhula eeraka: Akinoohiya urwaka wahikireeriheke.
Ni ahonkoha: Ncina naa tipani? Ule ahomwaakhula: Mi kineehaninya Yakopi.
Vano nlopwana ule aheera: Ncina naa khaninhala wiihaninya tho Yakopi, nanso Israyeli, kontha we uhomwaanana Nluku na atthu ni uhotthema.
Ni Yakopi ahonkoha eeraka: Kinapheela ucuwela ncina naa. Ule aheera: Unkikoherani ncina? Vaavale ahonreeriha.
Vano Yakopi ahovaha ncina na Peniyeli nenno nipuro nno, eeraka: Kontha kihomoona Nluku ni miitho aka ala ni mi kinkumi.
Aakhumile uPeniyeli, ukati wakhumaya ncuwa ni Yakopi anattumpela.
Phimaana mpaka nihuku noleelo annasirayeli khankhuraca ntinka unluttaniha natara ni iyuunu, kontha Yakopi ahaattiya wantinkani ukumanihile natara ni iyuunu.

Yoole ukati ule, Yakopi ahoweha ni phamoonawe Isawu awaaka, nari na alopwana iminya cese. Vano ahaakawa asaanawe ayo anvahaka Leya, Rakeli na asaarawe eeli oohitteeliheraninya.
Vano ahaaholiha asaarawe eeli oohitteeliheraninya na asaanaya ayo, ahomweesa Leya na asaanawe ayo uttuli waasaarawe oohitteliheraniya Rakeli ni Yusufu phaari oomalihera.
Wahoolo Yakopi ahaapwahaca nukhala uhoolo, ni ahoromela vathi imaara saapa mpaka waphilyawe wamunnawe.
Vaavale Isawu ahontthimakela, ahonkapatta nuunvaha alaahuma nuunsalameeha, ni othene yahonlaca.
Wahoolo ahoweha ni ahoona athiyana na amirawo ni ahokoha eeraka: Ala phaasipani arinaa ala? Ule ahaakhula eeraka: Ala pha asaana anvahilyawe Nluku wotthuna wawe karumeya aa.
Vano yahophiyaca asaarawe eeli oohitteliheraniya wamoca na asaanaya ayo ni yahoroma.
Ciicammo ahophiya Leya wamoca na asaanawe, ni ahoroma. Wiimaliheroni ahophiya Yusufu ni Rakeli, na ayo yahoromaca.
Nanlelo Isawu anakoha: Unhala wiirihani mihuwo cothene ciphwanyilyaka niphiro nnyo? Yakopi ahomwaakhula: Keera kiphwanye nnema wamiithoni wankunya aka.
Nanso Isawu ahomwiirela: Mwanhimaka, mi kihaana mihuwo cinci. Cirinaa nnyo uhalaneke.
Vano Yakopi ahomwaakhula: Mena, wakhala wiira uhaana nnema ni mi ukuse itthuvo yuvahilyaka ela, phimaana koonaka ikhove aa, toko wiira koonne ikhove ya Nluku, kontha we uhokaakhelela.
Kinawulepela ukuse iparakhaka iwaneliyaa kontha Nluku wo nnema hokivaha, ni kihaana ciinci. Ni ahonkhanyereriha mpaka Isawu waakhelela.
Isawu aheera: Nrwee neette. Mi kinahoola.
Nanso Yakopi aheera: Nkunya, kinawoona asaanaka ayo ukenkenyaca ni kihaana ikhontwaa ni imope cotothola naanano kaakuvihacaka, wonihuku nimoca kinawoova ukikhwacera cothene.
Fatari uhooleke nkunya, mi kinawa uttuli nwo keettaka vakani vakani. Kintthariha malonce onama ciri uhoolo nnya ni amirawo arinaka ala. Kinawuphwanya uSeyiri.
Vano, Isawu aheera: Kinawuhiyera atthu arinaka ala. Ule ahonkoha: Nlattuni? Wanaatosa mi kaphwanyaru nnema ni nkunya aka.
Phimaana Isawu ahoturuwela iphiro yaweenlyawe ahokoleelaka uSeyiri.
Nanso Yakopi ahopwahera arwaka uSukoti. Uphiya wawe ahoteka inupa ni macici onama cawe. Phimaana wiihaninyaka nenno nipuro nno uSukoti.
Paahi Yakopi ahophiya nari nkumi iparasa yo uSikeni ni ilapo yo Kanaa, akhumaka uPatan-Arami; ni ahomaka vakhiviru nuparasa.
Ni ahothuma nthala nankhurutunlyawe heema munthalani na asaana a Hemori, athumwane Sikeni ni nsurukhu iminya imoca.
Vaavale ahoteka ikhilompi ni ahovaha ncina na Nluku, Nluku o Isirayeli.
Nkwaha mmoca, Tina, mwana a Leya ayanryawe ni Yakopi, ahokhuma wiira aacuwelane athiyana oyeele ilapo ele.
Sikeni, mwanawe Hamori, nHevewu, mwene o yoole nttetthe ule, ahomoona ni ahontuphela.
Nanso nrima awe wahonphelyaa nlattu wa Tina, mwana a Yakopi, ni ule ahoncivela mwanthiyana ole ni ahomuulumana wonifento.
Phimaana Sikeni ahorwaa waahimerya athumwane eerelaka: Nkuulumele ule nthiyana ole wiira akhale mwaaraka.
Yakopi wacuwenlyawe wiira mwamwanawe Tina ahotankanyinya iharusi, asaanawe anari utakhwani walihaaya mihuwo; ahomaala awehereryaka uturuwaca.
Vano Hamori, athumwane Sikeni yahorwaa woopa mwaha ni Yakopi.
Ukati waturuwacilyaya utakhwani asaana a Yakopi yahocuwelaca cothene ni yahocukulaca nuurusiya venci cinenne kontha Sikeni ahopanka itthu yowuulihaca muru uIsirayeli, wanrupanyawe mwana a Yakopi; itthu ihimpankiya.
Nanso Hamori aheerelaca: Mwanaka Sikeni hociveliya ni mwaninyu. Kinawuvekelani wiira munvahe akhale mwaarawe.
Ni niyaranace nyu ni hi, nnivahaka asaanenyu asithiyana ayo ni hi ninawuvahani awihu ayo,
ni nkhale wamoca ni hi. Ilapo inoonenyu ila nkhale wohitwana. Mpanke marontta enyu ni nkhalane mathala.
Vano Sikeni aheerela athumwane ni asunnawe mwanthiyana ole: Nkikupali. Nkivahe mwanthiyana oyo. Mi kinawuulivani ihisapu yothene inhalenyu ukilamula.
Mwatthuna mmwelihe ihisapu yoothela ni contthuva mwali uyo. Mi kinakumiha cothene cinhalenyu uhimya, nanso nkivahe mwali uyo kinthele.
Vaavale, asaana a Yakopi yahonthepyaca Sikeni ni athumwane yeehaninya Hamori nlattu wootankanyaa iharusi ya Tina, mwanrokoraya.
Ni yahomwiirelaca: Khaninlamuliya upanka commo, unvaha mwanrokorihu nlopwana oohuula icantto kontha iri itthu yowuuliha muru.
Phimaana ninhala wutthunani nyu mwakhalaka toko hi. Mooliheke alopwana othene toko hi.
Vano ninawuvahani asaanehu ayo wiira mwaatheleke, ni hi, asaanenyu ayo ninawathela. Ni ninhala ukhala wamoca ni amocaru ni nyu.
Nanso mwahiniweke ni mwahuuleke icantto, ninankusa mwanihu uyo nuuthama.
Yaayo moolumo ayo yahoncivela Hamori ni mwanawe Sikeni.
Sikeni khapicile nuupanka yeereliyawe iyo kontha ahoncivela venci mwana a Yakopi. Ni Sikeni phaari oofentiya venci wowapwaha atthu othene yaariwo ntthoko na athumwane.
Phimaana ahorwaa Hamori ni Sikeni wathukumaniha alopwana othene oparasa ni wahimerya eeraka:
Ale atthu ale ari osalaama ni hi, phimaana naahiye akhale ilapo ehu ila ni apanke marontta aya. Kinawoona ilapo ihu iyo iri yinci. Ananivaha waathela asaanaya ayo ni hi ninawavaha asaanehu ayo.
Nanso ayo atthu ayo anhala ukupali ukhala ni hi ni ukhala amocaru. Hi alopwana va othene nolaka icantto, toko ayo cunlyaya.
Nnoona cani, imope caya nyo, ni nhakhu aya uyo, ni mihuwo caya nyo, khacinhala ukhala cawihu? Neewanane paahi ni anaahala ukhala wamoca ni hi.
Vaavale atthu othene yavira nkhora wo oparasa, yahomwiiwelela Hamori ni mwanawe Sikeni, ni alopwana othene yaavira wa nkhora woparasa, yahoolihiya icantto.
Waphilyaya nihuku noneeraru, ukati waryaya muhuvani ni yaweryaka venci makhwatta ayo, asaana eeli a Yakopi, Simeyoni ni Levi, asirokorawe Tina, yahokusaca khula ntthu ikatana awe, yahokelaca mparasa mmwe ni yaheevakaca alopwana othene.
Ciicammo yahomwiivaca ni ikatana Hamori ni mwanawe ni yahonkusaca Tina aari inupa ya Sikeni ni yahokhumaca.
Asaanawe Yakopi yahophiyaca wa atthu ookhwa ni yahohukhaca mparasa mmo mothene kontha yanootankanyinya iharusi ya mwanrokoraya Tina.
Yahokusaca ikhontwaa, imope, apuuru caari mparasa ni cothene caari mmattani.
Yahokusaca mihakhu ni yahavarakaca asaana na athiyana urwaa wapanka ipottha, ni yahohukhaca mmapaani mothene.
Phimaana Yakopi ahomwiirela Simeyoni ni Levi: Mokivelaveliha, nhokiputaniha na atthu ankhala ilapo ela, ni makanani ni maperesewu ncuwelaka wiira hi niri vakani, anaahala ulattulana nuuhonona ntthoko ehu.
Vano ale yahaakhulaca: Mpaka uyo umpanka mwanrokorihu toko puuta?
Nluku ahonlamulela Yakopi: Wunwe, urwee uPeteli ni wakhale wonwo ni wampankele ikhilompi Nluku ookhumelenle ukati wantthawa munnaa Isawu.
Vano Yakopi ahohimerya ntthoko nawe na atthu othene yarinawe eeraka: Mwakumihe anluku a malaponi othene wariyari winyu mwiirapihe ni mmware ikuwo cikina.
Vano nunwe nirwe uPeteli wonwo kinkontekela ikhilompi Nluku akaakhunle nihuku narinaka masukuli ni hokiveleela mmaphironi mothene mweettaka.
Vaavale Yakopi ahovahiya anluku othene oohimaana yari mmatatani ni ipirinku caari mmanyaruni ni Yakopi ahothipela vathi mooko uri wamoca nuSikeni.
Vano yahokhumaca, na atthu yakhala yeeyo ilapo eyo Nluku ahaacariha woova mpaka woolwana wattharatthara asaana a Yakopi.
Commo, Yakopi na atthu othene yarinawe yahophiyaca o Lusu uneehaniya uPeteli uri ilapo yo Kanaa.
Vaavale ahoteka ikhilompi ni nenno nipuro nno ahovaha ncina no El-Peteli, kontha Nluku ahonkhumelela ukati wantthawawe munnaawe.
Ahokhwa Teepora, karumeya a Repeka, ni ahovithiya vakhiviru nuPeteli vathi waya mooko ni ahovaha ncina na Alompakuti.
Wahoolo Nluku ahonkhumelela tho Yakopi, akhumaka uPatan-Arami ni ahonreeriha.
Vano Nluku ahomwiirela: We ncina naa Yakopi. Ukhuma ilelo ncina naa khaninhala wiihaniya tho Yakopi nanso ncina naa ninhala wiihaniya Isirayeli. Ni aheehaneliya ncina na Isirayeli.
Nluku ahomwiirela tho: Mi phi mi Nluku okuru cothene. Uyarace ni ukhalane ucuulu mwinci. Mwiirutthuni mwa we, inaakhumelela ilapo cinci na atthu enci, ni ammokhumelela mamwene menci.
Mi kimmowuvaha we ilapo invahilyaka Aparahamu ni Isaki. Wahoolo ilapo eyo kinavaha ucuulu aa.
Vaavale, wuulumaca wawe Yakopi, Nluku ahowela.
Vano aheesa nivatta no nluku nipuro noolumaninyawe ni Nluku, ni aheetthela yoowuriya ni makhura waculu waya nivatta.
Phimaana Yakopi ahovaha ncina no Peteli nipuro namuulumanyawe Nluku.
Wakhumilyaya uPeteli, unahanle ncoko vakani wiira aphiye ilapo yo Efarata, Rakeli ahonnyara mwana, nanso uyara wawe waari wookukuryaca.
Nari mmekho, mayoyariha ahomwiirela: Uhoove, kontha uhaana tho mwana mwanlopwana.
Vano wakhumaya nnepa awe, kontha hokhwa, ahonvaha mwana ule ncina na Penoni, nanso athumwane yahonvaha ncina na Pencamii.
Ni ala mananna ala pheeracilyawe wookhwa Rakeli ni ahovithiya ni iphiro yorwaa o Farata uneehaniya uPetelehemu.
Waculu waya mahiye, Yakopi aheemesa nivatta no nluku. Mpaka nihuku noleelo, nenne nivatta nne ninathonyera mahiye a Rakeli.
Vano Isirayeli ahokhuma arwaka unkhurutula heema awe withela Miktal-Eteri.
Anowiira Isirayeli athamelaka yeeyo ilapo eyo, Rupeni ahorwaa unthukumanana Piila, amwaara athumwane oohitteeliheraninya, ni Isirayeli ahocuwela. Yakopi ahaana asaana khumi nuuwa eeli:
Rupeni, ntthara na Yakopi, Simeyoni, Levi, Yutta, Isakari ni Sepuloni, ala yari asaana a Leya;
Yusufu ni Pencamii asaana a Rakeli;
Taani ni Nafitali asaana a Piila, ipottha ya Rakeli;
Kaate ni Aseri yaari asaana a Silipa ipottha ya Leya. Ala phaasaana yayarelyawe o Patan-Arami.
Yakopi ahorwaa unthotola Isaki, athumwane, o Manree yo Kiriyate-Arapa o Heporoni wakhalawe Aparahamu ni Isaki.
Mahuku ookumi a Isaki yari myakha iminya imoca ni myakha nuwa thamanini (180) ceyarelo.
Isaki ahomumula nuukhwa nooluvanle ni ahaatthara mayathumwane. Isawu ni Yakopi, asaanawe, yahonvitha.
Ula phu ucuulu wa Isawu, neehaniya Etomi.
Isawu ahaathela athiyana iriyari ya asaana uKanaa: Ata mwana a Eloni, nHitita; Oholipama mwana a Anaa, mwana a Sipeyone nHivita;
ni Pasimati mwana a Sumayili, mwanrokorawe Nepayote.
Isawu ahonnyarana Ata, Elifasi, ni Pasimati ahonnyarana Reweli.
Oholipama ahonnyara Yewusi, Yalawu ni Korani. Ala pha asaana a Isawu yayarenlawe ilapo yo Kanaa.
Vaavale Isawu ahaakusa asaarawe othene, asaanawe asilopwana na asithiyana na atthu othene ovatthokoni wawe; ni ahokusa mihuwo cawe, imope, mihakhu cawe ni citthu cothene caphwanyilyawe ilapo yo Kanaa, ni amwalanaka ni nhimaawe Yakopi ahothamela ilapo ikina.
Kontha mihakhu caya nnyo cari cinci, ni khacareerana ukhalakhala nipuro nimoca, ni ilapo yakhalakhalaya eyo khayarina coolya cootosa mwanlattu wonama carinaya nnyo.
Phimaana Isawu, neehaniya Etomi, ahorwaa ukhala mwako wo Seyiri.
Ula phu ucuulu wa Isawu athumwanaya annaEtomi, yakhalaca mwako wo Seyiri.
Ala phi macina asaanawe Isawu: Elifasi mwana a Ata, mwaarawe Isawu; Ruweli mwanawe Pisamate, mwaarawe Isawu.
Asaana a Elifasi: Teemani, Umari, Seefu, Kaayita ni Keenasi.
Timina ari mwaarawe oohitteeliheraninya a Elifasi, mwana a Isawu, ni ahonnyarana Elifasi Maalike; ala pha asaanawe Ata amwaara a Isawu.
Ala pha asaana a Ruweli: Naate, Seraa, Samaa ni Miisa; ala yari asaana a Pasimati, amwaarawe Isawu.
Ala pha asaana a Oholipama, mwanawe Anaa, mwanawe Sipeyone, athiyana oneeraru a Isawu; ni ahayarana Isawu: Yewusi, Yalawu ni Koraa.
Vano ala phi mamwene asaana a Isawu, asaana a Elifasi, ntthara na Isawu: Mwene Temaani, mwene Umari, mwene Seefu, mwene Keenasi,
mwene Koraa, mwene Kayeta, mwene Maliki; ala phi mamwene yayanryawe Elifasi ilapo yo Etomi; asaana a Ata athiyana oolupale a Isawu.
Ala pha asaana a Ruweli mwana a Isawu: Mwene Naate, mwene Seraa, mwene Samaa, mwene Misaa; ala phi mamwene yayanryawe Ruweli ilapo yo Etomi, asaana a Pasimati mwaara a Isawu.
Ala pha asaana a Oholipama mwaara a Isawu: Mwene Yewusi, mwene Yalamu, mwene Koraa; ala phi mamwene akhumakhumile ni Oholipama, mwana a Anaa, mwaara a Isawu.
Ala pha asaana a Isawu ni mamwene aya; ule neehaniya Etomi.
Ala pha asaana a Seyiri nHorewu, yakhalakhala ilapo eyo: Lotanimu, Sopalimu, Sipeyonemu ni Anaamu,
Tiisomimu, Eserimu ni Tisaamu. Ala phi mamwene o mahorewu, asaana a Seyiiri ilapo yo Etomi.
Ala pha asaana a Lotani: Hoti ni Homa. Mwanrokorawe Lotani eehaninya Timina.
Ala pha asaana a Soopali: Alvani, Manaate, Epali, Seefo ni Oona.
Ala pha asaana a Sipeyone: Ayaa ni Anaa; naaciya Anaa oonenenle iluusi co maasi oohiwelela ntakhwani, waahakhelawe apuuru a Sipeyone, athumwane.
Ala pha asaana a Anaa: Tisomi ni Oholipama, mwana mwanthiyana a Anaa.
Ala pha asaana a Tisomi: Hentta, Eesipa, Itera ni Kerani.
Ala pha asaana a Eseri: Piila, Saava ni Akaa.
Ala pha asaana a Tisomi: Usii ni Araa.
Ala phi mamwene o mahorewu: mwene Lotamu, mwene Soopelamu, mwene Sipeyamu, mwene Anamu,
mwene Tisomu, mwene Eserimu, mwene Tisomu; ala phi mamwene o mahorewu, toko caaryaya mamwene aya ilapo yo Seyiri.
Ala phi mamwene yathawaanle ilapo yo Etomi hinapaca ukhala mwene mwasaana o wIsirayeli.
O Etomi aholamula Peelamu, mwana a Peyori, ni ncina noparasa awe naari Tinapa.
Ahokhwa Peela, ni nipuru nawe, ahothawala Yopapimu, mwana a Seraa, o Posira.
Ahokhwa Yopapi, ni nipuru nawe, aholamulula Husamu, olapo yo Matanamita.
Ahokhwa Husamu, ni nipuro nawe, aholamula Hatatemu, mwana a Peetati, aarakalihile a Miitiya ncoko wo Mwape; ncina noparasa awe nari Avite.
Ahokhwa Hatatemu, ni nipuro nawe, aholamula Samulamu, o Masireka.
Ahokhwa Samulamu, ni nipuro nawe, aholamula Sawulumu, o Reyopoti, wamoca ni mooloko Ufarati.
Ahokhwa Sawulumu, ni nipuro nawe, aholamula Paali-Hanamu, mwana a Akipori.
Ahokhwa Paali-Hanamu, mwana a Akipori, ni nipuro nawe, aholamula Hatarimu; ncina noparasa awe nari Pawu; ni na amwaarawe nari Meetapeli, mwana a Materete, mwana Min-saape.
Ala phi macina o mamwene a Isawu, toko caryaya malokwawe, mapuro aya ni macina aya: Mwene Timinamu, mwene Aluvamu, mwene Yetetemu,
mwene Oholipamu, mwene Elaamu, mwene Pinomu,
mwene Kinasimu, mwene Temamu, mwene Mipisarimu,
mwene Makitiyelimu ni mwene Iramu. Ala phi mamwene o Etomi, toko caakhaliyaya ilapo aya. Ula phi Isawu, athumwane o annaEtomi.
Yakopi ahokhala ilapo yo Kanaa wonwo athumwane warwelyaya weettakaca.
Ila phi yookhumelela ya nloko na Yakopi. Yusufu warinawe myakha khumi na saapa aahakhela inama na asunnawe. Anawaakavihera asaana a Pila na asaana a Silpa asaara athumwane ni anawaahimerya athumwane coonanara caapankaya asunnawe.
Vano, Israel aananfenta venci Yusufu woopwaha asaana akina ayo kontha ayareele athumwane anooluvanle, phimaana yahonttotthihera ihancu yoorekama.
Ni wacuwenlyaya asunnawe wiira phinfentiya venci na athumwane woopwaha mwana phi mwana, yahonramaca ni khayamulumana wo nnema.
Vano aaholoha Yusufu nttora ni wahimenryawe asunnawe ale yahanca onrama wootepa.
Ni aheerela: Nviriyane nttora olohilyaka:
Natthukaca ihayi co tiriku omattani. Vano ihayi aka yahonwa ni weemela ni ihayi cinyu nnyo cahorukurerya ni wooromela ihayi aka.
Ni asunnawe yahomwiirelaca: Vano, weva onoona wiira unaahala unilamula? Ni yahonrama tho woopwaha nlattu wo nttora ni itthu yahimilyawe.
Wahoolo aaholoha tho nttora ni wahimerya asunnawe eeraka: Kiholoha tho nttora nkina. Ila ikwaha ila ncuwa, mweri ni itthoottwa khumi ni imoca cahokikhoromela.
Wahimenryawe athumwane na asunnawe, athumwane ayo yahoncaceraca yiiraka: Nttorani yooyo olohilyaa uyo? Maanaya wiira mi, anumwana na asunnaa ninwoworomela weva mpaka vathi?
Phimaana asunnawe othene Yanaanramaca. Nanso athumwane yeera yuupuwelaka itthu iyo.
Asunnawe Yusufu yahorwaa uhakhela inama ca athumwanaya vakhiviru nuuSikeni,
ni Isirayeli ahomwiirela Yusufu: Toko cincuwelaa asunnaa anhakela inama vakhiviru ni nuuSikeni. Kimphela wuruma urwee wonwo. Yusufu ahaakhula eeraka: Aye. Kiheewa.
Athumwane yahomwiirela: Urwee wonwo woone unari ukhaliyaka ratta, ukhuma asunnaa ni inama ciyo ni ukiwiihere ihapari. Yakopi anrumile nari nikuwa no Heporoni, ni Yusufu ahophiya uSikeni.
Vano nlopwana mmoca ahomphwanya akomankomacaka muthakoni ni ahonkoha eeraka: We, unaavyani?
Yusufu ahaakhula: Kinaavya asunnaka. Nkihimerye nipuro ninhakhelaya inama nnyo.
Nlopwana ule ahaakhula: Ayo ahokhumaca va. Mi kiheewa yiiracaka nrwee uTotaani. Vano Yusufu ahaatthara asunnawe. Ni ahaaphwanya anari vakhiviru ni uTotaani.
Nanso ale yahomoonaca nttayi nttayi, ni hinaphiya Yusufu, yahovanela umwiiva.
Ni yahohimeryana yiiraka: Hophiya nanttora uyo.
Vano nrwee nimwiive nunrihela nluusi, ni neereke hokhuriya ni nsene noone vano cinhalaya wiira ittora cawe nnyo.
Vano, wiiwa wawe Rupeni ahomananiha umwaakiha eeraka: Nihimwiive!
Ni aheera tho: Nhivuvihe iphome. Munrihele nluusi iri muthakoni mu, yooyo uyo nhinvaravare. Rupeni olumacenre coommo aavyaka mananna omwaakiha ni wiira anturusele wathumwane.
Uphiya wawe Yusufu, asunnawe yahonrulaca ihancu awe, yoorekama eyo,
nunvaraca nunrihela nluusi moohimasi.
Wookomacilyaya wiira alye yahoona nttayi nttayi mphwinko wa Annasumayili wakhuma uKiliyati. Ikamelo caya capakhinre ikaruma coonukhela, makhura o nrette ni makhura oonukhela caarwanaya Wiciipitu.
Yutta aheerela asunnawe: Ninhala uphwanyani namwiivaka nhimeehu uyo, nimaalanaka ukhwa wawe nwo.
Nrwee naathumihere Annasumayili. Nihinhasare ula nhimeehu iphula ni niitho. Ni asunnawe Yutta yahokupali.
Wattamenryaya anamarontta Annasumayili o Mitiyani, asunnawe Yusufu yahonkumiha Yusufu nluusi ni yahathumihera Annasumayili ni ncurukhu siriini nunkusa Wiciipitu.
Rupeni warwelyawe unweha nluusi mmo, khaamphwanyile. Woona wawe wiira Yusufu khaawo ahaahula coowara cawe,
aturuwelaka waasunnawe ni aheera: Mmirawo uyo mmwe khaawo! Kinhala wiira cani?
Vano yahomwiivaca napinkula nuruwyaa mphomeni ihancu ya Yusufu.
Ni yahorwaca waathonyera athumwanaya yiiracaka: Nihottotta ihancu ila kahiki khinakhala ihancu ya mwaninyu Yusufu?
Ni Yakopi ahoona wiira phi yeeyo ni aheera: Ila ihancu ila ya mwanaka! Nsene nihonhasara. Yusufu hokhuriya!
Vano Yakopi ahaahula coowara cawe nuwara icakho ni ahomunlela mwanawe mahuku menci.
Asaanawe othene, asilopwana na asithiyana yanawa ummaaliha, nanso aanakhotta umaalihiya nwo eeraka: Mena! Kinaahala wunla mpaka mmahiye nryawe mwanaka. Ni ahopwaherera umunlela.
Yooyo ukati uyo uWiciipitu, Annamitiyani yahontumiha Yusufu waPutifari, nhooleli a mayoorontta inupa ya Farawoo, mwene o Wiciipitu.
Yooyo ukati uyo, Yutta ahaahiya asunnawe ni ahorwaa ukhala inupa ya nlopwana mmoca eehaninya Hiira, ilapo yo Atulami.
Vano Yutta ahomoona mwanthiyana mmoca nKanaa eehaninya Suuwa. Ule ahonkusa nuunthela.
Ni mwanthiyana ole ahorupala ni onyara mwana nuummaha ncina na Eeri.
Ahorupala tho irukulu, ahonnyara mwana nlopwana nuunvaha ncina na Onani.
Ahaakulela tho nuunyara mwana ni ahonvaha ncina na Seela. Yooyo annyanre nari uKisipi.
Vano Yutta ahomwaverya Eeri, mwanawe oontthaara, nthiyana eehaninya Tamari wiira anthele.
Nanso Eeri, mwana oontthaara a Yutta, aari oohiloka wamiithoni wa Mwaneene Nluku, phimaana Mwaneene Nluku ahomwiiva.
Vano Yutta ahomwiirela Onani: Ukhale nkelanupa a munnaa, wiira munnaa akhalane ipyo.
Nanso Onani wacuwenlyawe wiira asaana ayo khanhala ukhala awawe, ukati wathukumananawe amwaara a munnaawe, aarihakacela vathi wiira hinyarele asaana munnaawe.
Ni yaapankawe ile yaari yoonanara wamiithoni wa Apwiya, phimaana nuuyo yahomwiiva.
Vano Yutta ahomwiirela Tamari: Weenaneleke unankhwelyaa uyo wapuwani wa athumwana mpaka wanhalawe wunnuwa mwanaka Seela. Kinawuvaha wiira unthele, kontha Yutta oolumacenre commo aaceraka wiira Seela ni uyo hikhwe toko cikhwilyaya asunnawe. Phimaana Tamari ahorwaa waathumwane.
Anavinrene mahuku menci, yahokhwa amwaara a Yutta, yaari mwana a Suuwa. Wahoolo Yutta aheepisiha nrima ni ahorwaa ni mpwanawe Hiira, Nnatulami, waweha ahakheli awe okhontwaa oTimina.
Vano ahohimerya Tamari wiira atiithyaa anrwaa oTimina uthikila mapururu okhontwaa.
Tamari ahorula ikuwo coonankhwele ni aheettiyelela wiitho nwo ni nleso wiira hicuweliye, ni ahonkoma wankhora wo Nayimi, uri iphiro yo Timina, kontha ahoona wiira Seela honnuwa ni khanvahiya tho wiira akhale awannyawe.
Vaavale Yutta umoona wawe Tamari amoonihile toko puuta, kontha anookhuneela ikhove awe iyo.
Yutta ahorwaa waryawe Tamari nuumwiirela: Nkawe, kinawuvekela kuuthukumanane. Kontha khacuwela wiira amwaara-mwanaka. Ni ule ahonkoha: Unhala ukivahani wowiira ukithukumanane?
Ule ahaakhula eeraka: Kinawuveleelihera ipuri yo muncicini mwaka. Ni Tamari aheera: Mwemesere itthu mpaka wanhalenyu uwiiha.
Vano ule ahonkoha eeraka: Kemesereke isiyani? Ule ahomwaakhula: Ikanyero eyo, ni nleso naa nno ni nttontto uri mmatatani mwa uyo. Yutta ahonvaha calepenlyawe, nuunrupana mpaka unrupaliha.
Wahoolo Tamari ahonwa nuurula nleso nawanryawe, ni ahowara ikuwo coonankhwele cawe.
Yutta ahonvaherera mpwanawe Nnatulami wiira oopole citthu cemesenryawe mmatatani mwa nthiyana ole, nanso khaamphwanyile.
Hiira ahaakoha alopwana o yoole nttetthe ole eeraka: Ri vayi namararuwa nonkomesa vakhiviru waya iluusi piili ciri ni iphiro yo Nayimi? Ayo yahomwaakhulaca: Mu mmwani mu khanirina namararuwa.
Vano uyo ahohokoleela wa Yutta ni ahomwiirela: Akimphwanyile. Uhiya commo, atthu o yoole nttetthe ule yiinre nwo khaawo nthiyana namararuwa.
Yutta aheera: Mweeco, ahalaneke cennyo cinhiyenryaka nyo. Akintthuna wiira nitarawyaace. Maana mi kahoovaherera ila ipuri ila wiira wanvahe, nanso we khumphwanyile.
Cinavinre myeeri miraru, Yutta ahohimerya wiira: Tamari aheetta uluva ni horupala irukulu. Vano Yutta aheera: Akumiheriye vate ni apahiye.
Ukati wakumiheriya awe vate wiira apahiye, Tamari aholeehera nhupi wa amaathi awe eeraka: Kirupalihile phi mwaneene nnya citthu nnya. Ni ahopwaherera eeraka: Nkoonani nnya, ni mmwaavye mwaneene ila ikanyero ila, nna nleso nna ni ula nttontto ola.
Vano Yutta ahocuwela citthu nnyo ni aheera: Amwaara-mwanaka ayo ahaana isariya yookivikana mi kontha kinoohavaha mwanaka Seela. Ni khaathukumananne tho.
Vano waphiilyaya ukati wooyara, wahoonnyaa wiira haana mavatta mmirimani mmo.
Wayaraawe va, mmoca uyo ahokumihera ntata nawe vate ni nthiyana mayooyariha ahonvara moono uyo nuuntthuka nluuci nookhwiila, eeraka: Ula phi oopacera.
Ukati waturusa awe mwana ule ntata nawe nno, nhimaawe ule phaphovawe nuupacera uyaryaa, ni nthiyana mayoyariha aheera: Uphwanyile cani ikhato yoovira? Ni ahovahiya ncina na Peresi manaaya wiira ikhato.
Wahoolo ahoyarya munnaawe, natthukiye mmoononi nluuci nookhwiila, ni ahovahiya ncina na Seera.
Yusufu ahorwaaninya Wiciipitu. Wonwo Putifari wanthumilyawe Yusufu mmatatani mwAnnasumayili. Putifari ari nhooleli a mayoorontta inupa ya Farawoomu, mwene o Wiciipitu, ahonthuma mmatatani mwAnnasumayili yammwiihile.
Mwaneene Nluku ari ni Yusufu, ni uyo anareeriya venci, nuupwaherera ni aakhala wapuwani wa nkunya awe munnaciipitu.
Putifari ucuwela wawe wiira Mwaneene Nluku ari ni Yusufu ni yaammunnuwiha nuureeriha miteko cothene cavarawe,
ni ahoncivela Yusufu mpaka onvaha ukhala nlamuli o wapuwani wawe wothene. Putifari ahonhiyera Yusufu ulamula wapuwani wawe wothene ni citthu cothene caarinawe.
Ukhuma ukati wanhiyenryawe ulamula wapuwani wothene ni citthu cothene, Mwaneene Nluku ahovaha iparakha inupa ya munnaciipitu, mwanlattu wa Yusufu. Iparakha ca Mwaneene Nluku cahomwareela mwa citthu cothene carinawe Putifari, ukhuma wapuwani mpaka umattani.
Vano, ahohiya citthu cothene carinawe, mmatatani mwa Yusufu, ni khaarina isukuli weetthu phi itthu, aawehererya ulya paahi. Yusufu aari ooreera ni aancivela na atthu.
Wakhanlyawe ukati vakani, amwaara a nkunya awe yahanca unthokoca numwiihana yiiraka: Uwe wakirupane!
Nanso ule ahokhotta ni aheera: Nkunya aka khanasukuli weetthu phi itthu ciri wapuwani ni cothene cirinawe hiile mmatatani mwaka.
Khaawo wapuwani va ookipwaha mi, ni khiiwo ikateelihilyawe, nanso nyu paahi, kontha amwaarawe. Kaahala upankelani itthu yoonanara toko ila, nuunkosera Nluku?
Toko coo, ale yaanankhanyereriha Yusufu khula nihuku, nanso uyo anawakhotta ni khaatthuna waattamanana.
Nihuku nimoca ahokela mpani wiira avare miteko cawe ni yooyo ukati uyo, khaariwo ntthu hata mmoca.
Vano ale yahovara ikuwo awe ni yahomwiirela tho: Nrwee, ukirupane! Nanso uyo ahokhuma mpani mmo ni waahiyera ikuwo eyo mmatatani mwaya.
Waatthawawe va, yahoona wiira hohiya ikuwo awe mmatatani mwaya,
ni yaheehana akarumeya ni weerelaca: Nkoonani! Ula Nheperewu ula niwiiheriyehu ula uwa uniruwana! Ule hokela mu ni aphavela ukirupana, nanso mi kihokhuwela.
Wakiwiilyawe kikhuwaka, hokihiyera ikuwo awe nuukhuma mpani mmo.
Vano ale yahosunka ikuwo eyo mpaka wawilyawe nkunya uwaani.
Vano yahaakulela uttonka itthu yakhumile yiiraka: Ile ipottha yo uHeperewu ile iniwiihenryaa eyo, yahokiwela mi ukiruwana.
Nanso wakhuwenlyaka wiira kaakuveliye, uyo hokihiyera ikuwo eyo nutthawa.
Wewilyawe nkunya awe itthu yattonkaya amwaarawe yiiraka: Coo phikipankilyaya ipottha iyo. Ahorusiya.
Ahoruma wiira arweeliye Yusufu ni ahovonyeriya nkalaposo mwatthukeliyaya anantthukiya a amwene. Yusufu ahokhala nkalaposo,
nanso Mwaneene Nluku ari nuule, yahomweettiha nnema, mpaka wiiwanana ni nhooleli onkalaposo.
Phimaana nhooleli onkalaposo ahomvaha Yusufu iyuulupale ya anantthukiya, ni yooyo phakhulela citthu cothene cakhumelela nkalaposo mmo.
Nhooleli khaarina masukuli ni Yusufu, kontha Mwaneene Nluku ari ni Yusufu ni yahonvaha iparakha wo miteko cothene cavarawe.
Unavinre ukati vakani, hutumu ni mayamikatthe o wamwene o Wiciipitu, yahonkosera nkunya aya, mwene o Wiciipitu.
Farawoo ahorusiya na ahooleli awe ale, nhooleli o mahutumu ni nhooleli o mayamikatthe,
ni aholamula utthukelaciya uwannyawe nhooleli o mayoorontta, nkalaposo mwaryawe Yusufu.
Nhooleli o mayorontta ahiile anantthukiya mmatatani mwa Yusufu ni eera aawehawehaka, ni yahokhala ukati vakani nkalaposo.
Vano yaholohaca hutumu ni mayamikatthe a mwene o Wiciipitu, yatthukeliye nkalaposo. Khula ntthu aholoha nttora nawe, oyeeli uhiyu mmoca yooyo ni khula nttora wahaana mataphuleleliyo aya.
Yusufu warwawe waweha wicisu, ahoona wiira yanacukulaca.
Phimaana ahaakoha akhuulupale a Farawoo, ni ale yaatthukiye wawaanyawe nkunya aya, eeraka: Nlattuni nyu ilelo nkhalaka oohitta?
Ale yahaakhulaca yiiraka: Nihaana nttora ehu ni khaawo oonitaphulela. Yusufu aheerelaca: Utaphulela nwo khunakhala wa Nluku? Nkihimerye mittora nnyo.
Vano hutumu ahonttonkela Yusufu nttora awe uyo: Munttorani mwaka kihoona mwiri unari vakhiviru ni mi,
ni mwiri uyo wahaana miritta miraru. Ni uyo wahophuwa, mpaka ukhalana ithutu ni wiima ni uttokottha mavareene.
Ikoomisi ya Farawoo yaari mmatatani mwaka. Kahokusa cowiima nnye ni waamela nkoomisini mwa Farawoo nuumvaha mmatatani mwawe.
Yusufu ahomwiirela: Mataphuleleliyo aya pha ala: Miritta miraru nnyo phi mahuku mararu.
Nhina wo mahuku mararu, Farawoo nowoowusa muru aa, ni nowowuutaphula ni wuuhokolosera nteko aa ni we ummomvaha ikoomisi mmatatani mwawe toko caalemalenlyaa umpanka waarya hutumu awe.
Ukiviriyane cothene caweettelaka ratta ukuupuweleleke mi, wakihimye wooreera wa Farawoo nwo, wiira kikhume nkalaposo mu.
Maana kiwiihiye utthuna nuuhitthuna, ukhuma ilapo yo maheperewu, ni ciicammo, uno khiiwo ipankilyaka yooreerela utthukeliya nkalapooso mu.
Weewilyawe muulupale omayamikatthe mataphuleleliyo omaana ale, ahomwiirela Yusufu: Ni mi ciicammo kihaana nttora aka: Wamuru waka cahaawo itthuttu tthaaru co mikatthe cootteela.
Itthuttu yooculu iyo cahaawo mikatthe co khula nnanna ni cooviyola cikina caancivela Farawoo, nanso asaanuni yaanaawa ulya ntthuttuni yarinaaka wamuru iyo.
Ni Yusufu aheera: Ala phi mataphuleleliyo aya: Itthuttu tthaaru nnyo, phi mahuku mararu.
Nhina wo mahuku mararu, Farawoo nowowutthukacera ni wuuthomya mmwirini, ni asaanuni ammoolya irutthu aa.
Waphilyaya nihuku noneeraru, naari nihuku napiiherawe Farawoo myakha ceyarelo ni ahaalattula mayoonlaka othene ni waavaha yoolya. Wamiithoni waya atthu ale ahaawusaca myuru nhooleli o mahutumu ni nhooleli o mayamikatthe.
Ahonhokolosera nteko awe hutumu, mpaka wakhanlyawe tho yoole mayonvaha ikoomisi Farawoo.
Nanso, ahoruma wiiviya wootthukaceriya nhooleli o mayamikatthe toko Yusufu caahimenryawe muutaphulelani nttora.
Paahi, nhooleli o mahutumu ule khamuupuwenle tho Yusufu, mpaka ahonliyala.
Wumaleloni wo myakha miili, Farawoo ahaana nttora awe. Ule anoweemela nceresere mooloko Niilu.
Vano cahokhumaca mmoolokoni mmo imope saapa cooreera ni cooneneva, caalya nceresere mooloko.
Wahoolo cahokhuma mmoolokoni mmo imope tho saapa, coonanaraca ni cowoottaca, carweele utakaneela ni cikhunanaya nnye nceresere mooloko.
Vano imope coonanaraca nnyo ni cowoottaca nnyo cahokhura imope cooreeraca nnyo ni cooneneva nnyo. Vano Farawoo ahonwa.
Ahohokoleela tho urupa ni aholoha tho nttora nikina. Miphapa saapa, cuulupale ni comaana, coocara ni cooreera, cahothapuruwa ntathi mmoca.
Vano cahophuwela tho miphapa cikina saapa, cooyeevaca ni coowuuma mu ncasini mmo, caapahiye ni iphyoo yaakhuma wuuthakoni.
Miphapa cooyeevaca nnyo cahomirya miphapa saapa coocara ni comaana nnyo. Vano Farawoo ahonwa, ni ahoona wiira aari nttora.
Wicisuru, cinancanre cowuupuwela coonkukuryeeha, ahoruma wiihanaciya mayaahako ni mayoocuwelaca o Wiciipitu ni ahaattonkela mittora nnyo, nanso khaawo oonrye utaphulela.
Vano nhooleli o mahutumu ahomwiirela Farawoo: Ilelo phinoopuwelaka caaliyanlyaka.
Ikwaha imoca Farawoo wahorusiya na arumeyi aa eeli ni waholamula otthukiya mi ni nhooleli omayamikatthe owannyawe nhooleli omayoorontta.
Uhiyu mmoca, khula ntthu wa hi, aholoha nttora ni khula nttora wahaana mataphuleleliyo aya.
Wahoreera! Ahaawo ni hi mommo mmirawo mmoca Nheperewu, karumeya a nhooleli omayoorontta. Nahonttonkela cennye mittora cihu nnye ni ule ahotaphulela, anihimeryaka wo khula ntthu manaaya nttora awe.
Ni cothene cahokhumelela toko canihimenryawe. Mi kihoturuseliya nteko aka ni nkina uyo heeviya wootthukeleliya.
Farawoo ahoruma wiihaninya Yusufu eeraka: Awiihiye wowakuvyaa akhumihiyaka ukalapooso. Nametthileene irori nuuwara ikuwo cikina aheethoonyera wa Farawoo.
Farawoo ahomwiirela Yusufu: Kahaana nttora nimoca ni khaawo noorya utaphulela. Nanso kiheewa wiira we, weewaka nttora unawoorya utaphulela.
Yusufu ahomwaakhula: Iyo khinkhuma ni mi, nanso Nluku nawuvahani nyu ntaphulelo no nnema.
Vano Farawoo ahonttonkela nttora ule Yusufu: Kiholoha kineemenle nceresere mooloko Niilu.
Cahokhuma mmoolokoni mmo imope saapa cooreera ni cooneneva, caalya ni mooloko uyo.
Wahoolo cahokhuma cikina tho saapa coonanara ni cowootta. Akinoona imope coonanara mwiilaponi mothene.
Imope coonanara ni cowootta nnyo cahokhura imope saapa cooneneva nnyo cakhumelenle woopacera nnyo.
Hata cinakhuunreene, khacacuwannyaa wiira ciholya canvira cikhalaka yooyo nkhalelo uyo. Vano kahonwa.
Wahoolo kaholoha tho nttora nkina. Kahoona miphapa saapa, coocara ni cooreera, cathapuruwa ntathi mmoca.
Vano cahophuwela tho saapa coonyaala ni cooyevaca, cowumihinya ni iphyoo yooviha yakhuma muuthakoni.
Miphapa cooyevaca nnyo cahomirya miphapa saapa comaana nnyo. Kihaattonkela iyo acuweli, nanso khaawo oonrye utaphulela.
Farawoo, mwarina nttora mmoca, eera phi Yusufu. Nluku hoohimeryani Farawoo, itthu imphavelawe upanka.
Imope saapa cooreera nnyo, ciri myakha saapa ni miphapa saapa comaana nnyo, ciicammo ciri myakha saapa, va uri nttora mmocaru.
Imope saapa cowootta ni coonanara nnyo cakhumelenle uttuli waya cikina nnyo, ni miphapa saapa cohicara ni coomihiye ni iphyoo yooviha yakhuma muthakoni, ciri myakha saapa. Cinhala ukhala myakha saapa cotala.
Phi ciicammo toko cuuhimenryaka Farawoo, Nluku hoothoonyera itthu inhalawe upanka.
Myaakha saapa cooruweriya cihanle vakani uwa ilapo yo Wiciipitu.
Wahoolo cimmowa myakha saapa cotala. Vano ukati wothene wooruweriya ummooliyaliya, kontha itala eyo immohasara ilapo yothene.
Itala inhala uwa immokhala yootepa, woovikana ukati waruweriye khunhala wuupuweleliya tho mwiilaponi.
Nttora uhowela imaara piili Farawoo, kontha itthu ila iholakeliya ni Nluku ni immwa yakuvyaka.
We Farawoo umphavele nlopwana oocuwelaca ni unhele ulamulela ilapo yo Wiciipitu.
Farawoo waahele atthu oowehaweha, anhala utotokaniha mphantte woneethanu wo coolya co Wiciipitu nhina wo myakha saapa cooruweriya nnyo.
Ayo anlamuliya utotokaniha yoolya yootosa inhalaya wooryaniha ukati wooruweriya uyo, nuusunka itiriku, ni we Farawoo unlamuliya uwehawehaka ni usunkiha mmakhupini ummasittatti.
Yeeyo yoolya iyo inhala usunkiya eyo, phinhala ulaminya myakha cotala cinhala uwa mWiciipitu mu, wiira ilapo ihihasaryee ni itala.
Ala moopuwelo ala yahoncivela Farawoo na anamiruku awe othene.
Phimaana Farawoo ahaakoha: Nanso ninaahala umphwanya ntthu toko ula ookhalana Nnepa wa Nluku?
Farawoo ahomwiirela Yusufu: Toko ciinryawe wowuthonyera Nluku citthu nnya cothene, khaawo ntthu annkhili nuucuwelaca toko we.
We thi we unhala ulamulela inupa aka, ni uneethi aka wothene unhala wiiwelela nlamulo naa, nanso wahiceni, thi mi muulupale wowuupwaha we.
Ni Farawoo ahopwaherera: Kinawuuvaha nenna vaa ulamulela ilapo yo Wiciipitu yothene.
Wahoolo, Farawoo ahonrula nnikokhoni nneela antthittelawe nuummwariha Yusufu nnikokhoni mwawe. Aholamula uwarihiya ihaancu yoovevyaala, ni ahommwariha nkuhu wowooru nsiko.
Ni ahommweliha ikaaro awe yonayeeli yo omwene ni uhoolo wawe yahaawo anamakhuwela yeera: Nhule iphiro. Yusufu heesiya ulamulela ilapo yothene yo Wiciipitu.
Farawoo ahomwiirela tho Yusufu: Mi Farawoo, nanso wohinuulumo naa, khaawo nolamuliya upanka itthu phi itthu mWiciipitu mothene.
Farawoo ahommaha Yusufu ncina na Safenate-Paneya ni ahommaha nthiyana wiira akhale mwaarawe, Asenate, mwana a Potifera, nhooleli osataka yo Oni. Wahoolo Yusufu ahorwaa wonoona ilapo yothene yo Wiciipitu.
Yusufu aarina myakha talathini ceyarelo wapacenryawe unvarela nteko Farawoo, mwene o Wiciiputu. Uyo ahonhiya Farawoo ni ahorwaa woonoona ilapo yothene yo Wiciipitu.
Ukati wo myakha saapa cooruweriya, ilapo yothene yahaana yoolya yinci.
Yusufu ahototokaniha yoolya yalikeleliye usunkiya, yo myakha saapa cooruweriya Wiciipitu ni ahosunka mmakhupini ummaparasa khula iparasa ahototokaniha itiriku yo mmattani.
Commo, Yusufu ahosunka itiriku yinci, toko nhaava wompharyaa. Uyo ahohiya waalikela yoolya iyo kontha khaawo tho oorya uphima mwanlattu wowinciva.
Cihinaya uphiya myakha cotala, Asenate, mwana a Potifera, nhooleli osataka yo Oni, ahonnyarana Yusufu asaana eeli.
Oopacera uyo, Yusufu ahommaha ncina na Manasesi, eeraka: Nluku hokiliyaliha mahuviho aka othene ni inupa yothene ya apaapa.
Mwana onayeeli ahommaha ncina no Farayimi, eeraka: Nluku hokipanka ocayra ilapo yahuvaka.
Commo, cahophiya ummaleloni myakha cooruweriya Wiciipitu,
ni cahopacera myakha saapa cotala, toko Yusufu wahoolelihenryawe uhimya. Yahaawo itala ilapo cothene, nanso ilapo yo Wiciipitu yahaawo yoolya.
Wancenryaya uvola itala ilapo yothene yo Wiciipitu, uneethi wahanca unlepela Farawoo yoolya. Uyo ahaakhula atthu o Wiciipitu, eeraka: Nrwee wa Yusufu ni mpanke inhalaawe wuuhimeryani.
Wamwaryenlyaya itala ilapo cothene, Yusufu aholamula uhuliya makhupi ni ahopacera utumiha itiriku, aatumiheraka atthu o Wiciipitu, maana itala yahotepa.
Ni atthu ookhuma ilapo cothene, yammwa Wiciipitu wiira yathume itiriku wa Yusufu, kontha itala yaanvira itepaka ilapo cothene.
Yakopi Wacuwenlyawe wiira ihawo itiriku Wiciipitu, aheerela asaanawe: Isiyani umakelaka uwehanaca paahi?
Aheera tho: Kiheewa yiiriyaka ihaawo itiriku Wiciipitu. Nrwee wonwo mwanithumele itiriku wiira nipwaherere ukumi ni nihikhwe itala.
Toko coo, asunnawe khumi a Yusufu yahorwaaca Wiciipitu uthuma itiriku.
Yakopi khantthunihile Pencamii, nhimaawe Yusufu, wiira aatthukane ikwaha, kontha aanawoova unkhumelela itthu yoonanara.
Asaana a Isirayeli yaari na atthu akina yarwaca uthuma itiriku, nlattu wotala yavonnle uKanaa.
Yusufu aari nlamuli olapo yo Wiciipitu ni yooyo phaatumihera itiriku atthu othene. Phimaana uphiya waya asunnawe Yusufu yahomuramela mpaka uphiya vathi.
Woona wawe, Yusufu ahaacuwelela asunnawe, nanso aakhanle toko khaacuwenle ni ahoopopiha eeraka: Nyu nnokhumakhuma vayi? Yahaakhulaca: Ninkhuma ilapo yo Kanaa naawile uthuma yoolya.
Yusufu ahaacuwela asunnawe, nanso ayo khayancuwelacile.
Vano ahoopuwela ittora calohilyawe nari na asunnawe ni aheerela: Nyu nri mayoohottela! Mwawile uhottelaca ilapo ehu ila wiira ncuwele nipuro nookhwyaa.
Ale yahaakhulaca: Mena, nkunya. Asaanenyu yawile uthuma yoolya.
Hi othene, athumwanihu ari amoca. Asaanaa ari atthu omaana, khaanakhala oohottela.
Nanso Yusufu ahaakhanyereriha eeraka: Mena! Nyu mwile uhottela wiira moonenele nipuro nookhwyaa ilapo ehu ila.
Ni ale yaheeraca: Asaanaa yaari khumi neeli, othene athumwanaya ari amoca ilapo yo Kanaa. Itthyaako eyo ihanle uwaani na athumwanaya ni nkina uyo hokhwa.
Yusufu ahaakulela eeraka: Phi vaava kihimilyaaka va. Nyu nri mayoohottela.
Nyu nnaahala ulawihiya. Kinalupela mwancina na Farawoo, nyu mu khannokhuma, mwahimmwaneke uno mwanhimenyu eetthyako uyo.
Munrume mmoca anrweele mwanhimenyu uyo vano akina vaa nhotthukiya. Commo phinhaleehu ucuwela wiira cinhimyenyu nnyo ciri citthu ceekhweeli atthuna cowoothiya. Cahikhaleke ceekhweeli, kinalupela mwancina na Farawoo wiira wanaahala ucuwanyaa wiira nyu khweeli nri atthu oohottela!
Ni ahaatthukela nkalapooso mahuku mararu.
Nihuku noneeraru Yusufu aheerelaca: Mi kinamoova Nluku. Mwapheela woopwaa, mpanke coo:
Mwakhala wiira nyu atthu omaana, munhiye munniinyu mmoca nkalapooso mu. Vano akina vaa nturuwaceke nuukusaka itiriku wiira mwalye uwaani.
Nkiwiihere vaa nhimeenyu eetthyako uyo wiira acuwannyee moolumo enyu yakhala wiira eekhweeli ni nyu phinhaleenyu uhikhwa.
Ayo yahotthuna upanka yahiminye eyo ni yaheerelana: Khweeli va ninattarusiya mwanlattu weetthu impankileehu nhimeehu uyo. Naammoonaka caacukula awe, ni waanisonttelelawe vaa, wiira ninhiye nkumi, nanso khanaantthunenle. Phimaana uniphwanyaka uno utapana uno.
Ruupeni ahaakhula: Akoohimenryeni wiira nhinhuvihe mmirawo uyo, nanso nyu khamwatthunne ukiiwa! Vano ninlamuliya waakhulela iphome awe eyo.
Nanso ale khayaacuwela wiira Yusufu naweewa, kontha oolumana ni ntthu aataphulela ni nuulumo naya.
Vaavale Yusufu ahothama ni wunla. Vano ahohokoleela tho ni ahoolumaca wiira atthukiye Simeyoni, othene amoonacaka.
Wahoolo Yusufu aholamula wiira icarihiye itiriku mmirupani mwaya mmo ni ituruseliye ipheeta yo khula ntthu munrupani mwawe, ni avahiye iphika coovira alyaaka. Ni commo wahopankiya.
Ale yahopakhira mirintti caya co tiriku mwa apuuru aya nuukhumaca.
Nipuro naamakilyaya nlattu wo wiileliya, mmoca uyo ahotthukula nrupa awe wiira ankumihe nankanka oonliha puuru awe, ni ahoona ipheeta umalakuni wonrupa awe.
Ni aheerela asunnawe: Kihoturuseliya ipheeta aka eyo. Ila mu munrupani mwaka mu. Yoovaka wanrimani waya ni attettemelaka yaheerelana: Isiyani ila Nluku inipankilyawe ela?
Waaphilyaya wathumwanaya, ilapo yo Kanaa, yahohimyaca cothene caakhumelenle, yiiraka:
Nlopwana mwaneene ilapo eyo honuulumacera ni honihela ukhala hi atthu oohottela.
Nanso hi nihonroromeliha wiira khanihiwena atthu oohottela niri atthu eekhweeli.
Niheera tho wiira naari asaana khuumi neeli athumwanihu ari amoca ni mwana mmoca uyo hokhwa, ni eethyako uyo ri na athumwanihu uKanaa.
Vano nlopwana mwaneene ilapo eyo honiirela: Nrwee noone mwakhala atthu eekhweeli: Nhimeenyu mmoca nolamuliya uhala vaava ni mi. Akina ayo aturuweke ni akuseke yoolya yalyeke uwaani na akhwaya.
Nanso mwakiwiihere nhimenyu eetthyako uyo phinhalaaka ukupali mi wiira nyu atthu omaana ni khannakhala mayoohottela. Vano phinhalaka wuhokoloserani munninyu uyo ni wutthuniherani upanka marontta ila ilapo ela.
Weetthiyaaya mirintti nnyo, wo khula nrintti wahophwanyinya nhukho woocara ipheeta. Yakopi na asaanawe woonnyaya mihukho nnye, yahoovaca.
Ni Yakopi aheerelaca: Nyu nnakimalihera asaanaka ayo! Kihanle wohi Yusufu, nnavaa kiri wohi Simeyoni, ninlelo nna nnopheela unkusa Pencamii? Cothene cinkikhuma mi!
Vano Rupeni aheerela athumwane: Kahinturuwaneke Pencamii uyo, mweevakace asaanaka oyeeli khaweetthu. Nkihiyere Pencamii uyo, thi mi kinhala unwacawaca.
Nanso athumwane yahaakhula: Mwanaka uyo khannonkusa. Munnawe hokhwa. Uyo nna phihanle. Itthu phi itthu yoonanara inhala unkhumelela eyo munkwahani mmo, vano phinhalenyu uvitha ipwi caka nnyo mmahiye kinari ni icuku.
Itala yaanatepa mwiilaponi mmo.
Vano wamanlyaya itiriku yothene yawiihilyaya asaana a Yakopi akhumanaka Wiciipitu, athumwanaya yaheerelaca: Nhokoleelace ni mwathume tho yoolya.
Nanso Yutta aheerela: Nlopwana uyo ahonileehera venci eeraka: Nhihokoleelace waryaaka wohimmwiiha nhimenyu uyo.
Mwanivahaka nhimehu uyo ninrwaanaka, ninaarwa, ninkoothuma ni wuthumelani yoolya.
Nanso mwahinivaheke ninrwanaka, khaninrwaa, kontha nlopwana uyo hoolumacile coo: Nhihokoleelace waryaka kahiki mwammwiihaka nhimenyu uyo.
Isirayeli ahokoha: Nkipankenleni yoonanara toko ila, munhimeryaka nlopwana uyo wiira nhaanaca nhimenyu nkina?
Ni ale yahomwaakhulaca: Uyo honikohakoha hi na amucihu. Ni honikoha tho eeraka: Athumwaninyu nanlelo ahaawo akumi? Nyu nhaana nhimenyu nkina? Hi nimwaakhunle paahi itthu yanikohawe. Nahala ucuwela cani wiira nohala uniirela mummwiihe nhimenyu.
Vano Yutta ahomwiirela Isirayeli athumwane: Munhiye mmirawo uyo kinrwaane, ninarwaca, wiira nyu ni hi na asaanehu nikhale akumi ni nihikhwe.
Ni kinawiilupelela veekhaka unvarelela uyo. Nkiheleke mi ukhala mayonvarelela mwana uyo. Kahinturuwaneke mpaka wuthonyerani wamiithoni winyu, phi mi cinhala ukikhalela ikhirini nnyo wamiithoni winyu ukati wothene.
Toko cinoonenyu, yiiriyaka khanapicile cono ninarwele ni ninaturuwile imaara piili.
Vano Isirayeli, athumwane Yutta, yahomwiirela: Wakhala wiira phinhalaya wiirannyaa, haya wakhale ciicammo. Nhele munrupani mwinyu mmo coolya comaana co mwiilaponi mwihu mu ni munkusere yooyo nlopwana uyo; makhura onrette vakani, urawo vakani, citthu coonukhela cikina ni miira, cowiima ni amentowa:
Nkuse ipheeta yoopitaanihinya, imaara piili piili ni nhokolose ipheeta yaheliye munrupani mwinyu waturuwenyu wa malakuni wo nrupa enyu. Kahiki itthu iyo ikhumelenle nlattu woovonyanihinya.
Munkuseke nhimenyu uyo ni nhokoleele wa nlopwana uyo.
Nluku Okuru-Cothene awooneleni ikiriri iriyari ya nlopwana uyo wiira ootthunihereni onturuwana nhimeenyu Pencamii ni nhimeenyu nkina uyo. Mi, kakhalaka woohasaana, kinakhalaka.
Vano asilopwana ale yahorwaa ni yahokhuruwela Wiciipitu anakusileene coovaha, ipheeta yoopitaanihinya piili piili ni Pencamii, ni yahorwaa wa Yusufu.
Yusufu, wamoonnyawe Pencamii na asunnawe, ahomwiirela nhooleli owapuwani wawe: Waakuse alopwana ala owaanyaka, wamwiive mwanama ni onlokihace, kontha ayo yoolya yoothana anhala ulya ni mi.
Ni ule ahopanka yahimeriyawe ni ahaakusaca mpaka inupa ya Yusufu.
Ayo yahoovaca wakusiyaya arwaaninyaka owaanyawe Yusufu ni yahoopuwela yiiraka: Niwiiheriye va nlattu wopheeta ihokoloseriye munrinttini mwihu ikwaha yoopacera: Uyo nophavela onittarusa, onihuviha, onipanka ipottha nuukusa inama cihu nnyo.
Phimaana, yahorwaa wa nhooleli onupa ya Yusufu ni yahomwiirela wakelaya wankhora.
Uviriyane, yoowe nkunya! Ikwaha yoopacera yawilehu va khweeli nawile othuma yoolya.
Nanso nipuro neemenlehu wiira nimake, nahotthukula mirintti cihu ni utthukula woono khula ntthu wakhalacenrehu ahophwanya ipheeta yawiihilyawe uwaani yoolikaneene. Phimaana nihohokolosa,
nuwiiha ipheeta ikina wiira nithume yoolya. Khanincuwenle ntthu nihelenle ipheeta mmirinttini mwihu mmo.
Vano nhooleli ule aheera: Nkhalane nnema. Nluku inyu, phi Nluku a athumwaninyu, phuvahileni nhakhu munrinttini mwinyu mmo, kontha ipheeta enyu kahaakhela. Vano ahontthukula Simiyoni nunrweha waryaya asunnawe.
Wahoolo, ahaarwana inupa ya Yusufu, ni ahaavaha maasi, uwiwululacera inyaa ni inama caya nnyo ahovaha yoolya.
Vano ayo yahototokaniha coovaha caya cahalaya unvaha Yusufu uthana, kontha yahocuwela wiira phahalaya unlyana.
Waphilyawe Yusufu yahonvaha cammwiihenryaya ni yahonlapela yooromaka mpaka vathi.
Vano uyo ahaakohaca isalaama ni aheerela tho: Ari eehalini athumwaninyu, nlopwana oowuluvala kihimenryenyu uyo? Nanlelo haawo nkumi?
Ayo yahaakhulaca: Nrumeyaa, athumwanihu, nanlelo akumi, ahaawo salaama, ni othene yahonlapela.
Awehaka nceresere ni amoonaka nhimaawe Pencamii, mwana aanumwane, Yusufu ahokoha: Ula phi yooyo nhimenyu etthyako kihimenryenyu uyo? Ni ahopwaherera tho eeraka: Nluku oovahe nnema, mwanaka,
nlattu wootteeliya woomoona nhimaawe, Yusufu ahokhuma akuvyacaka wiira aphavele nipuro nowunla, ni akelaka mpaani, ahoonla.
Wakhucilyawe, ahokhuma ni eewehawehaka, aheera: Aliyeke yoolya eyo.
Ahomeeliya yoolya veekhawe Yusufu, woohatakanelana asunnawe ale, ni annaciipitu yalyanawe na ayo yahomeeliya veekha, kontha annaciipitu khayaalamuliya walyana annaperewu. Uyo waari mwiikho aya.
