Asunnawe yaheesiya wameca, attharanihiyaka mookomelo ayo, maciso eeyareelo, ukhuma omuulupale mpaka omwankani ni yammwehanaca atikhinacaka.
Vano yahomeeliya yoolya ya Yusufu wa meeca. Ni mencivelo o yoolya ya Pencamii yari yoopwaha imaara thanu menciviheriyo o yoolya ya asunnawe, ni yahoolyaca venci nuuwurya catthunaya.
Yusufu ahonvaha nhooleli owapuwani wawe, nna nlamulo nna: Ncarihe mmirinttini mwaya ala atthu ala yoolya yo khula nkwaratati mpaka cinhalaya woorya ukusa ni nhele ipheeta iwannyawe khula ntthu omalakuni womirinttini cawe.
Wahoolo nhele ikoomisi aka, yopheeta, munrinttini mwa mwana eetthyako uyo, ni wamoca ni ipheeta inthumenlyawe tiriku. Ni uyo ahopanka cothene toko cahimeriyawe ni Yusufu.
Wasilyaya, yaholehaca atthu ale ni inama caya.
Yaari ahinayaca upwaha iparasa eyo, phu ukati Yusufu wamwiirenlyawe nhooleli owapuwani wawe: Wunwe ni watthimakele atthu ale ni waaphwanyaka weerele: Nnakakhaniherani itthu yooreera ni yoonanara.
Khinakhala ila ikoomisi immureryawe nkunya aka ni immwaserera awe ihako? Nyu nhopanka yoonanara.
Waaphwanyilyawe ahaakuleliha ala moolumo ala.
Nanso ayo yahomwiirelaca: Nlattuni nkunya wuulumacaka commo? Uttayi ni yeeyo itthu iyo mpankaca arumeyaa.
Wooneke nsurukhu ula, uphwanyileehu umalakuni wo mirupa cihu, nihooturuselani nikhumaka ilapo yo uKanaa, naahala winnyacerani inupa ya nkunyaa ipheeta ni iwooru.
Akhalaka wiira mmoca wa arumeyi aa naphwanyaninya, eeviye, ni hi akina va ninakhala ipottha ca nkunya ehu.
Uyo aheera: Kihokupali. Yooyo nohala uphwanyaninya uyo, phinhala ukhala ipottha aka, akina ayo anawoopwaa.
Khula ntthu ahokurusa mirintti cawe wowakuvyaa ni wanca utaphula.
Nhooleli uyo ahanca uphavelaca wo khula nrintti, apaceraka wa muulupale mpaka umalihera wa mwana eethyako uyo. Ni ikoomisi iyo yahophwanyinya munnrinttini wa Pencamii.
Wakhumelenlyaya commo, ayo yahaahulaca coowara caya. Wahoolo, othene yahopakhiraca mirintti caya nuuturuwela arwaaka uparasa.
Yutta na asunnawe waphiyacilyaya inupa ya Yusufu, ni ule ari wonwo. Vano ale yahoromaca wamiithoni waawe ula, mpaka uphiya vathi.
Yusufu ahaakohaca: Ikipankacilenyu iyo isiyani? Nyu khannocuwelaca wiira ntthu toko mi kinawoorya uwasera ihako?
Vano Yutta aheera: Ninhala uwaakhulani nkunya? Ninhala uhimyani? Ninhala upanka cani mwaavi wiira niphwanye isariya? Nluku hokumihera wonene unyali ihu. Nkunya hi nna va ipottha caa. Wamoca ni uyo phwanyaninye ikoomisi iyo.
Vano aheera Yusufu: Akimpanka mi commo. Yooyo ntthu mphwanyaninye ikoomisi iyo phinhala ukhala ipottha aka. Wiireke nyu akina vaa, nturuweleke ni nnema waathumwaninyu.
Vano Yutta ahonciserera yoole, ni aheera: Sontte nkunya ukihiye, kinawulepela, kihaana nuulumo noophela wuulumaca wamiithoni waa, nkunnya aka, ni nhikiviruwele, kontha nyu nri toko Farawoo.
Nkunya aka uhaakoha arumeyi aa wiiraka: Nhaanaca athumwaninyu atthuna nhimenyu?
Hi nihoohimyacera nkunya niiraka: Nihaana athumwanihu owuuluvala ni mmirawo mmoca nnyanryaya anooluvanle, nhimehu. Ahaawo munnaawe yooyo ooyaraninya nrukulu nimoca hookhwa. Anumwane ayo anhalanne yooyo, ni athumwane ananfenta venci.
Vano we nkunya uhonireela: Nkiwiihere komoone mmiithoni mwaka.
Ni hi nihowiirela: Nkunya, mmirawo uyo khanhala waahiya athumwane, kontha arimelaru uyo apapeehu anaakhwa.
Vano nyu nheerela karumeya enyu: Mwahinmwanaceke mwanhimenyu uyo, khannohala woonaca ikhove aka.
Weeraka coo: Hi karumeya aa, nihorwaa waathumwanihu nihattonkela moolumo yoolumacilyaa nkunya.
Athumwanihu wanirenlyaya tho wiira nturuwele mwathume yoolya.
Hi niheerela: Khanintthuna urwaa nwo veekhehu. Ninhala uturuwela tho nwo mwanhimehu eetthyako uyo nanrwaanaka, kontha khaninkela namoonaka nkunya uyo ikhove awe mwanhimehu ahirweke ni hi.
Vano honirela karumeya aa, athumwanihu, coo: Nyu nhocuwelaca wiira amwaaraka yayanre asaana eeli.
Mmoco uyo heetta ni mi kiinre, khweeli yooyo hokhuriya, ni akimmoona tho mpaka nna.
Vano mwankusaka ula waamiithoni waka, ni imwiirannyaka itthu phi itthu iyo, nnaahala uvitha irutthu aka mmahiye ni icuku.
Nna va mi karwaka waathumwanihu, karumeya aa, woohinrwana mmirawo uyo, athumwanihu cinryaaya wonvarecesa.
Anaahala ukhwa ucukula yakela yanoonaka uturuwa veekha wohi mmirawo ula. Ni hi ninaahala wavitha apaapehu ayo ni masukuli.
Phimaana mi kiceemesaka wamiithoni waa unsunka mmirawo uyo ni kiheerela: Aahituruwele tho uno ikikhalele mi ikhirini iyo mahuku othene.
Vano nna mi kikhale ipottha ya nkunya aka nipuro nahalawe ukhala mmirawo uyo. Vano uyo arweeke uwaani na asunnawe ayo.
Kinkohimya isiyani mi karwaka waathumwane wohinkusa mmirawo uyo? Akintthuna woona mi yoonanara inhala wakhuma apaapa ayo.
Yooyo ukati uyo Yusufu anawoolwana wiivithavitha nwo wamiithoni wa atthu othene, phimaana ahokhuwa eeraka: Mwakumihe ananrumeya ayo othene va. Co khaawo ahanle nenno nipuro nno, ukati ule Yusufu weecuwanehilyawe na asunnawe.
Vaavale ule ahanca wunla venci mpaka Annaciipitu wiiwa ni ihapari iyo yahophiya waFarawoo.
Vano aheerela Yusufu asunnawe ale: Mi Yusufu. Apaapa nannelo ahaawo akumi? Nanso asunnawe ale yahosankaca venci, mpaka woolwana umwaakhula.
Ni aheerelaca Yusufu asunnawe ale: Nciserace woono. Umwattameryaca waya, aheerelaca: Mi nhimeenyu Yusufu, yoole nyu munthumihileenyu arwaninyaka Wiciipitu.
Vano va nhicukulace ni nhiiriyelele mwanlattu nyu wookithumiha kiwaaninyaka uno, kontha Nluku aacenre wiira woopwe ukumi watthu enci, phimaana akiholihaka uno.
Nna nhina woomyakha miili niri nhina ntalani ilapo yothene, ni cinaahala myakha mithanu khacinhala waaliya ni hata wuruliya.
Nanso Nluku hokihooliha uno wiira kikhale ipyo yoomuci mwiilaponi mu ni kiwoopoleni ni wuukhikicerani venci.
Khannakhala thi nyu nkiwanne uno, nanso Nluku, ni hokipanka ukhala namanantthu a Farawoo ni nlamuli o uhano ni nlamuli o Wiciipitu wothene.
Nturuwele wowakuvyaa waapaapa ni mwaahimerye: Nohimya co mwaninyu Yusufu: Nluku mi hokipanka mwaneene ilapo yothene yo Wiciipitu. Mmwe woono, woohipica.
Nyu nnowokhala nttetthe wo Koseni, vakhiviru ni mi. Ukhuma nyu, asaanenyu ayo, ucuulu inyu uyo, ikhontwaa cinyu nnyo, imope cinyu nnyo ni ikaruma cinyu nnyo cothene mmwane.
Mi kinnowulihani kontha cinaahala tho va myakha mithano cotala. Mwahitthuneke nyu na amucinyu othene ni mihuwo cinyu cothene nnahala uhuva.
Cothene nnawoona ni miitho enyu, ni nhimaka Pencamii phi saahiti. Nawoona wiira khweeli thi mi kinoolumaca nnya citthu nnya.
Mwahimerye apaapa waneerihiyaka woolemelihiya mi Wiciipitu ni citthu cothene cinoonenyu. Ni mwaawihe apaapa woono wowaakuvyaa.
Vano ule ahonkapatta Pencamii nhimaawe oonlaka uno, ni Pencamii ciicammo ahonvara mmakhatani mmo ni uyo oonlaka uno.
Wahoolo ahaavaha alaahuma asunnawe ni othene yahoonlaca. Waculuru asunnawe ayo phoonryaya umuulumana.
Vano weewiiyaya uhano wiira asunnawe Yusufu ahowaca, Farawoo ni mahumu awe othene yahotteeliya.
Vano Farawoo ahomwiirela Yusufu: Waahimerye asunnaayo yapakhirihe mirintti nnyo asinama ayo, aturuwele ilapo yo Kanaa.
Ni yaturuwele woono, yaawihe athumwana na alokwaa othene. Mi kinnowavaha itthaya yomaana mWiciipitu mu ni nyu nnaahala ulawa nhakhu weelapo ila.
Waarume yakuse ampakhira o Wiciipitu wiira yaawiihe asaaraya, asaanaya na athumwaninyu.
Cihukukureheni citthu cinyu, kontha mapuro ooreera o Wiciipitu anhala ukhala awinyu.
Commo yahopanka asaana a Isirayeli. Yusufu ahaavaha asunnawe ampakhira ni iphika toko Farawoo calamunlyawe.
Wo khula ntthu ahonvaha nrintti wokuwo conaanano, nanso ni Pencamii ahomvaha makoopiri opheeta iminya ttharu ni mirintti mithanu cokuwo conaanano.
Athumwane ahaavelelihera inama coopakhira khumi, cinapakhinre citthu cootepa ooreera co Wiciipitu, ni inama khumi coopakhira cinakusile itiriku, mikatthe ni iphika cikina co munkwahani.
Wahoolo aholeehana na asunnawe, ni wakhumaya aheerelaca: Nhinyakulihane ni iphiro!
Yahohokolya Wiciipitu aturuwelaka wathumwanaya aneehaninya Yakoopi ilapo yo Kanaa,
ni yahottonkaca ihapari yiiraka: Yusufu ninlelo haawo nkumi! Khweeli yooyo phi nlamuli olapo yothene yo Wiciipitu. Vaavale nrima wa Yakopi wahomwattakyaa ni ahovittikhuwa. Ni khaalamuliya waakupali asaanawe ayo.
Nanso wahimeriyawe cothene calehenryawe Yusufu, ni Yakopi oonaka ampakhira yavelelihilyawe Yusufu wiira arweliye, nnepa awe wahokhala mmapuroni.
Isirayeli aheera: Paahi! Mwanaka Yusufu ninlelo haawo nkumi. Kinkomoona kihinakhwa.
Isirayeli ahokhuma ni citthu cothene carinawe. Uphiya wawe uPeresepa, ahovaha citthu anlapelaka Nluku a Isaki, athumwane.
Ni Nluku ahomuulumana Isirayeli uhiyu nnyoonini eeraka: Yakopi, Yakopi! Uyo ahaakhula eeraka: Kiri va.
Nluku aheera: Mi kiri Nluku, Nluku a athumwana. Uhoove urwaa Wiciipitu, kontha wonwo kinkowupanka nloko nuulupale.
Mi kinaahala urwaa Wiciipitu wamoca ni we, ni khweeli kinaahala wuuhokolosa. Ni ntata na Yusufu ninaahala uputthaputtha miitho aa.
Vaavale Yakopi ahokhuma uPeresepa. Asaana a Isirayeli yahaakusaca athumwanaya, asaanaya ni asaaraya mwampakhira yakumihilyawe Farawoo.
Ciicammo yakokusa inama caya ni mihakhu cothene caphwannyilyaya uKanaa. Commo Yakopi ahorwaa Wiciipitu ni ucuulu awe wothene.
Ahaakusa Wiciipitu asaanawe, ucuulu awe, asaanawe asithiyana na asiculawe asithiyana, manaaya wiira, nloko nawe nothene.
Ala phi macina a atthu o nloko na Yakopi yarwele Wiciipitu: Rupeni, ntthaara na Yakopi.
Ala phaari assana a Rupeni: Enoki, Palu, Esiroomi ni Karimu.
Ala pha asaana a Simeyoni: Yemuweli, Yamini, Owati, Yakimi, Sowari ni Sawulu, mwana a nthiyana nKanaa.
Ala phaari asaana a Levi: Kerisoni, Kowate ni Merari.
Ala phaari asaana a Yutta: Eri, Onani, Selaa, Peresi ni Seraa. Eri ni Onani yakhwile ilapo yo Kanaa. Ala phaari asaana a Peresi: Esiromi ni Hamuli.
Ala phaari asaana a Isakaari: Tolaa, Puwaa, Yaasupe ni Sinromi.
Ala phaari asaana a Sepuloni: Serete, Eloni ni Yaleeli.
Ala phaari asaana yayanryawe Leya ni Yakopi uPatani-Aramu, unhiya mwanawe Tina. Ucuulu awe wothene waari talathini na araru (33).
Ala phaari asaana a Kaate: Sefomi, Haaci, Suuni, Esipomi, Eri, Aroti ni Areli.
Ala phaari asaana a Aseri: Imina, Isivaa, Isivii ni Periyasi, ni mwanrokoraya Sera. Ala phaari asaana a Periya: Heperi ni Malekiyeli.
Ala pha asaana khuumi na siita yayanryawe Yakopi ni Siilipa, ipottha ya Lapanu, anvahaka mwanawe Leeya.
Ala phaari asaana a Rakeli, amwaara a Yakopi: Yusufu ni Pencamii.
Asenate, mwana a Potifera, nhooleli osataka yo Oni, ahommaha asaana eeli Yusufu Wiciipitu: Manasesi ni Farayimi.
Ala phaari asaana a Pencamii: Pelaa, Pekeri, Asipeli, Sera, Namani, Eyi, Rosi, Mupimi, Hupimi ni Aarite.
Ala phaari asaana a Rakeli ayanryawe ni Yakopi othene yaari khumi na cese.
Mwana a Tani aari Husimi.
Ala phaari asaana a Nafitali: Yaseeli, Kuni, Yeseri ni Silemi.
Ala phaari atthu saapa onrukulu na Piila, ipottha ya Lapanu aamahilyawe mwanawe Rakeli, ayanryawe ni Yakopi ahomwiihana Yakopi.
Othene yarwele Wiciipitu ni Yakopi, ucuulu awe wothene woohalikelela asaara asaanawe, yaari sitiini na siita atthwene.
Woncerera asaana eeli a Yusufu yayanryawe Wiciipitu, nloko na Yakopi naarwele Wiciipitu nahophiya Sapiini (70).
Vano, Yakopi ahonhooliha Yutta wa Yusufu, wiira acuwele maphiyero o Koseni. Uphiya waya nwo,
Yusufu, na ampakhira awe oolikana, ahorwaa uKoseni wiira aakumanane athumwane. Vano woona wawe, aheekamela ni waakapatta, vano nakapattilene, ahoonla ukati mwinci.
Isirayeli ahomwiirela Yusufu: Nna miva pooti ukhwa, kontha kihoona ikhove aa ni kihocuwela wiira ninlelo we uri nkumi.
Vano Yusufu aheerela asunnawe na amuci aya othene athumwane: Kinarwa unhimerya Farawoo wiira asunnaka na amuci aya apaapa yakhala uKanaa ahowa woono.
Kinkowiira, alopwana ayo ahakheli, anhakhela inama ni ahowana ikhontwaa caya, imope caya ni cothene ciri cawaya.
Farawoo awiihanakani ookohakani wiira: Nnovarani va?
Mmwaakhuleke coo: Arumeyi aa anhuwa inama ikhumelo ni nari acikani, toko capankaya amuci ihu okhalayi. Commo phinhalenyu utthuniheriya ukhala nttetthe wo Koseni, kontha ahakheli othene anathanyiya na annaciipitu.
Yusufu ahorwaa wa Farawoo unvaha ihapari eeraka: Apaapa na asunnaka ahowa. Ankhuma uKanaa ni ikhontwaa caya, imope caya ni mihakhu cothene cirinaya. Nna ari uKoseni.
Wahoolo ahaathanla asunnawe athanu ni ahonthoonyihera Farawoo.
Farawoo ahaakoha: Nnovara ntekoni? Ayo yahomwaakhulaca: Karumeya aa ari ahakheli onama toko amuci ihu okhalayi.
Yahomwiirelaca tho: Naawile ukhala mu ukati vakani kontha itala uKanaa nwo inaatepa, ni inama ca karumeya aa khacinoona yoolya. Sontte, watthunihere karumeya aa ukhala uKoseni.
Vano Farawoo ahomwiirela Yusufu: Athumwana na asunnaa yowenle we
ni ilapo yo Wiciipitu iri ni we. Upanke mananna ooreera, wiira athumwanaa na asunnaa akhale mapuro omaana. Waahiye akhale uKoseni. Woona wiira akina ayo ari atthu ankhili, waavahe nteko woohakhela inama caka.
Vano Yusufu ahaakusa athumwane mpaka wa Farawoo, ni Yakopi ahonreeriha Farawoo.
Farawoo ahonkoha Yakopi eeraka: Urina myakha mikavi?
Yakopi ahomwaakhula Farawoo eeraka: Myaaka caka co weettakaca ciri iminya wo talathini (130). Ciri vakani ni coorika, ni khacimphiya toko cakhalaya mayapaapa.
Vano Yakopi ahonreeriha Farawoo ni ahorwaa.
Yusufu aheesa ni waavaha athumwane ni asunnawe mapuro oocayira olapo yo Wiciipitu, nttetthe wo uRamacese, toko calamunlyawe Farawoo.
Ahaavaha yoolya yo watosa, ukhuma athumwane, asunnawe ni amucyawe othene mpaka asaana yarinawe khula ntthu.
Khayaariwo yoolya ilapo yothene kontha itala yanatepa, ukhuma Wiciipitu mpaka uKanaa wanaakhwiya nlattu wotala.
Yusufu ahototokaniha ncurukhu wothene waari Wiciipitu mpaka uKanaa wathumeliye itiriku ni ahorwana waFarawoo.
Waamanlyaya ncurukhu wothene Wiciipitu mpaka uKanaa, annaciipitu yahorwaa unlepela Yusufu yiiraka: Univahe yoolya! Uhinihiye nikhwaaka itala nlattu woomala ncurukhu ihu.
Yusufu aheerela, paahi mmwihe inama cinyu nnyo mwaakakhanihe ni itiriku, kamana ncurukhu inyu uyo uhomala.
Yusufu ahowiiheriya inama nnyo ni ule ahaavaha itiriku akakhanihaka ni ikhavalu, ikhontwaa, imope ni apuuru. Mwakha wothene ahaaliha annaciipitu yakakhanihaka yoolya ni inama.
Mwakha oyo wahovira ni wawilyaya mwakha nkina, yahoturuwela tho wa Yusufu yiiraka: Khaninoona tho mananna oowiipitha we kontha ncurukhu ihu uyo uhomala ni inama cihu nnyo cihokhala cawaa, khiiwo tho inihalenle uvaha cihikhanle irutthu cihu ni imatta cihu.
Uhinihiye nikhwaaka ni ukhwelakhwela imatta cihu wa miithoni waa, unithume hi ni uthume imatta cihu nnyo wakakhanihaka ni itiriku, vano hi ni imatta cihu nnyo, ninakhala ipottha ca Farawoo. Univahe yoolya wiira nikhale akumi, nihikhwe itala ni ciicammo imatta cihu cihihononyee.
Commo Yusufu ahothuma imatta cothene co Wiciipitu anthumelaka Farawoo. Annaciipitu yahothumiha imatta caya cothene kontha itala pheerihile commo. Phimaana ilapo yothene yahokhala ya Farawoo.
Ukhuma wariyari mpaka mmaceresere mothene molapo yo Wiciipitu, Yusufu ahaapanka ipottha atthu othene.
Cahanle coohithuminya caari paahi imatta ca ahooleli osataka kontha Farawoo aholamula uvahiya coolya, cennyo phaapisiha nrima phimaana ahithumihaka imatta caya.
Vano Yusufu aheerela atthu ale: Nviriyane. Ilelo kihoothumani nyu ni imatta cinyu nnyo, nna vaa nri a Farawoo, ipyo phi ila, nlimeke ni waala ittima nnyo.
Nanso nhaana munvahaka Farawoo mphantte woneethanu wo coolya cinhalenyu wuurula. Mphantte woneecese uyo unhala ukhala wawinyu wiira mpanke ipyo ni yoolya yawinyu ni ya asaana enyu ni atthu othene ankhala uwaannyu nwo.
Ale yahomwiirelaca: Nkunya, we uhoopola ukumi ihu kamana uhonipanka nnema ninakhala ipottha ca Farawoo.
Toko coo, itthaya yothene yo Wiciipitu, Yusufu ahokumiha nlamulo niriwo mpaka ilelo. Mphantte wonethanu wo coolya unkhala wa Farawoo, nanso imatta ca ahooleli osataka khacinkhala ca Farawoo.
Annasirayeli yahokhala Wiciipitu, ncoko wo uKoseni. Wonwo yahophwanya imatta cinci ni yahoyaranaca ni wuncereranyaa venci.
Yakopi ahokhala myakha khumi na saapa Wiciipitu ni myakha cookumi awe cari iminya wa arupayini na saapa (147).
Wonnyawe wiira uhaattamerya ukati wookhwa, Isirayeli ahomwiihana mwamwanawe ni ahomwiirela: Wakhala wiira unakifenta, ukivare mweetto ni ulupele wiira unaahala ukhala eekhweeli ni mi. Vano kinwiirela uhikivithe mWiciipitu mu.
Kakhwaka vale, uhikivithe mWiciipitu mu nanso ukirwaane mahiye avithiye mayapaapa uKanaa. Yusufu ahaakhula: Kinkopanka toko cinkilepelenyu.
Vano Isirayeli ahonkhanyereriha eeraka: Ulupele. Yusufu aholupela ni Isirayeli aheecatalela wankorini.
Unavinre ukati vakani, Yusufu ahohimerya wiira: Athumwanaa anawerennya ni ule ahorwaa waathotola, warwaawe vaa ahaakusa asaana awe eeli, Manasesi ni Farayimi.
Yakopi ahohimerya wiira: Mwamwanaa Yusufu howa wuuthotola. Isirayeli aheemananiha wunwa mpaka woorya wunkoma wankorini.
Ni ahomwiirela Yusufu: Nluku Okuru-Cothene hokiphwanya uPeteeli, ilapo yo uKanaa ni hokireeriha,
eeraka: Nloko naa nno ninahala uyaraca ni winciva ni mommo, cinkokhumelela ilapo cinci ca atthu ni kinkowuvahani ilapo ela ukhala yawinyu ukati wothene.
Vano, asaanaa eeli, Farayimi ni Manasesi waayarenlyaa Wiciipitu mi kihinaya uwa uno, ari awaka; toko ciryawe Rupeni ni Simiyoni.
Vano asaana anhalaa waayara ayo awaa, nanso mwanlattu wookhala nrukulu nimoca na Manasesi ni Farayimi na ayo anaahala waakhela mphantte wohiyeriya unaaca asunnaya.
Mi kikhumaka uPatani, keettaka ni iphiro kihocukula nlattu wokikhwela Rakeli ilapo yo uKanaa unahanle vakani uphiya uFarata. Kihonvitha ni iphiro yoorwaa uFarata, uneehaninya uPetelehemu.
Woonnyawe Isirayeli asaana a Yusufu, ahokoha eeraka: Ala tasipani?
Ala pha asaana Nluku akivahilyawe. Vano Isirayeli aheera: Waawane woono kawareerihe.
Miitho a Isirayeli yahoririyaca mwanlattu wo wuuluvala ni ule khoonaca ratta. Phimaana Yusufu ahaakusa asaanawe ayo ni weemesa vakhiviru waya athumwane. Vano Isirayeli ahaavaha alaahuma ni waakapatta,
ni ahomwiirela Yusufu: Akaacuwela wiira kinawoona tho ikhovyaa, nna vaa Nluku hokitthunihera woona asaanaa.
Vano Yusufu ahaatamiha wamweettoni wa athumwane ni ahooroma mpaka iyuuci awe uphiya vathi.
Vano Yusufu ahaakusa oyeeli, Farayimi ahomweesa moono nlopwana vakhiviru waya moono nthiyana wa Isirayeli, ni Manasesi ahomweesa moono nthiyana vakhiviru waya moono nlopwana wa Isirayeli ni oyeeli ahaaciserihaca wa Isirayeli.
Vaavale Isirayeli ahotaphula ntata no moono nlopwana nuuthatela wa muru wa Farayimi mwana omwankani, ni avirikanihaka myoono nnyo, ahokusa ntata no moono nthiyana nuuthatela wa muru wa Manasesi mwana omuulupale.
Vano ahonreeriha Yusufu eeraka: Nluku amweettelaya mayaapaapa Aparahamu ni Isaki, Nluku kihaakhenle meettelo aka mpaka nihuku noleelo.
Ncelo kooponle coonanara cothene, waareerihe ala amirawo ala. Yihaneliye ncina naka ni macina o mayapaapa Aprahamu ni Isaki, ni wincive uneethi aya vathiva.
Woonnyawe Yusufu athumwane yeesaka ntata no moono nlopwana wa muru wa Farayimi, khawancivenle. Phimaana ahovara ntata na athumwane apheelaka waakakhaniha naari wa muru wa Manasesi weesa wa Farayimi ni naari wa muru wa Farayimi weesa wa muru wa Manasesi.
Ni aheerela: Nhipanke commo paapa. Ula phi omuulupale, mweeseke ntata ninyu no moono nlopwana wa muru wawe vaa.
Nanso athumwane yahokhotta ni yahomwiirela coo: Mi kinacuwela, mwanaka, mi kinacuwela. Ni uyo naahala ukhalana uneethi mwinci ni naahala ukhala nkhuulupale. Nanso unokhalaru ciicammo, nhimaawe uyo phinhala utepa ukhala muulupale wompwaha munnaawe uyo ni uneethi awe unaahala ukhala mwinci.
Commo Yakopi ahaareerihaca wowaareeriha nenno nihuku nno eeraka: Uneethi wo Isirayeli wapheelaka ureerihana unahala uromola macina enyu wiiraka coo: Nluku opanke we toko campankilyawe Farayimi ni Manasesi. Ni ahomweesa Farayimi uhoolo wa Manasesi.
Wahoolo Isirayeli ahomwiirela Yusufu: Kihanle vakani ukhwa, nanso Nluku nohala ukhala ni nyu ni naahala wuuturuselani ilapo ya amuci inyu okhalayi.
Vano we ukhala wiira uhaana iyuulupale yo wapwaha asunna ayo, kinawuvaha nttetthe uri myako wakhilyaka Amorewu ni ikatana ni myura caka.
Vano Yakopi aheehana asaanawe ni weerelaca: Mmwaace woono wiira kuuhimeryeni citthu cinhala wuukhumelelani uhoolo.
Nthukumanace va wiira mwiiwe nyu asaana a Yakopi, mwiiwe inhimyawe Isirayeli, athumwaninyu.
Rupeni, we uri ntthaara naka, ikuru caka, nhokorokho woopacera wo mwiirutthuni mwaka, ootepa uttitthimihinya ni ootepa ikuru.
Unaviluwa toko maasi. Khunkhalana tho iyuulupale kontha we uhowela ikori ya athumwana; uhaawela amweettyaka ni uhaaveeha.
Simiyoni ni Levi ari ntthu ni munnaawe, ikatana caya nnyo ciri ikaruma cookhwiri.
Akintthuna upanka mphantte miruku caya nnyo, akintthuna ukhala mmikuttanoni mwaya mmo kontha waviruwacilyaya aheeva atthu enci, nuusama waya nwo ahokwanyulaca ni uthikilaca mitinka imope.
Uhotakhaliya urusiya waya nwo wowoopiha, uhotakhaliya uviruwa waya nwo wookhwiri. Mi kinawaakawanihaca ilapo ya Yakopi ni kinawaamwarusela ilapo yo Isirayeli.
Yutta, asunnaa anaahala wulemeliha, ntata naa ninaahala wavara nsiko eenani aa, asaana a Yakopi anaahala umoromela Yutta wiitho wawe.
Yutta ri toko mwaakharamu, we, mwamwanaka, uneetta toko kharamu oovara. Unonkoma toko kharamu nlopwana ni unrupa toko kharamu nthiyana, tipani nohala woorya wuuwusa?
Nttontto wo omwene khunhala unkhuma Yutta, hata ikopo yo nlamulo khinhala unkhuma mmatatani mwa, mpaka ukati unhalawe uwa mwaneene ni uyo naahala ulemelihiya ni ilapo cothene.
Yooyo naahala untthukelela puuru awe wanrittani woolipa; ikuwo cawe naahala ukattha ni ivinyu, iphome yo uva inamwareela nkuwoni mwawe.
Miitho awe ankootepa uriipa woopwaha ivinyu. Miino awe utepa utteela woopwaha iphepa.
Sepulooni nokokhala nceresere ipharyaa nipuro ninkelaya weemela apaketi, mipika cawe cinaphiya mpaka oSitoni.
Isakaari uri puuru oolipa rupile iriyari mirintti cawe.
Oonaka wiira nipuro nimmumulawe nno niri nooreera ni itthaya eyo iri yoocivela, makhata ayo ahokusa mirintti nuuvara miteko co makokoromwa.
Tani naahala waakihera citthu cikhanle coneethi awe toko nihimo phi nihimo no Isirayeli.
Tani nokokhala toko mwiikhomya unceresere iparapara, ivili inari nceresere iphiro, inluma ikottokottho yo khavalu ni inammulusa ntthu nowela uyo.
Nyenyu Mwaneene Nluku, mi kinawehererya woopola winyu!
Kaate naahala wananiinya ikhotto ni miphwinko, nanso uyo phinhala waatthema ni woomolanihaca.
Meeca a Aseri anhala ucara coolya; Yooyo phinhala uvaha coolya co mamwene.
Nafitali ri toko naahe ookwattula muntthapweni, phimaana napanka isukuhuulu.
Yusufu uri mwiri wo mihokorokho, woomela nceresere iluusi, miritta caya nnyo cinavira waculu waya isiri.
Nuuviruwa wa anamyuupa uhomwaattakanana anvonyeraka myuupa caya nnyo wo nceece.
Nanso muura awe uyo khattinkihile, myoono cawe ciri cokuru ni cowoorya uvonya myuupa, mwanlattu wo ntata na muulupale a Yakopi mwancina na nhakheli, mwala wo Isirayeli.
Mwancina na Nluku a athumwane, ookavihere we, Mwancina na Nluku Okuru Cothene oovahe cinenne iparakha co wirimu, iparakha cowiiserya cinenne, iparakha cocaayira ni cootosa.
Iparakha ca athumwane cinapwaha iparakha co myako cookhalayi. Makhalelo o myako coohimala cennya iparakha nnya cothene cirwee mwiirutthuni mwa Yusufu. Cirwee uhoolo wawe ule aakhanle oomwalanihinya na asunnawe.
Pencamii ri toko mwiici wooluwa wicisuru unakhura inama, ni ucoocilo unakawaniha yahanle.
Ari phi yaala ala apankile mahimo khumi na meeli o Israyeli. Ciicammo athumwanaya phaahimenryaya wowavahaca iparakha, avahiyaka khula ntthu iparakha camwaacile.
Wahoolo Yakopi ahaattonkela asaanawe eerelaka: Kihanle vakani urwaa wa amuci aka akhwile khalayi. Mwakivithe wamoca ni miyapaapa nnikhukuni niri imatta ya Foromi nHitiita.
Nikhuku niri imatta yo Makipela, vakhiviru ni uManree, uKanaa, imatta Aparahamu inthumanannyawe Foromi, nhitita, aaceraka wiira akhale mahiye a amuci awe othene.
Wonwo hovithiya Aparahamu na amwaarawe, Isaki na amwaarawe. Ciicammo wonwo kihonvitha Leya.
Ukhuma imatta eyo ni nikhuku niri mmattani mmo cothene aathumananinye ahitita.
Aanowiira amalihaka wattonkela asaana awe nnya citthu nnya, Yakopi aheecatalela nuukhwa. Vano aahovithiya wamoca na amuci awe.
Yusufu ahaawuluwela athumwane, ahonlela ni waakapatta.
Wahoolo ahaavaha nlamulo akulukhano yaavara nteko nenno nipuro nno wiira yattikitthele nrette wohunttiha irutthu ya athumwane, ni ale yahaattikitthela.
Yahovira mahuku arupayini oolikana, kontha yooyo phaari ukati waalamunliyaya uttikittheliya makhura nrutthu na annaciipitu yahonla mahuku miloko mithanu na miili.
Wavinryaya mahuku onokhwa ayo, Yusufu ahoolumaca ni mahumu a Farawoo eeraka: Wakhala wiira nyu nnakifenta mwamuulumane Farawoo mwancina naka mi.
Apaapa ahokilupeliha yiiraka: Kihanle vakani ukhwa. Mwakivithe mahiiye yiitthenkacenryaka ilapo yo Kanaa. Vano va, mwanvekele wiira akitthunihere urwaa waavitha apaapa akinkela kaapicaka kinawa naanano.
Ahaakhula Farawoo eeraka: Urwee wavithe athumwana ayo toko aneene cuulupelihilyaya.
Vaavale Yusufu ahorwaa waavitha athumwane. Ule ahaatthukana ikwaha malaka kano othene a Farawoo, alamuli yavaranawe nteko wamoca na alamuli othene o Wiciipitu.
Vano wahiya alamuli ayo, yahorwaa ciicammo amuci o ntthoko na Yusufu asunnawe na atthu othene yaari mmatatani mwa Yakopi. Yahinnye uKoseni nwo yaari paahi asaana, imope ni ikhontwaa.
Ciicammo yahavelela atthu uwela ikhavalu naampakhira omope. Ikwaha iyo yaari ya atthu enci.
Uphinnya waya ipuwa ya Atate, vakhiviru ni mooloko Yortani yahocukula ni wunla venci; mpaka Yusufu ahokhala mahuku saapa onlelaka athumwane.
Atthu o Kanaa yakhalakhala yaayo mapuro ayo woona waya wunliya venci wapuwani ya Atate yaheeraca: Annaciipitu ampanka matthanka, phimaana nne nipuro nne nattamanne mooloko Yortani nihaninyaka Apeli-Misirayimi.
Commo asaana a Yakopi yahopanka toko caahimeeriyaya na athumwanaya.
Yahaakusaca athumwanaya mpaka ilapo yo uKanaa ni yahaavithaca nikhuku niri imatta yo Makipela vakhiviru ni uManree, imatta ile yathumiheriyawe Aparahamu ni Foromi Nhitita wiira ikhale ikhapuri coohala uvithana alokwawe Aparahamu.
Naavithileene athumwane ale Yusufu ahoturuwela Wiciipitu na asunnawe na atthu othene yanvelenle.
Asunnawe Yusufu woona waya wiira athumwanaya ahokhwa yaheeraca: Wakhala wiira Yusufu haana itwaana ni hi, ni aphavelaka onivihera ikuhukuhu mwanlattu wa yoonanara yampankilehu, niireke cani?
Phimaana yaholeeheraca nhupi woonhimerya Yusufu wiira: Athumwana ahinaya ukhwa yahoniruma
wiira munhimyacere coo: Kinawuuvekela waalevelele coonanara ni itaampi cuupankilyaya. Nnna vaa ulevelele itaampi ca karumeya a Nluku a athumwanaa. Vano Yusufu wakhela wawe nhupi ule, aahoonla.
Wahoolo yahowaca asunnawe Yusufu ni yahonkhoromela wiitho weene ni yaheeraca: Hi nihowa va, wiira nikhale ipottha caa.
Vano Yusufu aheerelaca coo: Nhoovace, mi kinalamuliya ukhala nipuro na Nluku?
Nyu nhokipankaca mi itthu yoonanara, nanso Nluku hopanka yeeyo itthu iyo ukhala yooreera, wiira mi ilelo kisunke ukumi wa atthu enci.
Phimaana nhoovace, mi kinaahala wuuvahani nyu yoolya wamoca na asaanenyu ayo. Commo phenryawe Yusufu wowamaaliha asunnawe ni ahoolumacera wo nifento.
Vano Yusufu ahokhala Wiciipitu myakha iminya nuuwa khumi, nari wamoca na amuci awe othene na athumwane,
mpaka ahoona ucuulu woneeraru wa asaana a Farayimi. Ni ahaakhelela asaana a Makhiri, mwana a Manasesi ukhala awawe.
Vano Yusufu hinaya ukhwa aheerela asunnawe ayo coo: Kihanle vakani ukhwa, nanso khweeli Nluku naahala wuukaviherani nyu, mpaka naahala wuukumihani ila ilapo ela, oorwehakani ilapo yilupelenlyawe Nluku unvaha Aparahamu, Isaki ni Yakopi.
Vaavale Yusufu aheerelaca asaana a Isirayeli wiira nnolamuliya ulupela, eeraka coo: Nluku ookavihereni nyu, nhala nkumihaca makhuva aka ayo mu.
Phimaana Yusufu aakhwile narina myakha iminya nuuwa khumi (110) ceyarelo. Nrutthu wa Yusufu wahottikittheliya makhura oohunttiha irutthu, nuuheliya ncaneesani ni yahosunkiya Wiciipitu.











































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































Vano nihuku nimoca nuulumo na Mwaneene Nluku nahowa waYona mwana a Amitayi niiraka:
Wunweke ni urweke isitati yuulupale yo Ninive waahimyacereke moolumo aka kontha coonanara caya cowela mpaka waryaka.
Nanso Yona ahonwa atthawaka wamiithoni waMwaneene Nluku arwaka uTarisi, ahokhuruwela uYopa, waaphwanyalyawe ikalawa yarwaa uTarisi, aholivela ikwaha ni ahokela, wiira aatthukane nloko anakalawa yarwaa uTarisi, apheelaka waatthawela uttayi Mwaneene Nluku.
Vano Mwaneene Nluku ahoruma iphyoo yuulupale mpaharini ni ahopanka nkhaya mpaka ikalawa yahanle vakani uphwyaa.
Vaavale anakalawa yahoovaca venci, ni khula ntthu ananlepela nluku awe, ni yahorihela mpaharini mirintti carinaya nkalawani, wiira awukule ulemeliya nwo. Vaavale Yona ahokhuruwela nhina ikalawa weecatalenlyawe arupaka ikhove.
Nhooleli okalawa ahorwaa waYona ni ahonkoha wiira unrupani? Wunwe ni unlepele nluku aa, noone toko nanoonela ikiriri wiira nihikhwe.
Wahoolo yaheerelana nrwee nipanke mwavi wiira nincuwele tipani uniwiihenre nenna nihusinna. Ni yahopanka mwavi ni wahomorela waYona.
Vano yahomwiirela: Unihimerye nenna va, uniwiiherenreni nenna nihusinna. Nteko aa phuvi? Unkhuma vayi? Ilapo aa phivi ni ikhapilani?
Yona ahaakhula: mi Heperewu, ni kinawoova Mwaneene Nluku, Nluku o wirimu, apattusile ipahari ni itthaya.
Vaavale atthu ale yahanca woova venci ni yahomwiirela: Isiyani yeela ipankile ela? Kontha atthu ale yahocuwela wiira atthawile wamiithoni waMwaneene Nluku, maana ahaahimyacera.
Yahomwiirelaca: Nuupankeke isiyani wiira ipahari imaale? Kontha nkhaya natepaca mpaharini.
Yona ahaakhula: Nkikuse ni nkivonyere mpaharini; ipahari inaahala umaala. Ni kinacuwela wiira nkhaya ula wile mwanlattu wa waka.
Vaavale anakalawa yaanvira yeettihaka ni ikuru caya apheelaka uphiya ukhopela. Nanso khayoonrye, kontha mpaharini nkhaya aantepa.
Vano yahaalepela Mwaneene Nluku a Yona, yiiraka: Contte Mwaneene Nluku, nhinihiye nikhwaka nlattu wa coonanara ca Yona, nhinootherye hi va ukhwa wawe kontha nyu Mwaneene Nluku nhopanka wootthuna winyu.
Vaavale yahonteesa Yona ni yahonvonyera mpaharini, ni nkhaya ahomaala ucaca.
Vano atthu ale yahoovaca venci Mwaneene Nluku, ni yahaavahaca itthuvo Mwaneene Nluku ciicammo yakhuluvelihaka waatthara.
Vano Yona nari mmirimani mohopa ahoswali aasukuruku Mwaneene Nluku
eeraka: Mmahuvihoni kihokhuwelela Mwaneene Nluku ni ahokaakhula. Mmirimani mahiye kihokhuwa, ni nyu nheewa ncu naka.
Nhokirihela mpaharini mapuro oowiisya cinenne ni kihokhala oorukureriya ni maasi ni mawimpi moolupale othene yaavira waculu waka.
Kihoona toko kihomwalaanihiya ni nyu. Akaacuwela wiira kaanhala woona tho inupa enyu ittakattifu.
Maasi othene yahokikhuneela mpaka ukittiya iphumu; ni ipahari yahokimirya ni makukhu o mpaharini yahokivilikelela mmuru.
Kihokhuruwela mpaka vathi waya myaako, mpaka ilapo ya atthu ookhwa ni mikhora caya cahokitthukela mommo. Nanso nyu nhokikumiha mapuro oowiisa, nuukivaha ukumi; Mwaneene Nluku; Nluku aka!
Upheelaka nnepa aka urimela mi kihowuupuwelelani nyu, Mwaneene Nluku, ni iswali caka cowela warinyu, mpaani mwinyu moottakattifihiya.
Ale anaswalela anluku oohimaana ahiyaka ikiriri ca Nluku.
Nanso mi kinaahala uwiipelani macipo oowunnuwihani ni wuuvahani itthuvo. Kinkopanka ile yookhuluvelihilyakani. Woopwa ukhuma wa Mwaneene Nluku.
Vano Mwaneene Nluku ahoolumana ihopa wiira inraphye Yona, ni Yona ahoraphenya ucenkweni.

Imaara yonayeeli nuulumo na Mwaneene Nluku nahowa waYona niiraka:
Wunwe ni urwee isitati yuulupale cinenne yo Ninive waahimyacere atthu o Ninive moolumo yuuhimyacenryaka.
Yona aheetthenkaca, ahonwa toko cakhanlyawe oohimeriya na Mwaneene Nluku. Ahorwaa uNinive. Ninive yaari isitati yuulupale cinenne yeettiya mahuku mararu uttupulaniha iriyariru.
Yona ahophiya uNinive. Aheetta nihuku nimoca akhalaka uwaahimyaca eeraka: Anhala mahuku arupayini Ninive ukwanyulaciya.
Vano atthu othene uNinive yahonkupali Nluku ni yahorukunusa mirima, ciicammo yaholeehana untthuka ramatani ukhuma atthu oolupale, mpaka acikani, othene yahommwaraca nakotto athoonyiheraka wiira ahorukunusa mirima caya.
Mwene o Ninive weewilyawe ni uyo ahonwa wahiceni wawe phurulaka ikuwo cawe cothene nuummwara nakotto phunkomaka wattuurani.
Ciicammo Mwene na ahooleli awe yahokumiha nlamulo nowahimyacera atthu othene unsitati wiira: Hikhale nohala ulya hata uwurya ukhuma atthu, inama coohuwiya, toko imope ni ikhontwaa, cihivahiye coolya ni maasi wala cihihuleliye cirwaka ulawiha coolya.
Atthu othene (ni inama cothene) amware nakotto anlapele Nluku ni ikuru, arukunuse mirima caya ni uhiya coopanka caya coonanara cothene.
Atthuna commo Nluku nahala unoonela ikiriri, ni urusiya wawe unahala uvira ni khaninhala ukhwa.
Nluku ahoona mananna cakhanlyaya oorukunusa mirima caya akhalaka oohiya coonanara caya ni Nluku khaahuvihile tho atthu ayo.
Nanso vaavale, Yona ahorusiya ni ahocaca.
Vano ahoswali akohaka Mwaneene Nluku toko co: We Mwaneene Nluku, mi akeenre kihinaaya ukhuma ilapo aka wiira phi yeeyo yahalaa upanka? Phimaana kipankaka mananna ootthawela uTarisi! Mi kahocuwela wiira we uri Nluku ookiriri ni oothunku, wiira we uri Nluku oopica ucaca, eemaani ni ooreera, ciicammo ukati wothene uri oolevelela.
Pahi, nyu Mwaneene Nluku, nkiive, kontha fatari kikhwe kihikhale nkumi.
Mwaneene Nluku ahaakhula: We Yona wookupali wiira uhaana isariya yoorusiya toko co?
Vaavale Yona ahokhuma uNinive, phurwaaka mphante unkhuma ncuwa ni ahonkoma. Vano ahoteka nrapattha ni ahonkoma wantthuucini waya, awehereryaka woona itthu yahala wiiranyaa nsitati mmo.
Vano Mwaneene Nluku ahomeliha mwamwiri wootthavelaca wiira Yona amumule wantthuucini ni atteeliye. Vaavale Yona ahotteeliya venci.
Nanso usa waya, ncuwa nipheelaka ukhuma, Nluku ahonruma mwaamunku wiira eeve mwamwiri uyo ni wahokhwa.
Wakhumilyaya ncuwa, Nluku ahowiha iphyoo yooviha cinenne ikhumaka unkela ncuwa. Yona ahociriphuwa nlattu wo nttukuttha ni ncuwa nampaha mmuruni mwawe. Vano ahopheela ukhwa ni aheera: Fatari kikhwe kihikhale nkumi.
Nluku ahonkoha Yona eeraka: Uhaamini urusiya nlattu wo yoola mwamwiri ula? Yona ahaakhula: Khweeli kihaana isariya yoorusiya toko co mpaka ukhwa.
Vano Mwaneene Nluku aheera: Ula mwamwiri ula wunnuwile uhiyu, ni uhiyu nkhwawe uyo wahokhwa. We khiiwo ipankenlyaa ula mwamwiri ula ni khawunnuwihile, vano unawoonela uthunku.
Mi ni isariya caka cothene akinlamuliya woonela ikiriri isitati yo Ninive, uryaya atthu enci oohicuwela itthu yooreera ni yoonanara woopwaha elufu iminya wosirini (120.000) ni inama cinci ciriwo?




































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































Wiipaceroni wa Nhupi Wooreera wa Yesu Kristu, Mwanawe Nluku.
Ohaantikhiya ni nnapiyu Isaya: Kimmonrumiha uhoolo wa mayanhupi aka, nohala wulokiherani iphiro.
Ncu ninkhuwa ntakhwani, Nlokihe iphiro ya Apwiya, mookole mittala.
Ciicale, Yohani Mpatisa phooneliye ntakhwani wiira eetthucihe opatiso wo urukunusa nrima wiira itaampi cileveleliye.
Yaanamwikamela atthu othene olapo ya Yutteya, na atthu ankhala uYerusalemu, ni yaanapatisiya ni ule umooloko Yorttani, alaphaka itaampi caya.
Yohani awara ikuwo yo mapururu onkamira, eethukelaka nyununi mo nrapala, yoolya awe yari mattettentte ni urawo wo ntakhwani.
Ni wowaalaka anaahimya coo: Uttuli waka mi nawa nkinaku rina ikuru impwaha yawaka, ni mi akimphwanela wooroma wiira kitthukule miripwe cokwakwatta cawe.
Mi kinawuupatisani ni maasi, nanso Ule naahala wuupatisani muNnepa Nttakattifu.
Waheranyaa, mahuku ale, Yesu awaaka ukhuma uNasaree yo Kalileya, mpaka upatisiya ni Yohani umooloko Yorttani.
Wakhumawe mmaasini mmo, ahoona irimu ihulyaka, ni Nnepa, woonnya toko ikhuntta inkhuruwelaka.
Ni ukhuma wirimu nineewiya ncu nnohimya: We uri Mwanaka oofentiya, nokiphela nrima.
Wahoolo Nnepa Nttakattifu wahoonrweha utakhwani, ni
ahokhala wonwo mahuku arupayini, ni ahothokociya ni Sotwani; ni cahawo wonwo inama cowoopiha, ni ancelo yahonkavihera.
Utthukiya wawe Yohani, Yesu akenle uKalileya, wahimerya atthu Nhupi Wooreera wa Nluku, eeraka:
Ukati uhophiya ni ciicammo Omwene wa Nluku uhophiya. Nrukunuseke nrima, nkupalelaka Nhupi Wooreera.
Aviraka nceresere ntthiya no Kalileya, ahomoona Simoni ni nhimaawe Anteree avonyeraka matthavi aya mpaharini mmo, nlattu yaari mayototha ihopa.
Yesu aheerela: Nkitthare Mi, ni Mi kimmowupankani mayowatotha atthu.
Ahiyaka nanaanoru matthavi aya, yahontthara Yesu.
Napwahile vakani, ahomoona Yakopu, mwana a Sepeteu ni nhimaawe Yohani, alokihaka nkalawani matthavi aya pweehanaka nananoru.
Ni ale yahonhiya Sepeteu athumwanaya ni mayanteko aya, yahontthara.
Yaanarwa uKafarnaum. Nihuku no Ntivela ahokela nnsinakokani, ni aheetthuciha atthu.
Na atthu othene yaanawumiya mwaano ni miitthuciho cawe, nlattu aheetthuciha toko ntthu nolamula ni khari toko mayowantikha.
Ahaawo nnsinakokani mmo ntthu arina nnepa woonanara, apacile ukhuwa:
We urinani ni hi, Yesu o Nasaree? Wawenle unikwanyulaca? Mi kihocuwela wiira uri Nttakattifu a Nluku.
Yesu ahonkuphula, eeraka: Omaale we, ni ukhume wantthu ula.
Vano, nnepa woonanara, unantathile ni ikuru, ukhuwacaka, wahokhuma wantthu ule.
Othene yahotikhinaca, mpaka ukohana ayayoru: Isiyani ila? Moone meetthuciho oonaanano, uromoliya ni nlamulo mpaka ulamulela minepa coonanara ni nnya cinamwiiwelela.
Ni ncina nawe nahorumannya nttetthe wothene, ilapo yo Kalileya.
Akhumaka unsinakoka ahokela mpani mwa Simoni ni Anteree, wamoca ni Yakopu ni Yohani.
Amaathyawe Simoni yaanawerenya wakorini, awerenyaka irutthu yothene, ni nananoru yahonhimerya ca iretta ila.
Attameryaka, Yesu ahaavarela ntata mpaka waawusa. Iretta yahaahiya, na ale yahopacera wakaavihera.
Ucoocilo, ncuwa ninakwattuwile, yahomwiihera aretta na ale yahoosiya ni nnepa woonanara,
na atthu othene owatthokoni yahothukumana wankhora.
Ahaavoniha aretta enci, yahoosiye ni coowerya, ni ahoomola minepa coonanara cinci; nanso khahiya wuulumaca minepa nlattu yaanancuwela.
Wicisuru, uhinasa ahoonwa ni ahokhuma; phurwaka ntakhwani wiira aswali.
Simoni, na ale yaari ni Yesu yahontthara.
Umphwanya waya, yahomwiirela: Atthu othene anawuphavelani.
Nanso ahaakhula: Nirwe ncoko nkina, itthoko co vakhiviru, neetthucihe wonwo, nlattu wo yela phikumenlyaka.
Ni ahorwaa ilapo yothene yo Kalileya, eetthucihaka mmasinakokani, ni oomolaka minepa coonanara.
Ntthu o makuttula ahonrwela Yesu ni ankhoromelaka ahonlepela: Watthunaka vale unawoorya ukivoniha.
Amoonelaka ikiriri, Yesu ahonthatela ntata mpaka unkwanya, eeraka: Kinatthuna, uvone.
Nananoru, makuttula yahonhiya, ni irutthu yahokhala toko khalayi.
Ni Yesu ahonleeha phunlakaka, ni moolumo ala:
Ukiiwe ahinhimerye ntthu itthu ila. Nanso upacera urwaa wamayasataka ni uvelelihe itthu ilamuliye ni Musa; nlattu wa atthu anhapihiya makuttula, wiira akhale saahiti aa.
Ule, mweeco, urwaa wawe ahopacera ulattula ni uhimya itthu yeeranele, mpaka Yesu uhoorya ukela ooniyaka mmawaani phukhalaka ntakhwani; na atthu olapo ile yaananrwela.
Anavinre mahuku vakani, ni Yesu naturuwile uKafarnaum wahorumanyaa wiira ri uwaani.
Yahothukumana atthu enci, mpaka uphunyana wankhora, ni Yesu aheetthuciha moolumo.
Vano yahomwiihera ntthu oowuntakyaa, akusiye na atthu acese.
Ukhala wiira khayoorya unkusa mpaka waryawe, nlattu wo mphwinko, yahokhunula nivatho nipuro naryawe Yesu, ni ciicale, anahunle iparo, yahokurusela nrepa naryawe ntthu oowuntakyaa.
Wowoona ukupali waya atthu ale, Yesu ahomwiirela ntthu oowuntakyaa: Mwanaka, itaampi caa ciholeveleliya.
Wonwo mweeco, yahoonkoma mayowantikha vakani yaakakaka munrimani mwaya:
Nlattuni, Ule uulumacaka co? Nakufuru. Noorya tipani ulevelela itaampi, hiri Nluku paahi?
Yesu, nanso acuwelaka moopuwelo aya mpaka ahaakoha: Nlattuni muupuwelaka ciicale munrimani mwinyu?
Itthu yootepa urika phivi, umwiirela oowuntakyaa, Itaampi caa ciholeveleliya, atthuna umwiirela, Wunwe, ukuse nrepa naa ni weette?
Vano paahi; wiira ncuwele wiira Mwanawe Pinattamu haana ikuru vathiva yolevelela itaampi,
kinawuulamula amwaacaka ntthu oowuntakyaa ukuse nrepa naa ni urwee uwaanyaa.
Ntthu ule ahoonwa, ahokusa nrepa nawe ni ahokhuma ooniyaka na atthu ale othene, mpaka othene wumiya mwaano, ni yaananttottopela Nluku yiiraka: Khaninoona itthu co nikhalakaru.
Imaara ikina tho ahokhumela vate mphante wo ipharyaa; ni mphwinko wa atthu othene wahontthara, Ule eetthucihaka.
Nanso aviraka uyo ahomoona Levi, mwanawe Alfeu nonkomile inupa yowaakheleliya nsoko, ni ahomwiirela: We, ukitthare Mi. Ni Levi ahonwa anttharaka Yesu.
Nari wamoca, itthoko ya Levi, mayoliviha nsoko enci na atthu ookosakosa yahoonkomaca wameeca wamoca ni Yesu ni uwiitthuca awe, nlattu khayaamala urunwa atthu yaantthara.
Mayowantikha yanrumelelihana ni mafarisi, amoonaka ulya na atthu ookosakosa ni mayoliviha nsoko, yaheerela uwiitthuca awe: Nlattuni, nalya na atthu ookosakosa?
Yesu eewaka cothene ahaakhula: Kahiwena akumi phimmwavya tothoro, nanso, aretta. Mi akiwenle weehana atthu aattakattifu, nanso atthu ookosakosa.
Owiitthuca a Yohani ni mafarisi yaantthuka, yahowa unkoha Yesu: Owiitthuca a Yohani ni mafarisi anatthuka ni uwiitthuca aa ahitthukaka isiyani?
Yesu ahaakhula: Asimpwana awe mayothela anawoorya utthuka, mayothela nari na ale? Mahuku othene ankhalaya wamoca ni mayothela khanoorya utthuka.
Anaahala uphiya mahuku anhalaya waakhiya mayothela, vano phankelaya utthuka.
Khaawo neesera icaapha yonaanano ikuwoni yookhalayi, nlattu icaapha yonaanano inatepereriha mphantte wookhalayi, ni nikhwata ninatepa wunnuwa.
Ni khaawo nohela ivinyu yonaanano mmapikani ookhalayi, ahelaka vale, ivinyu inaahala upwesa mapika ookhalayi, ni ivinyu inarihakyaa wamoca ni mapika. Nanso ivinyu yonaanano inheliya mmapikani oonaanano.
Nihuku nimoca no ntivela Yesu anavira mmamattani na owiitthuca awe. Yeettaka mphironi, owitthuca awe yahoonta ncasi.
Mafarisi yahontthara, yiiraka: Nkoona, nlattuni ale apankaka itthu yowatelihiya upanka nihuku no ntivela?
Ahaakhula: Khannasoma itthu yapankilyawe Taviti, wammoonlyawe itala, ule na atthu yarinawe?
Wakenlyawe inupa ya Nluku, ukati wa mayasataka muulupale Apiyatari, ni walilyawe mikatthe coottakattifihiya coolamuliya ulya mayasataka paahi, ni ahaavaha atthu yarinawe?
Ni ahopwahera: Ntivela nihopankeliya ntthu, ni kahiwena ntthu phipankeliye ntivela.
Mwanawe Pinattamu phi mwaneene ntivela.
Yesu ahokela tho nnsinakokani. Ahokhala wonwo ntthu oonririya ntata.
Vano ale yaananhottela wiira amoone ammoonihaka nihuku no ntivela wiira ankasari.
Yesu ahonhimerya ntthu arina ntata noonririya: Wunwe ni uwe iriyari ila va.
Wahoolo ahaakoha: Inoleveliya, nihuku no Ntivela, upanka itthu yooreera atthuna itthu yoonanara, woopola ukumi atthuna uhiya uharipwyaka? Ale yahomaalaca.
Vano, awehaka ni urusiya, ni ummweryaka nrima nlattu woturumala mirima caya, ahomwiirela ntthu: Wookole ntata. Ahookola ntata ni nna nahovona.
Wakhumilyaya, mafarisi yahothukumana na aHerotiyano wiira avaanele mamwiivelo.
Yesu ahorwaa untthiyani na owiitthuca awe, atthariyaka ni mphwinko muulupale wakhuma uKalileya, ni Yutteya,
uYerusalemu, uItumeya, ukhopela Yorttani, ni nceresere Tiro ni Sittoniya. Ahophwanyinya ni mphwinko muulupale, wewiilyaya itthu yaapankawe.
Ahaahimerya owiitthuca awe, anlokihere ikalawa yaankani, wiira hiphunyererihiye ni mphwinko uyo.
Woona ahaavoniha atthu enci, ni nlattu weetthu ila, ale yanawaaninya ni ikwerere wiira ankwanye.
Minepa coonanara, wamoonaya, caanankhoromela wamiithoni wawe ni caanakhuwa: We uri Mwana a Nluku.
Ule nanso anawaateliha wiira ahicuwelihe.
Wahoolo ahowela mmwaakoni, ni aheehana ale yatthunyawe, na ale yahomwaattamerya.
Ahaathanla khumi na eeli phwaavahaka ncina na amitthenka wiira yakhaleke ni Uyo, ni aarume, wiitthuciha,
ni yaphwanyeke ikuru yo woomola minepa coonanara.
Ahaathanla khumi na eeli ala: Simoni, ammahilyawe ncina na Peturu,
Yakopu, mwanawe Sepetteu, ni Yohani nhimaawe Yakopu, ammahilyawe ncina Powanerce, manaaya asaana utari;
Anteree, Filipe, Partimeu, Mateu, Tomee, Yakopu mwanawe Alfeu, Tateu, Simoni Selote,
ni Yutta Iskariyoti, anthumihile Yesu.
Waphilyaya uwaani, mphwinko wa atthu wahothukumana tho, mpaka wahinoryaya ulya.
Ni amawaawe, wiiwawaya itthu ila, yahokhuma wiira ammare, nlattu yeeriya: Hoolociya.
Ni mayowantikha, yakhuruwenle o Yerusalemu yahohimya: Hovariya ni Peelsepu. Ni thotho. Nawoomola minepa coonanara ni ikuru ca mwene a minepa coonanara.
Vano Yesu aheehana ni wahimerya mmalikaniheroni: Noorya cani, Sotwani umoomola Sotwani?
Omwene wakawaniyaka, omwene ule khunoorya ukhala.
ni inupa yakawanihiyaka, inupa ile khinoorya ukhala.
Phimaana, akhalaka Sotwani eecanihaka ikhotto mwaneene eekawanihaka, ni khanoorya ukhala tho, homala.
Khaawo noorya ukela inupa ya ntthu ookhomaala ni unhukhela mihakhu cawe woohipaca ummara phooryaka unhukhela wahoolo.
Khweeli kinawuhimeryani: Itaampi cothene ni ikufuru cothene cinkhala coromoliya na atthu, cothene cimmoleveleliya,
nanso, ntthu nohala ukufuru Nnepa Nttakattifu khammwa uleveleliyaka akhalakaru; nowookhala ni itaampi awe mahuku othene.
Ahaahimerya itthu ila nlattu yahimenrye: Ule navariya ni nnepa woonanara.
Vano yahophiya anumwane na asihimaawe, ni anemenle utaa, yahaaruma atthu umwihana.
Mphwinko wa atthu wahoonkoma ntotho wawe, atthu yahonhimerya: Ahaawo vate anumwana na asihimaa, anawuphavela.
Ahaakhula: Amanyi ni asihimaaka phapani?
Ni athetulaka miitho mwaatthu ale yanrukurenrye, aheera: Ala pha manyi na asihimaaka.
Ntthu nopanka utthuna wawe Nluku, ule phi nhimaaka, mwanrokoraka ni amanyi.
Ahopacera tho wiitthuciha nceresere ntthiya. Mphwinko muulupale wahothukumana ntotho wawe, phimaana ahowela nkalawani ni ahoonkoma mmwe, phukhalaka mphwinko woonene.
Anaweetthuciha citthu cinci mmalikaniheroni ni anawahimerya mmeetthucihoni mwawe:
Mmiriyane. Mayowaala ahokhuma arwaka uwaalani.
Waalaawe, ipyo ikina yahomorela nceresere iphiro ni yahowaca asanuni, yaholya.
Ipyo ikina yahomorela wakokotthoni, wonwo wahakhanle itthaya yinci, khipicile umela nlattu itthaya khayaakenle uttayi.
Nanso, ncuwa, ukhuma waya, yahopahiya, nlattu wohikhalana itthaya yinci mitithari cahooma.
Ikina yahomorela wamwiwani, ni miwa cahoonuwa, cahomirya ipyo ni khayeemile.
Ikina yahomorela itthaya yooreera ni yunuwaka, ni inarenre, yaheema, ni wuncereriya mpaka ukhala talathini, sitiini ni iminya khila ipyo.
Ni ahopwahera eeraka: Urina manyaru uwiwelela, eeweke.
Nahanle veekha, atthu yanrukurerya wamoca ni owiitthuca awe khumi na eeli yahonkoha manaaya nlikanihero nne.
Ahaakhula: Nyu nhovahiya ucuwelaca ikano yo omwene wa Nluku, nanso, atthu ari utaa citthu cothene anahimeriya ni malikanihero,
wiira yoonaka, yoone, ni ahicuwelele; yiiwaka, yiiwe, ni ahiiwehe wiira ahirukunuse mirima, aleveleliyaka itaampi caya.
Ni ahopwahera: Khanneeweeha manaaya nlikanihero nna? Nnohala mweeco, wiitthuca cani malikanihero makina ayo?
Mayowaala nawaala nuulumo,
ari nceresere iphiro, pha ale yahimerye nuulumo, aneewile nuulumo. Sotwani nawa waatamiha nuulumo naaliye.
Ciicammo, ale yaakhenle ipyo mapuro ookokoottho, pha ale yiinre aneewile nuulumo, woohipica anawaakhelela ni nrima wootteeliya,
nanso kharina mitithari mwaale, khankhala nthiti ni yawaaka mahuviho, atthuna yomolanihaciyaka nlattu wo nuulumo, wohipica anattittha.
Ahaawo akina, anaakhela nuulumo mapuro o miiwa. Ala anawiiwa nuulumo,
nanso nlattu woramela itthu yo nttuniyani, wothokociya ni mihakhu ni citthu cikina cinonlelaya, cinakela munrimani mwaya anattitthiha nuulumo ni khaneema.
Atthu anakhela nuulumo itthaya yooreera pha ale aneewa nuulumo, anaakhelela, aneewa mpaka wiima ni wincereriya talathini, sitiini ni iminya khila ipyo.
Ahaahimerya tho: Pooti inaweesiya isamaninya nhina mwaya itthuttu atthuna vathi waya nkori? Keera ineesiya waculu mmutto?
Nlattu khiiwo yovithiya ihinhala wooneleliya, ni khiiwo yowipithya ihinhala ukhumela woonene.
Ntthu akhalanaka manyaru oowiiwelela, eeweke!
Ni ahopwahera: Mmiriyaneke ratta itthu ineewenyu. Nnowophimiya ni itthuttu inhalenyu uphimela, ni thotho nnowowincereriya.
Vano ntthu rina, nowowuncereriya, ni ntthu hirina, nowowaakhiya, mpaka citthu cirinawe.
Ni anawiira: Omwene wa Nluku uri toko ntthu avonyenre ipyo awe vathi.
Arupe, unwe, uhiyu ni uthana, ipyo inamela ni inawunuwa, ule woohicuwela cani.
Itthaya inavaha veekhaya, woopacera ntathi, wahoolo ncasi, ni umwiisoni ncasi nocara meele.
Ni yowiima yattokotthaka, naahepha nlattu wahophiya ukati woohephiya.
Vano aheera: Ninhala ulikanihera ni isiyani omwene wa Nluku? Atthuna ninhala utaphulela ni nlikaniheroni?
Uri toko inuku yo nrale, ineera inaliye vathi, iri yootepa uyeva mweenuku cothene;
nanso, yaaliyakaru, inawunuwa, inathatuwa mwiri muulupale woopwaha miri co mmattani ni inamwarya miritta caya mpaka asanuni o wirimu woorya uteka ipuuru muntthucini mwaya.
Ni malikanihero menci toko ala Yesu anaweetthuciha nuulumo, toko woonawe wiira anawiiweha.
Khoolumacera woohikhala ni malikanihero; nanso uyo anawataphulela cothene owiitthuca awe anari veekhaya.
Nihuku nne, unaripenle, ahaahimerya: Nrwee nilapuwele ukhopela.
Ahiyaka miphwinko, owiitthuca yahonkusa, toko caryawe nkalawani, ni cahommelela ikalawa cikina.
Vano ahokhumelela naphuvo muulupale ophyoo ni mawiimpi yanawicattakanihaca ni ikalawa mpaka yahala vakani ucara maasi.
Yesu, nari mphantte wottuli wokalawa, anarupa naphitenrye nsawu.
Yahoommusa ni umwiirela: Mwalimu, khunoona wiira ninakumpwela? Unwaka, aholamulela iphyoo ni aheerela ipahari: Imaale, ihittinke! Iphyoo yahomaala, ni ipahari yothene yaheera riya-riya.
Wahoolo ahaahimerya: Nlattuni nkhalaka atthu oowoova osilili? Nhikupaliki?
Yanawoova venci ni yaanahimeryana: Tipani Yoola? Hata iphyoo, ni ipahari cinamwiiwelela?
Yahophiya nikhopela nikhwaya ntthiya, ilapo yo Yeraseno.
Yesu nalapuwile ahosiceriya ni ntthu aakhuma umahiye, avariye ni nnepa woonanara.
Akhala umahiye, ni khaawo oorya ummara, mena vakani untthuka ni unyolo,
nlattu imaara cinci ahotthukiya ni unyolo mpaka wuntakaca unyolo ni unyakataca ikatiyato; khaawo oorya ummoniha.
Mahuku othene anaweetta, uthana ni uhiyu mmarekhano ni mmyaakoni, akhuwaka ni eerakalihaka ni maluku.
Amoonaka Yesu uttayi, ahotthimakaca ni ahonkhoromela ni
ahokhuwa ni ncu nowirunya: Nyu nrinani ni miyano, Yesu Mwana a Nluku Ooculu. Nhikoopopihe!
Ni khweeli, Yesu anamwiirela: Ukhume mwantthuni mu, nnepa woohiloka.
Wahoolo ahonkoha: Ncina naa tipani? Ahaakhula: Mphwinko phi ncina naka, nlattu niri enci.
Ni yahonlepela ankhanyererihaka wiira ahomoliye nttetthe ule.
Caanalya vano ikuluwe nceresere mwaako,
ni minepa coonanara cahonlepela Yesu: Nnilamulele nakele nkuluweni mmwe.
Yesu ahorumelela, ni nenna nna minepa coonanara cahokhuma wantthuni ni cahokela nkuluweni, ni nikhoto nne nari toko ikuluwe elufu piili (2000) naheevonyera muntthiyani ni nahottittha.
Ahakheli yahotthawa ni yahovira alattulaka mmawaani; na atthu enci yahowa woona itthu yeeranele.
Waphiyaya nipuro naryawe Yesu, yahomoona ntthu avariye ni minepa coonanara noonkomile, nawanre ni nakhalanne ankhili, ni yahoova.
Asaahiti a ntthu oovariya ni minepa coonanara ni itthu yeranele ni ikuluwe yahottonka itthu yeranele.
Vano yahoonlepela Yesu wiira athame ilapo aya.
Yesu ahoturuwela okalawani; ni ntthu avariye ni minepa
Yesu khantthunihenre, nanso ahomwiirela: Urwee uwaanyaa, wamawaa ni wattonkacere citthu cothene cupankenlyaya Apwiya, ni toko ciwoonenlyaya ikiriri.
Ahokhuma wonwo, ni ahopacera uTekapoli itthu yampankenlyawe Yesu, na atthu othene yahotikhinaca.
Yesu nalapuwile ntthiya ni ikalawa, ni neemenle nceresere ntthiya wahothukumana mphwinko muulupale wa atthu.
Ahophiya vano muulupale o nsinakoka, eehaninya Cayro, ni umoona wawe Yesu, ahonkhoromela,
ni ahonlepela ankhanyererihaka: Mwanaka mwanthiyana hanle vakani ukhwa; uwe unthatele matata akhale nkumi.
Yesu ahommeleela phutthariyaka ni mphwinko muulupale wamphunyereriha.
Vano, nthiyana mmoca awuva iphome iyakha khumi na piili,
ni anaweettihiya venci mmatatani mwaya mayoovoniha enci, ni arihile mihakhu cawe cothene, nanso woohiphwanya nafasi, hata iretta awe yaanavira etepacaka.
Neewile ca Yesu, ahotakaneela ni mphwinko, ni awaaka uttuli wawe ahonkwanya nihancu nawe;
aheecirela mweeco: Mena kakwanyaru cowara cawe, kimmovona.
Nananoru iphome yaheemela, ni ahoona mwirutthuni mwawe wiira ikwerere awe ihovona.
Nenna nna, Yesu, oonaka wiira ikuru awe yahokhuma mwirutthuni mwawe, ahorukunuwela mphwinko akohaka: Kikwanyile tipani?
Owiitthuca awe yahomwiirela: Unawoona wiira miphwinko cinawuphunyereriha miphantte cothene, ni unakoha: Akikwanyile tipani?
Nanso Yesu ahoweha nceresere aphavelaka umoona ntthu apankile itthu ile.
Vano nthiyana ahocuwela ciheeranya mwirutthuni mwawe oovaka ni athukumelaka ahokhuma ahonkhoromela Yesu ni ahonhimerya citthu cothene.
Ni ule ahomwiirela: Mwanaka, ukupali waa uhowoopola. Urwee ni nnema ni uvone ikwerere aa.
Yesu uulumacaka ninlelo yahowa atthu akina akhumaka inupa awe muulupale o nsinakoka phwiiraka: Mwana aa hokhwa.
Yesu, nanso, neewile moolumo ale, ahomwiirela muulupale o nsinakoka: Uhituthuwe, ukupaliki paahi.
Ahaateliha othene wiira: Hikivelele ntthu, hikhanle Peturu, Yakopu ni Yohani, nhimaawe Yakopu.
Uphiya waya uwaanyawe muulupale o nsinakoka, Yesu aheewa ikuttho yuulupale ya atthu enci yunlaka mpani.
Ni akelaka, ahaahimerya: Ikuttho ila wunla nwe isiyani? Mwana uyo kakhwile, narupa paahi.
Nanso atthu ale yaananthyaa, Yesu ahaakumihera utaa atthu ale othene ni aakusaka athumwane na anumwane, na ale yammelenle, yahokela mpani mwataleliye mwanamwane.
Ni ammaraka ntata, aheera: Mwanaka kinawulamulela, wunwe.
Nananoru mwanamwane ahoonwa ni ahopacera weetta, ari mweeco, ni iyaakha khumi na piili. Othene yahooma mwaano.
Yesu ahaalepela wiira itthu ile ihicuweliye ni ntthu, ni aholamula uvahiya yoolya mwanthiyana.
Ukhuma wawe wenwe, ahorwaa wamoca ni owiitthuca awe.
Nihuku no ntivela ahopacera wiitthuciha nnsinakoka na atthu enci yamwiiwa, wanawooma mwaano ni yaanahimya: Inonkhuma vayi itthu ila ni ucuwelani uno uvahiyawe uno? Cinopankya cani cotikineeha nya ni ntata nawe?
Kahi nkarapintero, mwanawe Mariya, ni nhimaawe Yakopu, Yosefi, Yutta ni Simoni? Ni asirokorawe khari ni hi? Yahoviruwaca.
Yesu aheerela: Namilohi notarawiya uwaanyawe paahi, waama wawe ni wapuwani wawe.
Ni wonwo khoonrye upanka cotikineeha hata mena. Ahaavooniha aretta vakani paahi, athatelaka matata.
Ahotikhinaca uhikupali waatthu ale. Vano ahoviravira itthoko co wattamana eetthucihaka wonwo.
Aheehana khumi na eeli, ni ahopacera waruma eeli eeli, ni ahaavaha ikuru yolamulela minepa coonanara.
Ahaalamulela wiira ahikuse itthu yootthumiri ni iphiro, wala nkatthe, wala nrupa, mena nsurukhu nyununi, akuse ikopo paahi.
Aware ikwakwatta ni ahiwye ihancu piili.
Ni ahaahimerya tho: Mwakelaka inupa, nkhale wonwo mpaka wunwa nipuro nno.
Ni mwahaakheleliyeke nipuro nno, na atthu ale yahiwiwekeni, woothama vale, nkukutthe ntthupi no manyaa enyu, wiira ikhale itthu inthoonyera mirima caya atthu ale.
Amitthenka yahorwaca ni yahaalaka atthu oottharuwela itaampi.
Yahoomola minepa coonanara ciinci, yahaattikitthela ni makhura aretta enci mpaka waavoniha.
Mwene Heroti aheewa cuulumaceriyaka ca Yesu, nanruma ncina nawe ni anawiira: Ula phi Yohani Mpatisa oonwelenle mwaatthu ookhwa, phimaana cinawithoonyera mwa ule ikuru coopanka cotikhineeha.
Akina yaanawiira: Phi Eliya. Akina yanalipihera: Ri nnapiyu toko anapiyu akina.
Heroti nanso, wowiiwa itthu ila anahimya eeraka: Yohani unthikinlyaka isiko phunwelenle.
Khweeli, Heroti phalamunle utthukiya Yohani ni weesiya nkalaposo, nlattu wa Herotiyata, amwaarawe Filipe nhimaawe, anthenlyawe.
Nlattu Yohani anamwiirela Heroti: Khunleveliya ukhalana amwaarawe nhimaa.
Herotiyata hopophela nreca ni anatthuna umwiiva, nanso khoorya,
nlattu Heroti anamoova Yohani ni, acuwelaka wiira ari ntthu ooloka ni nttakattifu, anamwaakhiha; wamwiiwawe anasanka, nanso anammiriyana ni uciveliya.
Nanso nahophiya nihuku nooreera, Heroti wopuwelenlyawe nihuku nayariyawe ahophavela yoolya yinci yowaavaha oolupale owahano, oolupale anakhotto, ni mamwene o Kalileya.
Nakenle wiina mwana nthiyana a Herotiyata wahoncivela Heroti na atthu yaalattuliye. Mwene ahomwiirela mwali: Ukilepele itthu phi itthu intthunaa ni mi kimmowuvaha.
Ni ahopwahera: Kimmowuvaha itthu yothene inhalaa ukilepela hata ukhalaka mwanusu omwene aka.
Mwali ahokhuma waakoha anumwane wiira: Kilepele isiyani? Ala yahaakhula: Muru wa Yohani Mpatisa.
Mwali akelaka tho nenna nna, ahonlepela mwene, eeraka: Kintthuna uvahiya nananoru, unaheliye munttiisini muru wa Yohani Mpatisa.
Mwene ahotuthuwa, nanso nlattu woolupela wawe ni, nlattu waatthu yaalatuliye, khathunne unthuwa.
Nenna nna ahonlamulela mayorontta uwiha muru wa Yohani. Mayorontta ahorwaa nkalaposo ni ahothikila isiko ya Yohani,
ni wahoolo ahowiha muru munttiisini mpaka ummaha mwali, ni ula ahaavaha anumwane.
Ucuwela waya itthu ila owiitthuca a Yohani, yahokusa nrutthu ni yahothipela mmahiyeni.
Amitthenka yahothukumana wa Yesu ni yahonttonkacera citthu cothene capankilyaya ni citthu cihilyaya.
Ni Yesu ahaahimerya: Mmweeke, nirwe nipuro nowiipithyaa ni mmumule vakani, nlattu yaari enci yaarwa ni yaawa mpaka uhikhalana ukati woolya.
Vano yahorwaa ni ikalawa nipuro nowiipithyaa nahaariwo hata ntthu.
Yoonaka arwaka, enci yahocuwela ukitthu unkelaya. Ni mmatthokoni mothene yahorwaa, yeetaka vathi, nipuro nne, ni yahophiya nraci.
Wakhuruwawe nkalawani, Yesu ahoona mphwinko muulupale ni ahoonela ikiriri, nlattu yaari toko ikhontwaa cohikhalana nhaakheli. Vano ahopacera weetthuciha ukati mwinci.
Ncuwa wakelaya utthekuwa, owiitthuca awe yahomwattamerya nuunhimerya: Nipuro nna niri toko mwini, ni ncuwa notthekuwa.
Walamulele urwaa mmawaani ni mmatthokoni cowattamana wiira yathume yoolya.
Ahaakhula: Mwaavahe nyenyu wa yoolya. Na ale yahonhimerya: Wothuma mikatthe cowavaha atthu ale othene, nimphavela ncurukhu iminya piili.
Yesu ahopwahera: Nhaana mikatthe mikavi? Nrwee moone. Anakohile atthu, yahaakhula: Mikatthe mithanu ni ihopa piili.
Ahaalamulela wonkomiha atthu vakani khila nipuro mmalasini makithi.
Ni yaanawunkoma khila ipuwa atthu iminya ni ipuwa ikhwawe atthu hansini.
