Vano ahokusa mikatthe mithanu ni ihopa piili ni, aweehaka wirimu, ahosukurela. Ahomyaniha mikatthe ni ahaavaha owiitthuca awe wiira yakawele atthu. Ni ahaakawela ihopa piili,
na atthu ale yaholya mpaka uvona.
Ni ahocariha tho itthuttu khumi na piili ikalakathela cahanle co mikatthe ni co ihopa.
Vano yalilyayo mikatthe nye yaari atthu elufu thanu.
Nananoru ahaakhanyereriha owiitthuca awe ukela nkalawani nuulapuwela nikhopela nikhwawe no Petsayita; mwaneene alaseraka mphwinko.
Analasenre mphwinko ule, ahowela umwakoni, uswali.
Wiila waya, ikalawa yari iriyari ntthiya, ni Yesu aheemela nceresere veekhawe.
Woona wawe wiira yahoocya weettiha ikalawa nlattu iphyoo yanavirikana, aheekamela weeraka mapikoosa, eettaka wamaasini mpaka utthuna uhapuwa.
Nanso owiitthuca yamoonaka weetta wamaasini yahopuwela wiira nnepa, ni yahokhuwa.
Othene mweeco yahomoona ni yahotuthuwa. Mwaneene nanso aholumacera, eeraka: Mpise nrima, phi mi, nhoove!
Wahoolo, ahokela nkalawani mwariyaya, ni iphyoo yahowukuwa. Othene yanawoova venci.
Khayeewehile ni nlelo itthu yeranele ni mikatthe nye nlattu woolipa mirima caya.
Analapuwenle ukhopela, ahophiya ilapo yo Yenesare ni ahovonyera vathi nankura.
Anakhumile nkalawani, atthu uwonwo yahoncuwela.
Yahophiya atthu enci olapo ile ni yahopacera wawiha aretta mmarepani ni aharweha nipuro nacuwenlyaya wiira phiryawe.
Mmatthokoni makani, itthoko cuulupale ni mmawaani, nipuro phi nipuro nakelawe yanaweesiya aretta mparaparani ni yahoonlepela wiira aleve mena ukwanyiya nlempe no nhancu awe. Na atthu othene yankwanya yanavona.
Mayowantikha ni mafarisi akina, akhumaka o Yerusalemu, yahothukumana ntotho wawe Yesu.
Yahoona wiira owiitthuca awe akina yanalya nkatthe ni matata oohirya, manaaya woohinyawa.
Mafarisi ni Ayutta othene khanlya woohinyawa ratta ratta, toko calemalenlyaya atthu ookhalayi.
Waturuwaya uparasa, khayalya ihinaya unyawa; ni cihaawo tho citthu cinci cikina cimpankaya attharaka citthu cookhalayi, toko urapiha ikahi, myaapu, ni myaapu co ncukhuma ni mikori.
Yahonkoha vano, mafarisi ni mayowantikha: Owiitthuca aa ahiwelelaka citthu cookhalayi, alyaka ahinyawile, isiyani?
Yesu ahaakhula: Hohimya ratta nnapiyu Isayiya, awacakani nyu, atthu o mirima miili, toko cantikhiyaya: Mphwinko ula unakittitthimiha ni mattere, nanso nrima aya unkhala uttayi waka.
Anakilapela vathiru, ni yeetthucihaka malamulo a atthu paahi.
Ahiyaka nlamulo na Nluku, phuttharaka coohiyerana ca atthu, toko urapiha myaapu ni ikahi ni citthu cinci colikana nnya.
Ni aheerela: Nnahiya ntteeliyaka nlamulo na Nluku wiira nthareke coohiyerana cinyu.
Musa, mweeco, heera: Wattittimihe athumwanaa na anumwanaa; ni Ntthu nohala walapha athumwane na anumwane attarusiye ni eeviye.
Nyu nanso nneera: Ntthu nohala wahimerya athumwane atthuna anumwane: Itthu yahalaka wuvahani nyuva phi ila 'korpan' manaaya, itthu yoovahiya Apwiya.
Ciicammo khanonhiyera ntthu itthu yowapankela athumwane atthuna anumwane,
mmalihaka ciicammo nuulumo na Nluku nlattu wo coohiyerana cookhalayi cinvahenyu. Ni napanka citthu cinci toko nnya.
Eehanaka tho mphwinko, Yesu anawahimerya: Nkiviriyane othene, ni mwavye wiiweha.
Khiiwo iri utaa wawe ntthu, ineera inakenle nhina mwawe, phoorya untatusa iharamu; nanso inkhuma muntthuni, ila phinoorya untatusa iharamu.
Ntthu urina manyaru uwiiwelela, eewe!
Wakenlyawe mpaani, nahile mphwinko, owiitthuca awe yahonkoha manaaya nlikanihero nna.
Ahaakhula: Nyu ciicammo khaneeweha? Khannocuwela wiira, citthu cothene co utaa cinkela muntthuni, khacinoorya untatusa iharamu,
nlattu khinkela munrimani, nanso nnapwiipwini mwawe, ni wahoolo inakhumela wanipuroni waya? Ciicale anahimya wiira coolya cothene cooreera.
Ni ahohimya tho: Itthu inkhuma muntthuni, yeeyo phinontatusa iharamu.
Nlattu nhina nrima wantthu phinkhumaya moopuwelo oonanara: ulavalava, wiinya, wiiva,
uraruwa, isoyo, wunlela coonanara, uthepya, uhilemeliha irutthu, urama, ukufuru, wiicona, uhiwacera itthu yomaana.
Citthu nnye cothene coonanara cinkhuma nhina, ni cinantatusa ntthu nharamu.
Akhoolaka nipuro nne, ahorwaa nttetthe wo Tiro ni wo Sittoniya. Ahokela mpani ni khatthuna wiira acuweliye ni ntthu, nanso khoonrye wiipitha.
Vano wohipica nthiyana arina mwanawe mwanthiyana avariye ni nnepa woonanara weewilyawe wuulumaciya ca Yesu, ahowa unkhoromela wamettoni wawe.
Ari nthiyana nsenci, olapo yo Siriya-Fenisiya, ni ananlepela wiira oomole ncini wa mwanawe.
Ahaakhula: Wareerihe, toko, avone oopacera asaana; woona khavanreera ukusa nkatthe wa asaana ni warihela asilapwa!
Ale mweeco, yahomwakhula: Khweeli, Pwiya, nanso hata asilapwa analya vathivaya meeca coolya ca asaana cimmora-mora.
Yesu ahomwiirela: Nlattu wo nuulumo nna, urweke, ncini nookhuma mwa mwanaa.
Ahoturuwela uwaani ni ahomphwanya mwamhima nonkomile wakorini. Ncini nahonhiya.
Nakhumile tho nttetthe wo Tiro, ahowela o Sittoniya, mpaka ntthiya no Kalileya, aphulanihaka nttetthe wo Kapole.
Yahomwiihera ntthu oohiwa, ni wanrikarikela wuulumaca, ni yahonlepela wiira anthatele ntata.
Yesu antamihaka waatthuni ahonhela makokho mmanyaruni ahonsuwela ni ukwanya nlimi ni isene.
Ni awusaka miitho wirimu ahohihimerya, eeraka: 'Effatha' manaaya 'wiihule.'
Manyaru yahonhulya namarweele, nlimi nawe nahontthukuwa ni ahopacera wuuluma ratta.
Yesu aheera wiira hinhimerye ntthu itthu yeraneele, nanso waatepawe waateliha, phaatepaya umwarusela.
Atikhinacaka, yaanawiira: Cothene nopanka cotikhineeha, heewiha atthu uhiwa, ni wuulumaciha atthu oohuulumaca.
Mahuku ale, ukhala wiira wahotthukumana tho mphwinko muulupale na atthu khayarina yoolya, Yesu aheehana owiitthuca awe ni ahaahimerya:
Ukiiriha ihaaya mphwinko ula. Nna va ahovira mahuku mararu anari ni mi ni kharina yoolya.
Kaalaseraka ciicale woohilyetthu, wiira arwe mmwanyaya anaahala ukhwa mahile ni iphiro, kontha akina akhumile uttayi.
Owiitthuca awe yahomwaakhula: Nohala woorya cani ntthu waaliha nkatthe, watakhwani va?
Nanso ahaakoha: Nrina mikatthe mikavi? Yahaakhula: Mithanu na miili.
Aholamula wiira atthu yunkome vathi. Ni, akusaka mikatthe mithanu na miili, ahoreeriha, ahomyaniha ni ahaavaha owiitthuca awe, wiira yakawele na ale yahaakawela atthu.
Yahaana tho asihopa vakani. Ahoreeriha ni aholamula wiira yaakawele.
Yaholya mpaka urupala, ni ikalakathela cahanle nyo owiitthuca awe yahottottela itthuttu thanu na piili.
Atthu ale yaari elufu cese (4000). Wahoolo ahaalasera.
Ni awelaka vano nkalawani ni owiitthuca awe, ahorwaa mittetthe co Talmanuta.
Yahowa mafarisi yapacenre unyakulihana ni Yesu ni woontteha yahoonlepela ikanyero yo wirimu.
Yesu ahihimeryaka ni nrima wothene, aheera: Nlattuni weesiyani nihimo nna ninalepelela ikanyero? Khweeli kinawuhimeryani wiira nihimo nna khaninhala uvahiya ikanyero hata vakani.
Ni aahiyaka, ahokela nkalawani, mpaka ulapuwela ikhopela ikina.
Owiitthuca yaholiyala uwya mikatthe, ni nkalawani khayaarina tho waari nkatthe mmoca paahi.
Yesu aheerela: Moone, nkhale miitho mmwehaka ratta miropo co mafarisi ni miropo ca Heroti.
Na ale yahopacera uvanyihana, yoopuwelaka wiira waaciye uhikhalana nkatthe.
Yesu nanso, weewilyawe moolumo ale, ahaahimerya: Nlattu isiyani moopelaka mwaha o itthu yohikhalana nkatthe? Nanlelo khannahelelela ni khanneeweha? Nri ni nrima woturumala.
Nhaana miitho ni khannoona? Nhana manyaru nanso kanneewa ni khannopuwela.
Itthuttu kavi coocara ni coohala caattottenlenyu, wamyanihilyaka mikatthe mithanu kaakawelaka atthu elufu thanu? Yahaakhula: Khumi na piili.
Ni wamyanihilyaka mikatthe saapa pwaavahaka atthu elufu cese, mwacarihile itthuttu kavi cokalakathela co mikatthe? Yahaakhula: Saapa.
Ni anaweerela: Nanlelo khanneewa?
Yesu ni owiitthuca awe yahophiya o Petsayita ni yahomwiihera ntthu oohoona, anlepelaka wiira ankwanye.
Ahommarela ntata ntthu oohoona ni ahonrweha nceresere itthoko, ahonhela isenye mmithoni mwawe, ahonthatela matata nuunkoha: Unawoonaka itthu?
Ule ahoteesa miitho ni aheerela: Kinawoona atthu, yeettaka ankhala toko miri.
Ahonthatela tho matata mmiithoni, ni ule ahopacera woona uparapara, ni ahovona, oonaka rattaratta uttayi ni uparapara citthu cothene.
Yesu vano ahonlamulela urwaa uwaani, ni ahomwiirela: Uhikele mena umawaani.
Yesu ahoonwa na owiitthuca awe, akelaka umawaani co Sesareya wo Filipe. Mphironi ahaakoha owiitthuca awe, eeraka: Atthu ayo aneera wiira Mi kipani?
Yahomwiirela: Yohani Mpatisa, akina Eliya, ni akina tho aneera wiira uri mmoca mwa anapiyu.
Ni ahaakoha: Ni nyu nneera Mi kipani? Peturu ahaakhula: We uri Kristu.
Ahaalamulela vano, wiira ahinhimerye ntthu itthu ila.
Wahoolo ahopacera weetthuciha wiira Mwanawe Pinattamu naahala uhuva venci ni ukhottiya ni mahumu, ni oolupale a mayasataka, ni mayowantikha, mpaka wiiviya ni wunwelela anavinre mahuku mararu;
ni anawahimerya itthu ila wohakhuwa-khuwa. Peturu ahomwiihana Yesu ni ahopacera unkuphula.
Yesu nanso arukunuwaka, ni awehaka owiitthuca ahonkuphula Peturu, eeraka: Uthame wiitho aka, Sotwani, kontha khummwacera citthu ca Nluku, nanso paahi citthu ca atthu.
Eehanaka mphwinko wa atthu wamoca ni owiitthuca awe, aheerela: Ntthu, atthunaka ukitthara, eerune mwaneene, akuse nsalapa awe ni akitthare.
Nlattu, ntthu nohala uphavela woopola ukumi awe unanrihya, ni unhala unrihya nlattu wo miyano, ni nlattu wo Nhupi Wooreera nowowopola.
Enhala ukhuma isiyani, ntthu uphwanya ittuniya yothene ni arihaka nnepa awe?
Atthuna ntthu nohala uvaha isiyani wo wakakhaniha nnepa awe?
Ntthu mweeco nohala wuliya muru nlattu wo Miyano ni nlattu wo moolumo aka wamiithoni wanloko nna nookosakosa nimwalaanne ni Mi, ciicammo, Mwanawe Pinattamu naahala wuliya muru nlattu wa ale aphiyaka o nnemani wa Athumwane wamoca ni Ancelo attakattifu.
Yesu ahaahimerya tho: Khweeli kinawuhimeryani wiira akina mwaala ari vava khanhala ukhwa ahinaya woona omwene wa Nluku uwaka ni ikuru caya.
Anavinre mahuku siita, Yesu ahaakusa Peturu, Yakopu ni Yohani, ni ahaaweliha veekhaya, mwaako woorekama. Ni aheetatusa wamiithoni waya.
Coowara cawe cahothatuwa coowarya, cootteela usilili toko khaawo mayokattha vathiva uwoorya utteeliha ciicale.
Ahaakhumelela Eliya wamoca ni Musa ni ooyeli yanawuulumaca ni Yesu.
Peturu ahomwiirela Yesu: Mwalimu oreera ukhala vava, niteke marapattha mararu, nimoca na waa, nikina na Musa nikhwawe na Eliya.
Kontha khayaacuwela itthu yaahimyawe nlattu yanawoova venci.
Ni nahokhuruwa nihutte nakhunenle ni ntthuuci, ni nahokhuma ncu nnihutteni neera: Ula mwanaka oofentiya. Yooyo mwiiwe.
Nenna nna, awehaka, khayamoonne tho ntthu, ari Yesu veekhawe.
Wakhuruwaya mmwakoni, Yesu ahaalamulela wiira ahihimerye ntthu itthu yoonyaya, mpaka wahoolo Mwanawe Pinattamu nonwelenle mwaatthu ookhwa.
Ale yahotthara moolumo ale, nanso yaanakohana ayayoru manaaya, 'wunwelela mwaatthu ookhwa.'
Ni yahonkoha yiiraka: Mayowantikha aneerelani wiira woopacera Eliya phinhala uwa?
Ahaakhula: Aye, Eliya, awaaka woopacera naahala weesa wanipuroni waya citthu cothene, nanso yantikhiye isiyani ya Mwanawe Pinattamu, wiira nalamuliya uhuva venci, nuunyoholiya.
Ni mi mweeco kinawuhimeryani: Eliya ahowa, ni yahompankela cothene catthunaya, toko caantikhiye.
Naphile waryaya owiitthuca awe ahoona mphwinko muulupale wa atthu warukurenrye ayoca, ni mayowantikha anyakulihanaka na ale.
Amoonakaru Yesu yahotikhina ni yahotthimakaca unkoha isalama.
Ni ule ahaakoha ale: Nnonyakulihanani?
Ntthu mmoca mwa mphwinko ule, ahomwiirela: Mwalimu, kihowiihera mwanaka, rina nnepa woohuulumaca.
Wammaraka vale, unamphatela vathi ni ule napacera ukhuma niphooru, ucekesa miino ni phuumaka teyeye. Kihaalepela owiitthuca aa wiira yoomole ncini, nanso khayoonrye.
Yesu aheerela: Nyu, nloko noohikupali, kinhala ukhala ni nyu mpaka yakhani? Kinhala wuvilelani mpaka yakhani? Nkiwiihere woono.
Yahommwiihera. Nimoonakaru Yesu, ncini nahompukunyaa mwanhima ni ikuru, mpaka umphatela vathi, ni ahopacera uphirikyaa akhumaka niphooru mwano.
Yesu ahaakoha athumwane: Itthu ile inomwiiryanyaa ikhumelo yakhani. Na ale yahaakhula: Ikhumelo mwanamwane,
ni imaara cinci nahommonyera wamooroni ni mmasini wiira amwiive, nanso wooryaka vale upanka itthu, unoonele ikiriri, nuunikhavihere.
Yesu ahomwiirela: Wooryaka! Ntthu nokupali citthu cothene cinawooryanyaa.
Nenna nna, athumwane mwana oyo yahokhuwa: Kinakupali; nkikavihere uhikupali waka!
Yesu, oonaka wiira atthu enci yanawa, aholamulela nnepa woonanara ni aheerela: Nnepa wohuulumaca ni wohiwa, Mi kinawulamulela, ukhume wamwana ola, nuuhinturuwele tho.
Ni nnepa, ukhuwaka ni wicipulacaka ni ikuru, wahokhuma. Mwanhima ahokhala toko ookhwa, mpaka atthu enci wiira hokhwa.
Nanso, ammaraka ntata, Yesu ahommusa, ni ule aheemela.
Ukelawawe mpani, owiitthuca yahonkoka veekhawe: Nlattuni hiyano khanoonrye woomola?
Ahaakhula: Nloko nna ninoomoliya ni iswali ni utthuka paahi.
Akhumaka wonwo yahottupulaniha ilapo yo Kalileya, ni Yesu khatthuna wiira acuweliye ni ntthu,
nlattu anavira eetthucihaka owiitthuca awe ni anaweerela: Mwanawe Pinattamu naahala urwehiya mmatatani mwaatthu anhala umwiiva, nanso, nakhwile nowowunwelela anavinre mahuku mararu.
Nanso ayo khayeewehile nuulumo nne, ni yanamoova unkoha.
Yahophiya uKafarnaum, ni, anari uwaani, Yesu ahaakoha: Mwavanyihanani mphironi?
Yahomaalaca, nlattu mphironi yanavanyihana ayayoru, wiira tipani ri muulupale mwaale.
Unkomaka, Yesu aheehana owiitthuca awe khumi na eeli ni ahaahimerya: Ntthu aphavelaka ukhala muulupale, eepanke mwankani mwaatthu, ni akhale nrumeyi a atthu othene.
Ni ankusaka mwanamwane, ahomweesa iriyari aya, ahommarela ni aheerela:
Ntthu nomwaakhela mwanamwane toko ula mwancina naka, nokaakhela Miyano, ni ntthu nokaakhela Mi, khankaakhela Mi, nanso Ule kirumile.
Yohani ahonhimerya: Mwalimu, nihomoona ntthu oomolaka macini mwancina naa, ni ntthu ule khannitthara, ni nihomwaateliha.
Yesu ahaahimerya: Nhimwaatelihe, nlattu khaawo nopanka cotikhineeha mwancina naka phukaapa mi nenna nna.
Ntthu hinoniina, nawiraana ni hi.
Ntthu novahani ikoopu yo maasi wiira mmurye nlattu wokhala owiitthuca awe Kristu, khweeli, kinawuhimeryani, khankela ahalelaka itthuvo awe mena vakani.
Ntthu nohala unkosiha mmoca mwaasinamwane ala ankikupali Mi, fatari atthukeleliye nsiko mmo nsilo noosileliya ni avonyeriye mpaharini.
Ntata naa nookosihaka, uthikile. Unareera ukela wokumini ni ntata noopahuwa, wahohiyana ukhalana matata oomeli ni urwaa umooroni oohinttiphyaa.
Wonwo uhinkhwa asunku, ni mooro khunttiphyaa.
Nnya naa nookosihaka, uthikile. Unareera ukela wokumini unapahuwile, wahohiyana ukhalana oomeli uvonyeriyaka umooroni.
Wonwo uhinkhwa asunku, ni mooro khunttiphyaa.
Ni niitho naa nookosihaka, uphele. Unareera ukela umweneni wa Nluku ni niitho nimoca, wahohiyana ukhalana oomeli uvonyeriyaka umooroni.
Wonwo uhinkhwa asunku, ni mooro khunttiphyaa.
Phimaana khula ntthu naahala ulukiya ni mooro.
Maakha phi itthu yooreera; nanso yathatuwaka ooririya, ammolukiya ni isiyani? Nkhalaneke maakha mwanyu ni mweetteke ni mpuha ntthu ni nkhwawe.
Nakhumile wonwo, ahokela nttetthe wo Yutteya ni ukhopela mooloko Yorttani, ni mphwinko unathukumanne tho nipuro naryawe, anaweetthuciha tho, toko calemalenlyawe.
Yahomwattamerya mafarisi ni yahonkoha anttehaka: Iri yooreera nlopwana wamwalaana amwaarawe?
Ahaakhula: Musa holamulenleni isiyani?
Yahomwaakhula: Musa holevela waavaha iwarakha yoomwalaana, ni waahiya.
Yesu ahaakhula tho: Nlattu woolipa winyu nrima phuvahilyaweni nlamulo nno.
Nanso, wupattusoni wolapo, Nluku ahompanka nlopwana ni nthiyana.
Phimaana, nlopwana naahala waahiya athumwane na anumwane ni nokookhala na amwaarawe.
Ni ooyeli ankookhala irutthu imoca. Phimaana, khankhala tho eeli, nanso irutthu imoca.
Vano, yooluttanihiya ni Nluku, khimwalaanihiya ni ntthu.
Anaphile uwaani, owiitthuca awe yahonkoha tho itthu ile.
Yesu ahaahimerya: Ntthu nohala wamwalaana amwaarawe ni waathela akina, neetta uluva ni nthiyana ule,
ni nthiyana ammwalaanaka mannawe nuutheliya ni nkina, neetta uluva.
Yahomwiihera asinamwane wiira aakwanye, nanso owiitthuca yahakuphula ale yawihile asaana.
Yesu, oonaka itthu ile ahonyonyiya ni aheerela: Mwalevele, amirawo akiweele, ni nhoomole, nlattu omwene wa Nluku uri wa waya.
Khweeli kinawuhimeryani, ntthu hinhala waakhela omwene wa Nluku toko mmirawo, khanhala ukela wonwo.
Wahoolo ahaakusa vayawani phwathatelaka matata ni ahaareeriha.
Wakhumilyawe eettaka ni iphiro, ahomwattamerya ntthu atthimakacaka, ni akhoromelaka ahonkoha: Mwalimu ooreera, kipankekeni wiira kiphwanye ukumi woohimala?
Yesu ahonhimerya: Nnokihanelani ooreera? Khaawo ooreera hikhanle Nluku paahi.
Unacuwela malamulo: Uhiive, uheette uluva, uhiinye, uhoothe, uhithepye, waalemelihe athumwanaa na anumwanaa.
Ahomwaakhula: Mwalimu, cothene nnya kihosunka ikhumelo mmirawo.
Yesu ammwehecesaka, ahomfenta, ni ahomwaakhula: Inawuhaleela itthu imoca paahi; Urwee, watumihe citthu cothene cirinaa, waavahe nsurukhu uyo atthu oothwenya, ni ommokhalana nhakhu wirimu; uwe ni ukitthare.
Nanso, weewilyawe moolumo ale, ahothulana ni ahothama ni icuku, nlattu arina mihakhu cinci.
Awehaka nceresere, Yesu aheerela owiitthuca awe: Urikarika venci, atthu oothaciri ukela wumweneni wa Nluku.
Owiitthuca wahooma uwanoni, wowiiwa moolumo ala. Nanso Yesu ahopwahera: Asaana aka, cirikarikilyaya ukela wumweneni wa Nluku, ale ankhuluvela mihakhu.
Khavarikile uvira nkamira mwiithe wo sinkano, uhohiyana ukela thaciri wumweneni wa Nluku.
Ale yahotikhina wootepa nanlelo ni yanawiirelana ayayoru: Vano, tupani nohala woopwa!
Awehecesaka, Yesu ahaakhula: Na atthu khinooryaniya, nanso ni Nluku citthu cothene cinawooryaniya.
Peturu ahopacera unhimerya: Hi nihohiya cothene nihottharani.
Yesu ahaakhula: Khweeli kinawuhimeryani wiira khaawo ntthu nohala uhiya inupa awe, asunnawe, asirokorawe, athumwane na anumwane, asaana atthuna imatta awe nlattu wo Miyano, ni nlattu wo Nhupi Wooreera,
phihaakhela mpaka imaara iminya, nanano ukati ula urihula, inupa, asunnawe, asirokorawe, anumwane, asaana ni imatta, wamoca ni womolanihaciya, ni wahoolo ukumi woohimala.
Enci oopacera ankokhala uwiheerya, ni uwiheerya ankokhala oopacera.
Owiitthuca yaanaweetta ni iphiro, awelaka uYerusalemu, ni Yesu anaweetta uhoolo waya. Yanatikhina ni yaanantthara ni woova. Ahaakusa tho owiitthuca khumi na eeli, ahopacera wahimerya itthu yahala umwiiranela,
eeraka: Mwiiwe, ninawela oYerusalemu, ni Mwanawe Pinattamu naahala urwehiya mmatatani moolupale a mayasataka ni mayowantikha, na ale anaahala ummaanela umwiiva nuunrweha waasenci.
Anaahala untarawa, unsuwela wiitho, umwapsyulaca nuumwiiva, nanso nihuku noneeraru naahala wunwelela.
Yakopu ni Yohani, asaana a Sepetteu, yahomwattamerya ni yahomwiirela: Mwalimu, nimphavela, unipankele yothene inhalehu wulepela.
Yesu ahaakoha: Nnophavela kuupankeleni isiyani?
Yahomwaakhula: Wumweneni waa, nunkome, mmoca mono nlopwana, ni nkina mono nthiyana.
Yesu ahaakhula: Khannocuwela itthu inlepelenyu. Nnawoorya uwurya ikoopu inhalaka uwurya, ni waakhela upatiso unhalaka waakhela?
Yahomwaakhula: Aye, ninawoorya. Yesu ahaahimerya: Nnowowurya ikoopu inhalaka uwurya, ni nnowopatisiya ni upatiso unhalaka upatiseriya,
nanso, wunkoma mono nlopwana atthuna nthiyana kahi phi Mi kinvaha, anovahiya ale asunkeriye.
Akina khumi, yiiwakaru itthu ile, yahonyonyiya ni Yakopu ni Yohani.
Yesu aheehana ni aheerela: Nhocuwela cimpankaya alamuli onlaponi wiira acuwanehe iyulupale aya mmalokoni ni mahumu aya.
Nanso ni nyuva khunhala ukhala commo. Ntthu nophavela ukhala muulupale mwa nyu eepanke nrumeyi,
ni nophavela ukhala oopacera mwa nyu eepanke ipottha ya atthu othene,
nlattu Mwanawe Pinattamu khaawile uvareliya nteko, nanso uvara nteko ni uvaha ukumi awe wiira oopole atthu enci.
Yahophiya uYeriko. Wakhumaya uYeriko ni owiitthuca awe, ni mphwinko muulupale, Partimeu, mayoolepela oohoona, mwanawe Timeu, ahonkoma nceresere iphiro aphavelaka ulola.
Weewilyawe wiira Yesu o Nasaree anavira, ahokhuwa: Yesu, Mwanawe Taviti, ukoonele ikiriri.
Atthu enci yanankuphula wiira ammaalihe, nanso anapwaha ukhuwa khula imaara wootepa eeraka: Mwana a Taviti, ukoonele ikiriri.
Yesu aheemela ni aheera: Mmwiihane. Yahomwiihana ntthu uhoona yiiraka: Ulipe nrima, wunwe, nawiihana.
Ni ule, arulaka ikacako awe, ahotupha ni ahorwaa waYesu.
Yesu ahonkoha: Untthuna kupankele isiyani? Oohoona ahaakhula: Mwalimu, koone.
Yesu ahonhimerya: Urwee, ikupalelo aa ihowoopola. Ni nananoru ahoona ni ahontthara Yesu mphironi.
Naattamenrye uYerusalemu, vakhiviru ni Petifaki ni Petaniya, cooco ni mwako Olivera, Yesu ahaaruma owitthuca awe eeli,
ni ahaahimerya: Nrwee iwaani yowaattamana, mwakelaka nnamphwanya mwaapuru ootthukiya, hinaya uweliya ni ntthu. Mwantthukule ni nkiwiihere.
Akhalaka ntthu nookohani, nlattuni mpankaka ciicammo. Mwaakhule Apwiya anamphavela, ni ankowuturuselani wowakuvyaca.
Yahorwaa phumphwanyaka mwaapuru natthukeleliye wankhorani, mphante wovate woluwani, ni yahontthukula.
Ni atthu yaari wonwo yahokoha: Nnopankani muntthukulaka mwaapuru?
Yahaakhula toko Yesu cahimenrawe, ni yahaahiya urwaca.
Yahonrwehela Yesu mwaapuru uyo, yahonkhunela cowara caya, ni Yesu ahomwela.
Atthu enci yaanawatala cowara caya mphironi, akina yamwarusela miritha cikithi caathikinlyaya mmattani.
Atthu yahoonle na ale yantthara yanakhuwa: Hosaana, noreeriya nowa mwancina na Apwiya.
Uhoreeriya omwene umwa wa athumwanihu Taviti. Hosaana wonculu.
Ahophiya uYerusalemu, Yesu ahokela Inupa ya Nluku, ni namanle uweha citthu cothene canrukurenrye, wahokhala yocoocilo, ahokhuma, phurwaka uPetaniya ni owiitthuca awe khumi na eeli.
Wasilyaya wicisu wakhumaya uPetaniya, Yesu yahommola itala.
Oonaka uttayi mwiri wonhokorokho waari ni matakhuru aya makithi, ahorwaa uweha wakhala wiira uhaawo nhokorokho wowiima, nanso attameryaka, khaphwanyile, aphwanyile matakhuru paahi, kontha khawari ukati wowiima mihokorokho.
Aheerela vano: Hikhale tho nohala ulya cowiima caa. Ni owiitthuca awe yaheewa itthu ile.
Yahophiya uYerusalemu, ni akelaka Inupa ya Nluku ahopacera woomola mayothumiha, na ale yathuma wonwo, ahokakhela vathi meeca a atthu yaakakhaniha, ni ihice ca atthu yathuma ikhuntta.
Ni khaalevela wiira ikusiye itthu yakhuma Inupa ya Nluku.
Ni anaweetthuciha eeraka: Ihantikhiya: Inupa aka inowowihaninya inupa yoswali uneethi wothene. Nanso nyu nhotatusa nikhuku na namwiinya.
Oolupale a mayasataka ni mayowantikha yaheewa itthu ile, ni yaanaphavela mananna umwiiva, nanso yaanamoova, nlattu mphwinko wothene wanawuminya mwaano ni meetthuciho awe.
Wiila waya, yahorwaa utaa waya iparasa.
Uvira waya, wicisu, yahoona mwiri wonhokorokho unoomile, ni mitithari caya cothene.
Ni Peturu oopuwelaka, ahomwiirela Yesu: Wooneke mwalimu, mwiri wonhokorokho ulaphilyaa, uhooma.
Yesu aheerela: Munkupali Nluku.
Khweeli kinawuhimeryani, ntthu eerelaka mwako ula: 'Wiiphele nipuro niryaa wivonyere upahari', ni ahaanyihereke munrimani mwawe nanso akupaliki wiira itthu ihimilyawe inaahala wiiranyaa; khweeli, inawiiranyaa.
Phimaana, kinawuhimeryani wiira citthu cothene cinhalenyu ulepela nswaliki, nkupaliki wiira nnawaakhela, ni nnapattha.
Mwemelaka vale wiira nswali, mwakhalanaka mwamweetthu ni nkhwiinyu, munleveleke wiira Athumwaninyu, ari wirimu, yuuleveleleni cookosa cinyu.
Nlattu, mwahaleveleleke akhwinyu, Athumwaninyu ari wirimu khanhala ulevelela cookosa cinyu.
Yahoturuwela uYerusalemu, ni Yesu eettaka Mpani mwaNluku, oolupale a mayasataka, mayowantikha ni mahumu, yahomwaattamerya
ni yahoonkoha: Umpanka citthu nnya ni nlamulo nawani? Ulamulenle tipani upanka citthu nnya?
Yesu ahaakhula: Hata ni mi, kinawukohani itthu. Nkaakhule vano kinaahala wuhimeryani cineeraka woopanka citthu nnya ni nlamulo nawani.
Upatisu wa Yohani waari wo wirimu, atthuna wa atthu? Nkaakhule.
Yahopacera ukohana ayayoru, yiiraka: Neeraka, wo wirimu, naahala wiira, 'Nhinkupalenleni mweeco?'
Neeraka, wa atthu, ninawoova mphwinko. Nlattu othene yanamoona Yohani toko nnapiyu.
Umwiisoni yahomwaakhula: Khanincuwela. Ni Yesu aheerela: Hata ni Mi akinohimeryani ni nlamulo nawani kimpankaka citthu nnya.
Yesu ahopacera woolumacera ni malikanihero: Ahaawo ntthu aanle imatta yo vinyu, ahopophela nkuco, ahothipa nlitti no waameliya ivinyu ni ahoteka ipwaro. Wahoolo ahaahiyera ananteko arwaka ikwaha awe yoottayi.
Ukati woohephiya, ahonruma nrumeyi awe wiira aakhele nuusu no cowiima co mmattani.
Ale nanso, yahommara, yahomwaatta nuunturusela uttuli wohiitthu.
Ni ahonruma nrumeyi nkina. Ni uyo tho yahompwesa muru ni yahontarawa venci.
Ahonruma nkina, ni ule yahomwiiva. Ahaaruma akina enci, na ale yahaatta ni akina weeva.
Nahalenle nlelo mwanawe oofentiya, umwisoni ahonruma ule, eeraka: Anaahala unlemeliha mwanaka.
Nanso, ananteko yaheerelana ayayoru: Ule phinkokhalana imatta ila! Nrwee, nimwiive, ni imatta inakhala yawihu.
Yahommara ni yahomwiiva, nuunrihela nceresere imatta.
Mwaneene imatta ile nohala upankani? Nahala uturuwa ni weeva ananteko ayo, ni wahoolo, naahala waavaha imatta ananteko akina.
Khansomile cowantikhiya cittakattifu? Nluku nikhottiye ni mayoteka, nihothatuwa nluku no wanlothoni nowokolela inupa.
Itthu ila inkhuma wa Apwiya, ni iri yoothamaliya wamiithoni wihu.
Yaanawavya ummara, nanso yanawoova mphwinko, nlattu yaheeweha ratta, wiira nlikanihero nne naaca yaayo. Yahonhiya ni yahorwaca.
Wahoolo yahonrumihela mafarisi ni maherotiyano akina wiira ammare mmoolumoni.
Amwaattameryaka yahomwiirela: Mwalimu, nihocuwela wiira uri nlopwana eekhweeli, khaawo nonramelaa, nlattu khumweha makhalelo a ntthu, nanso unawiitthuciha iphiro ya Nluku, toko cinkhalaya yeekhweeli. Unihimerye, iri itthu yooloka atthuna yoohiloka unvaha nsoko Sesari? Ninvahe atthuna nihinvahe?
Yesu acuwelaka wototha waya, ahaakhula: Nnokittehacerani? Nkiwiihere nikopiri, koone.
Yahomwiihera ni ahaakoha: Yawani ila yocaphariya, ni yowantikhiya ila? Yahaakhula: Ya Sesari.
Yesu aheerela: Mumvahe Sesari itthu ya Sesari, ni Nluku itthu ya Nluku. Ni yahotikhinaca venci.
Wahoolo yahowa masatuseu, ale aneera khuwo wunwelela wa atthu ookhwa, yahomwaattamerya, ni yahonkoha Yesu:
Mwalimu, Musa honantikhela wiira ntthu ankhwelaka munnawe, pwahiyaka amwaarawe woohikhalana asaana, nhimaawe nolamuliya unthela nthiyana oohinnya wiira ahiye ipyo ya munnawe.
Vano yahaawo asunna saapa, ni oopacera uyo ahonthela ni ahokhwa woohahiya asaana.
Oonayeeli ahonthela nthiyana ahinye, ni uyo ahokhwa woohahiya asaana, ni ooneeraru uyo waheerannyaa ciicammo,
ni othene saapa yahokhwa woohahiya asaana. Wiimaleloni waya nthiyana uyo ahokhwa.
Vanhala wunweleliya, nthiyana nohala ukhala amwaara awani, nlattu asilopwana saapa ale yahonthela nthiyana ule?
Yesu ahaakhula: Nyu nnawithepyaca nlattu woohicuwela cowantikhiya cittakattifu hata ikuru ca Nluku.
Phimaana wanhalaya wunwelela mwaatthu ookhwa, khuwo utheliya, mena khuwo uthelana, nanso ammokhala toko ancelo o wirimu.
Nanso itthu inaciya mowunwelelani mwaatthu ookhwa, khansomile ikitapu ya Musa, itthu yeeranele ni nikukhu napharela woohivya, toko Nluku caamuulumacenryawe eeraka: Mi kiri Nluku a Aprahamu, Nluku a Isaaki, ni Nluku a Yakopu?
Khankhala Nluku a atthu ookhwa, nanso Nluku a atthu akumi. Nyu khanreere weetta ni ututhi.
Ahomwaattamerya mayowantikha eewile avanyihanaka, ni oonaka wiira Yesu aakhunle ratta, ahonkoha: Phinni nlamulo noopacera o malamuloni othene?
Yesu ahaakhula: Noopacera phi nna: Wiiwe Israel, Apwiya Nluku ihu pha Mwaneene Nluku veekhaya.
Wafente Mwaneene Nluku aa, ni nrima aa wothene, ni nnepa aa wothene, na ankhili aa othene, ni ikuru caa cothene.
Nonayeeli phi nna: Umfente nkhwaa toko we o mwaneene. Khaniwo nlamulo noopwaha ala.
Mayowantikha yahomwiirela: Ureera cinene, Mwalimu, khaawoothile eenryaa wiira Ule ri veekhawe ni khaawo tho nkina noompwaha Ule;
nuumfenta ni nrima wothene, ni ankhili othene, ni nnepa wothene ni ikuru cothene, nuumfenta nkhwaa toko mwaneene, iri itthu yootepa woovikana isataka coopahiya ni coovelelihiya cothene.
Yesu, oonaka wiira ntthu ule ahaakhula ni nruku, ahomwiirela: Khuri uttayi ni omwene wa Nluku. Ni khariwo tho unkoha itthu.
Eetthucihaka Mpani mwa Nluku, Yesu ahokoha: Mayowantikha ahimyaka cani wiira Mesiya phiri mwanawe Taviti?
Taviti mwaneene, athoonyeriyaka ni Nnepa Nttakattifu, heera: Apwiya yaheerela Apwiya aka: Wonkome moono aka nlopwana, mpaka Mi keese eenani aa vathivaya manyaa aa.
Taviti mwaneene namwiihana, Apwiya. Nokhalaka cani mwanawe? Ni mphwinko muulupale wanamwiiwa ni utteeliya nrima.
Wowiitthuciha, Yesu anawiira: Nkhale miitho, mwisunke ni mayowantikha unacivela uthoonyera coowara coorekama nuukohiya isalama mmapuwani;
wonkoma mapuro uhoolo nnsinakokani ni mapuro anliya isukuhuulu.
Anawalyacera anankwele yoothereryaka ni iswali coottaliva. Ala anowowaakhela ihukhumu yootepa.
Nonkomile nipuro naheliya coovelela yawehaka atthu yahela nsurukhu nkasani mwe. Mathaciri menci yanahela nsurukhu mwinci.
Ahowa nthiyana nankwele oothwenya, ahelaka makopiri meli ooyevaca, manaaya nikupatta nonecese.
Eehanaka owiitthuca awe, Yesu ahaahimerya: Khweeli kinawuhimeryani wiira nthiyana ula nankhwele oothwenya hohela woopwaha atthu othene ahenle nkasani yo nhakhu.
Nlattu, othene yahenle yohalahala muthacirini mwaya, nanso nthiyana oothwenya ahenle yothene yarinawe, ni khahalanne itthu hata yankani.
Wakhumaawe Mpani mwa Nluku owiitthuca mmoca ahonhimerya: Mwalimu, moone, maluku menci ale ni cootekiya nnya!
Yesu ahaakhula: Unawoona cootekiya nnye cuulupale? Khaninkela naahalaka nluku nimoca waculu nluku nikhwaya, cothene cimmotankuliya.
Ni nonkomile mmwako wo Olivera uhoolo waya Inupa ya Nluku, Peturu, Yakopu, Yohani ni Anteree, yahonkoha ntthikini:
Unihimerye wiira citthu nnye cinhala wiiranyaa yaakhani, ni ikanyero inhala uthonyera wiira citthu nnye ciri vakhiviru.
Yesu ahopacera wahimerya: Mwisunke wiira hikhale ntthu noothepyani.
Kontha, anaahala uwa atthu enci mwancina naka yiiraka 'Phi mi!' mpaka wathepya atthu enci.
Mwiiwaka cuulumaciyaka cokhotto, ni myaha cokhotto, nhituthuwe. Citthu nnye cinalamuliya wiiranyaa nanso khunakhalaka mwiso.
Nloko nimoca ninhala uvaraana ni nloko nikhwaya, omwene mmoca ni omwene nkhwaya. Ilapo inaahala uthukumela mapuro makina, ni immovola itala. Citthu nnye ciri mapacerero woona coowerya.
Nkhale miitho! Anaahala wurwehani upwaroni, nnaahala wapsyuliya nnsinakokani. Nnaahala weemesiya wa miithoni wa mayansatoro ni mamwene nlattu wo Miyano, wiira mmahe usaahiti wamiithoni waya.
Nanso woopacera Nhupi Wooreera unaahala uhimeriya maloko othene.
Vano mwakusiyaka wiira moolumaciye makhuce, nhoove itthu inhalenyu uhimya. Nanso nhimye itthu inhalenyu uvahiya ukati yooyo, kahi mweeco nyuva nnohala wuulumaca, nanso Nnepa Nttakattifu.
Munna naahala unrweha unokhwani munnawe, ni athumwane mwanawe; ni asaana ammowuulumacera makhuce athumwanaya, mpaka weeva.
Ni nnaahala wiinananinya nlattu wo ncina naka, nanso ntthu nohala ukhalana nthiti mpaka umwisoni, nowowoopwa.
Moonaka citthu co miikho cikhumelelaka toko itankuleliyo wahimphwanelaya ukhala (nosoma uyo eeweehe), vano ale ari uYutteya atthawele mmwakoni.
Ari wancarani ahikhuruwe hata ahikele mpani wiira akuse citthu caya.
Ari mmattani ahituruwele uwaani wiira yakuse coowara caya.
Atakhaliye pha ale ari ni irukulu, na ale anamwiha asaana mahuku ale!
Nswali wiira itthu ile ihiiranye ukati weyiita.
Nlattu mahuku ale coohosiya cinkokhala toko caharyaya ukhalakaru, ikhumelo wapattusilyawe Nluku ittuniya, mpaka nnava, hata khacinkela cakhalaka tho.
Ni yahari Apwiya akhuvehaka mahuku ale, hata ntthu khoopwa, nanso nlattu wa atthu oothanliya naahala ukhuveha.
Akhalaka ntthu nohimeryani: 'Mesiya ri vava!' atthuna, 'Umoone wonwo!', nhikupali,
kontha anaahala wunwa amesiya oowootha ni anapiyu oowootha ni ankopanka ikanyero ni cootikhineeha wiira yaathepye, wanooranyaya, hata oothanliya.
Nanso nyu, mwisunke; kihohimeryani cothene marapuroru.
Nanso mahuku ale, anamanle mahuviho ale, ncuwa ninaahala uripela, ni mweeri khunhala waarya,
itthoottwa cinaahala umora wirimu, ni ikuru conculu cinaahala upukunyiya.
Vano naahala wooniya, awaka mmahutteni Mwanawe Pinattamu ni ikuru cuulupale ni waarya.
Nahala waruma ancelo awe ni wathukumaniha atthu yathanlilyawe mittetthe co micese cophyoo, umalenlyaya ilapo nuumalenlyaya irimu.
Mwiitthuce, mweeco, nlikanihero no mwiri wonhokorokho. Miritta caya cakhalaka miheenya, ni capaceraka uphuwa, nhocuwela wiira iyiita iri vakhiviru.
Ciicammo nyu, moonaka ukumelela citthu nnya, ncuwele wiira Mwanawe Pinattamu ri vakhiviru, wankhora.
Khweeli kinawuhimeryani: Khanimmira nloko nna cihiraneele citthu cothene nnya.
Irimu ni ilapo cinaahala uvira, nanso moolumo aka khanhala uvira.
Nanso khaawo nocuwela nihuku nne, hata ukati ule, mena ancelo o wirimu, mena Mwana, nanso Athumwane paahi phincuwela.
Nkhale miitho, nrontte! Nlattu khannocuwela nihuku ninhalaya uphiya ukati ule.
Uri toko ntthu alakenle ikhwaha awe, ahiyaka inupa awe, ahaahiyera iyuulupale arumeyi awe, khula ntthu ahovahiya nteko woovara, ni ahonlamulela mayokhaliha wiira arontte.
Vano nrontte, nlattu khannocuwela ukati unhalaawe uwa mwaneene itthoko; toko yocoocilo, atthuna uhiyu iriyari, atthuna uneepile nthupi, atthuna wicisu,
wahikhumelele wiira, nawile ni wututuserani, huphwanyeni nrupaka.
Itthu inohimeryakani nyu, kinahimerya atthu othene: Nrontte!
Yahanle mahuku meeli uphiya isukuhuulu yo Pasikuwa ni nihuku ninliyaya mikatthe coohimiropo, oolupale a mayasataka ni mayowantikha yanawaavya mananna untthuka wo makhuce nuumwiiva.
Yanawiira: Itthu ila ihiiriye mahuku osukuhuulu wiira atthu ayo ahipanke ipokoho.
Yesu nari uPetaniya, nonkomile wameeca mpani mwawe Simoni omakunttula, ahowa nthiyana, acisile iphotiri yo nluku ya alapasturo inheliya makhura oonukhela yeehaninya narttu, anthumihiya ncurukhu mwinci, napwesile iphotiri, aheetthela makhura mmuru mwaYesu.
Nanso akina yahonyonyinya, yiirelanaka ayayooru: Ariheliyeni ciicammo makhura ala?
Yanawoorya uthumihiya ni ncurukhu iminya tharu, mpaka wakawela atthu oothwenya. Ni yahonkuphula nthiyana ule.
Yesu nanso aheera: Nhiyeke. Munkuphulelaka isiyani? Hokipankela itthu yooreera;
Kontha, atthu oothwenya phinakhalaneenyu, ni mwatthunaka nnawoorya waapankela cooreera, nanso miyano akinkhala ni nyu mahuku othene.
Ale ahopanka itthu yoonryaya. Ahoottiha ni makhura irutthu aka ahoolelihaka uvithiya waka kihinaaya ukhwa.
Khweeli kinawuhimeryani, wiira mwiilaponi mothene unhalaya ulalyaa Nhupi Wooreera, inaahala tho uhimiya itthu yapankilyawe wiira upuweleliye.
Vano, Yutta Iskariyoti, mmoca mwaale khumi na eeli, akenle woolupale a mayasataka wiira amulume makhuce Yesu.
Weewilyaya moolumo ale, cahaatteela mirima ni yahovanela ummaha nsurukhu. Yutta anawavya ukati wontumiha Yesu.
Nihuku noopacera no mikatthe coohimiropo, ukati waveleelihiya mwakhontwa o Pasikuwa, owiitthuca yahonkoha Yesu: Nnotthuna ulokiheriya vayi nipuro noonlya Pasikuwa?
Ahaaruma owiitthuca eeli ni aheerela: Murwee uparasa. Nnaahala umphwanya ntthu oocisa mwaapu wo maasi. Muntthare,
ni unkelaawe, munhimerye mwaneene inupa: Mwalimu nakoha: Inupa inhalaka umaka iri vayi, kinlyaka Pasikuwa ni owiitthuca aka?
Ni naahala wuthonyerani nsana nuulupale uculu nooreerihiya ni nowaaya; mwanilokihere nenno.
Akhumaka owiitthuca awe, yahorwaa uparasa, ni yahophwanya toko cahimeriyaya; ni yahontthonkomaniha Pasikuwa.
Wiila waya, Yesu ahophiya na owiitthuca awe khumi na eeli.
Anonkomacile alyaka, Yesu aheera: Khweeli kinawuhimeryani, mmoca mwa nyu, nolya ni mi, naahala ukuuluma makhuce.
Yahanca ucukulaca, yiirelanaka ayayoru: Kahi thi mi?
Yesu ahaakhula: Phi mmoca mwa nyu khumi na eeli, nokilyana nttiisi nimoca.
Nlattu, Mwanawe Pinattamu narwa, toko cantikhelyawe, nanso natakhaliya ntthu nohala unthumiha! Phatari ahiyariye.
Walyaya, Yesu ahokusa nkatthe ni nareerihile, ahomyaniha ni ahaavaha owiitthuca awe, eeraka: Nkuseke, nlyeke, ila phi irutthu aka.
Wahoolo ahokusa ikikhompe, ahosukuru ni ahaavaha ni othene yahowurya.
Ni ahaahimerya: Ila phi iphome aka, iphome yo waatana wonaanano, invuviheriya atthu enci.
Khweeli kinawuhimeryani wiira akinhala tho uwurya yowiima ila yo viteera mpaka nihuku ninhalaka uwurya tho wumweneni wa Nluku.
Aneepile ncipo, yahokhumaca arwaka umwako wo Olivera.
Yesu ahaahimerya: Nyu othene, uhiyu ula, nnaahala uhiya ikupalelo nlattu wo miyano, kontha ihantikhiya: Kinanrakaliha nhakheli ni ikhontwaa cinkomwaryaca.
Nanso kinonwelenle, kimmowuhoolelani wokela uKalileya.
Peturu aheera: Hata othene ahiye ikupalelo aya, nanso mi, mena.
Yesu ahomwaakhula: Khweeli kinawuhimeryani, ilelo uhiyu ula, nthupi uhinaya wiipa imaara piili, unakikhotta imaara tharu.
Nanso Peturu ahopwahera wakhula ni ikuru eeraka: Hata kilamuliye ukhwa ni nyu, akinookhottani. Ni othene yahoolumaca ciicale.
Yahorwaa nipuro neehaninya Yetsemani, ni Yesu ahaahimerya owiitthuca awe: Munkome vava mi kiswaliki.
Ahonkusa Peturu, Yakopu, ni Yohani, ni ahanca woova ni ucukula.
Ahaahimerya: Nnepa aka unacukula, icuku yo nokhwa. Nkhale vava ni nrontte.
Apwahaka vakani, ahowuluwela vathi ni ahoswali wiira wooryanyaa, ukati ula ukipwahe.
Ni ahohimya: Apa, Tiithi; Nyu nnawoorya cothene. Nkitamihe mmahuvihoni! Nanso, cihipankiye cintthunaka, nanso cintthuneenyu.
Uturuwa wawe, aphwanyile arupaka, ni ahomwiirela Peturu: Simoni unarupa? Khawoonrye wiliphila iwora imoca?
Mwiliphile ni nswaliki wiira nhithokociye. Nrima unatthuna ratta, nanso irutthu khinlipa.
Ahorwaa tho uswalini, akulelaka moolumo yaayo.
Ahoturuwa, ni ahaaphwanya arupaka kontha miitho aya yahocara ikhove. Ni khayoona yomwakhula.
Ahowa imaara yoneeraru mpaka waahimerya: Mpaka nna nnaarupa ni nnamumula tho? Wahotosa! Ukati uhophiya. Mwanawe Pinattamu naahala urwehiya mmatatani mwaatthu ookosakosa.
Muunwe, Nrwee! Kitumihile uyo hophiya.
Yesu oolumacaka nanlelo phaphilyawe Yutta, ari mmoca mwaale khumi na eeli, ni mphwinko muulupale wakhumile woolupale a mayasataka, mayowantikha ni mahumu ni warina ikatana ni ikopo.
Namakhuce ahaahimerya ikanyero eeraka: Nohalaaka unkoha isalaama, phi yooyo, mumvare ni munkuse natthukiye ratta.
Uphiya wawe, ahomwaattamerya ni ahomwiirela: Mwalimu! Ni ahonkoha isalaama.
Yahommara Yesu, ni yahontthuka.
Vano, mmoca mwaale eemenle wonwo, ahokumiha ikatana ahorakaliha ipottha ya nkhulupale a mayasataka, ahonthikila nnyaru.
Yesu ahaahimerya: Nkhumile ni ikatana ni ikopo uwa ukitthuka, toko mayohukha.
Kaari ni nyu mahuku othene mpani mwa Nluku, kiitthucihaka ni khamwakitthukile. Nanso wiira citthariheleliye toko caantikhiyaya.
Vano, anhiyaka, othene yahotthawa.
Ni ahontthara mmirawo mmoca eekhunenle ikuwo. Yahommara,
nanso ahiyaka ikuwo ile, ahotthawa pwitipwiti.
Yahonrweha Yesu wankhulupale a mayastaka wathukumannyaya othene oolupale a mayasataka, mayowantikha ni mahumu.
Peturu ahontthara uttayittayi mpaka nhina ipuwa ya nkhulupale a mayasataka. Peturu wonkomilyawe wamoca ni ananteko ootthaka mooro.
Vano, oolupale a mayasataka ni mayothukumana othene yaavya osaahiti, wowiira amwiive Yesu, nanso khayaaphwanyile.
Enci yaanahimya cowootha, nanso cahimilyaya khaweerana.
Ahaawo yeemenle ni uromola yowootha ila yiiraka:
Hi nihomwiiwa ahimyaka: Kinhala ukwanyula inupa ila, itekiye ni matata a atthu, ni mahuku mararu kinaahala uteka ikina yoohitekiya ni matata a atthu.
Nanso, hata ciicammo usaahiti aya khaweeranne.
Vano, muulupale o mayasataka aheemela iriyari aya atthu yathukumanne ni ahonkoha Yesu: Khunakhula itthu nhina osaahiti ommahaya atthu ala?
Yesu nanso ahomaala ni khaakhunle itthu. Muulupale a mayasataka ahonkoha tho: We uri Kristu, Mwana a Nluku Ooreerihiya?
Yesu ahaakhula: Kiri mi, ni nnaahala umoona Mwanawe Pinattamu nonkomile moono nlopwana wa Nluku Okuru, ni awaka mmahutteni o wirimu.
Vano, muulupale a mayasataka ahaahula coowara cawe ni aheera: Nimphavela tho vayi osaahiti?
Mwanamwiiwa ukufuru nwo. Nneera cani? Na atthu othene yahonhukhumu ukhwa.
Wahoolo, akina yaanapacera unsuwela, yahonkhunela wiitho ni ikuwo nuumwaatta yiiraka: Uhimyace nnapiyu! Ni mayorontta yahonkusa nuumwaattakaca.
Peturu neemenle vate wapuwani, ahophiya nanteko mwanthiyana a muulupale a mayasataka,
ni umoona wawe Peturu ootthaka mooro, ahomwehecesa ni ahomwiirela: We khweeli wari ni Yesu o Nasaree.
Ule nanso ahoruna, eeraka: Akinoncuwela, hata akineeweha inhimyaa iyo. Wahoolo ahokhumela vate iluwani, ni nthupi waheepa.
Nanteko mwanthiyana, umoona wawe tho, ahaahimerya atthu yaatamananyawe: Ula phi mmocaru.
Nanso ahoruna imaara yonapiili. Ukati vakani tho, ale yaari mmo, yahonhimerya Peturu: Khweeli we phi mmocaru, kontha uri nkalileya.
Nanso aholapha ni aholupela eeraka: Akinoncuwela ntthu nnomwaacenyu.
Ni nenna nna nthupi waheepa imaara yonapiili. Vano, Peturu ahoopuwela itthu yahimilyawe Yesu: Nthupi uhinaya wiipa imaara piili, we unaahala ukiruna imaara tharu. Ni vava ahopacera wunla.
Usakaru, yahothukumana oolupale a mayasataka wamoca ni mahumu ni mayowantikha, ni mayonthukumano othene; ni untthuka waya Yesu, yahonkusa ni yahommelela waPilatu.
Pilatu ahonkoha: We uri Mwene a Ayutta? Yesu ahomwaakhula: We uhohimya.
Ni oolupale a mayasataka yahonriyelela citthu cinci.
Pilatu ahonkoha tho eeraka: Khunakhula itthu? Woone, citthu cinci cinriyeleliyaa na atthu ala.
Yesu nanso khaakhunle tho itthu, ni Pilatu ahotikhina.
Nihuku nosukuhuulu, Pilatu aholemalela untthukula nantthukiya mmoca yantthunaya atthu.
Ahaawo nlopwana mmoca, eehaninya Parapasi, atthukiye wamoca na anaporonka nlattu yamwiivile ntthu ukati wonkhitto.
Mphwinko wa atthu, wahonwa ni wahopacera ulepela itthu yalemalenlyawe wapankela.
Pilatu ahaakhula: Nnotthuna wiira kutthukuleleni Mwene a Ayutta?
Nlattu ahocuwela wiira oolupale a mayasataka yamwiihenre nlattu woonrama.
Nanso oolupale a mayasataka yanatheperya mphwinko wiira phatari Pilatu antthukule Parapasi.
Pilatu ahaakoha: Kinhala umwiiriha isiyani ula nnomwiihanenyu Mwene a Ayutta?
Na ale yankhuwaca tho: Unkhomele wansalapani!
Vano Pilatu aheera: Tthekileni? Nanso ale yanakhuwaca: Unkhomele wansalapani!
Pilatu, atthunaka wamaaliha atthu ale, ahaataphulela Parapasi. Ni aholamula wiira Yesu apsuliye ni akhomeliye wansalapani.
Anakhotto yahonkusa upwaroni ya nsatoro, ni yaheehaninya anakhotto othene.
Yahomwariha ihancu yookhwiila, ni yahomweesa ikhilempa yo miiwa wamuru wawe.
Wahoolo yahopacera unkoha nretele yiiraka: Salaama, Mwene a Ayutta!
Yanamwaatta wamuru ni nthale ni yanansuwela ni ankhoromelaka yananlapela.
Wamanlyaya untarawaca yahonrula ihancu yokhwiila ni umwariha tho cawawe. Vano yahonkusa wiira akhomeliye wansalapani.
Yahommara athumwane Alisantere ni Rufu, eehaninya Simoni o Sirene aakhuma umawaani ni ahokanyererihiya ukusa nsalapa.
Yahonrweha nipuro neehaninya Kolokootha, manaaya, nipuro nokohi.
Yahommaha ivinyu yootakaniheriya ni miira, nanso ahokhotta uwurya.
Wahoolo yahonkhomela wansalapani. Ni akawelanaka cowara cawe, yahopanka mwaavi wiira yoone yahalaawe uphwanya khula ntthu.
Yaari iwora yoneeraru wakhomeliyawe wansalapani.
Waculu wawe yahantikhiya yariyeleliyawe: MWENE A AYUTTA.
Yahokhomeliya wamoca ni Ule, mayohukha eeli, mmoca, moono nlopwana, nkina moono nthiyana.
Ciicammo cootthariheleliya cowantikhiya cineera: Ahaalikeliya na atthu oonanara nrima.
Atthu yaavira ayo, yananruwana, apukunyaka muru, yiiraka: We! Watankulaca Inupa ya Nluku ni uteka tho mahuku mararu.
We wicoopole o mwaneene nuukhuruwe wansalapani!
Oolupale a mayasataka ni mayowantikha yanateehana, yiiraka: Hoopola akina ni khanoorya wicoopola mwaneene.
Akhuruwe naanano wansalapani uyo Kristu, Mwene o Israel, wiira nimoone ni ninkupali. Na atthu ale yakhomeliye ni Ule, yananruwana.
Waphilyaya ukati woothana ipiphi yahokhunela ilapo yothene mpaka yocoocilo.
Uphiya waya yocoocilo Yesu ahokhuwa ni ncu noorunya: Eloi, Eloi, lama sapaktani! Manaaya: Nluku aka! Nluku aka! Ukihiyenreni veekhaka?
Umwiiwa waya, akina yaari wonwo, yaheera: Moone, nomwiihana Eliya!
Mmoca mwaale ahothimakaca uwiha ntthoce nooheliya makari ahotthukelela muntathini ni ahommaha wiira awurye, ni ahohimya: Noone wiira Eliya nawa unkurusela vathi.
Akhuwaka ni ncu noorunya, Yesu ahokhwa.
Vano ikuwo yo Mpani mwaNluku yahaahuwa iriyariru ukhuma uculu mpaka vathi.
Muulupale a anakhotto eemenle cooco wariyawe Yesu, umoona wawe akhwaka ciicale, aheera: Khweeli ula ari Mwana a Nluku!
Yahaawo tho athiyana yemenle uttayi amwehaka; mwaale ahaawo Mariya Mantalena, Mariya anumwane Yakopu mwankani ni Yosefi, ni Saloome.
Wariyawe Yesu uKalileya yaayo yahontthara nunvarela nteko, ni athiyana akina enci yanvelenle wakenlyawe uYerusalemu.
Wiila waya, hapo wari ukati wowiitthenkaciya nihuku nontivela,
ahowa Yosefi o Arimateya, humu oocuwanyaa ni oottitthima, akhuluvenle uwa waya omwene wa Nluku, alipile nrima wokela waPilatu ni aholepela nrutthu wa Yesu.
Ni Pilatu ahaakaaka wiiwa wawe wiira hokhwa, ni amwiihanaka muulupale anakhotto ni ahonkoha akhala wiira khwile mwakhalayi.
Ni nahimeriye ni muulupale uyo, nrutthu ahovahiya Yosefi.
Yosefi nathumile ikuwo, ahokurusa nrutthu wansalapani, ni ahokhuneela ni ikuwo eyo. Wahoolo ahommitha mmahiye yathipiye wamwalani ni ahopirikisela nluku nuulupale wankhora wo mahiye.
Mariya Mantalena, ni Mariya anumwane Yosefi yahoona nipuro navithiyawe.
Uvira waya nihuku no ntivela, Mariya Mantalena, Mariya anumwane Yakopu ni Saloome yahothuma makhura oonukhela ni yahorwaa uttikitthela nrutthu wa Yesu.
Wicisu ncuwa nikhumaka nihuku noopacera nosumana, yahorwaca umahiye.
Yanawaakaaka yiiraka: Tipani nokela unipirikisela nluku nno wankhora wo mahiye?
Nanso, awehaka, yahoona wiira nluku nopirikiseliya nceresere ni nari nluku nuulupale cinene.
Ukela waya mmahiye yahomoona mmirawo nonkomile moono nlopwana, awanre ihancu yooteela, ni yahotuthuwa.
Uyo nanso, ahaahimerya: Nhituthuwe. Nnomwavya Yesu o Nasaree akhomeliye wansalapani. Honwelela, khaawo va. Moone nipuro namweesilyaya.
Vano, murwee, mwahimerye owiitthuca awe ni Peturu wiira Yesu naahala wuhoolelani uKalileya. Wonwo nnaahala umoona toko coohimenryaweni.
Akhumaka umahiye yanatthawa ni uthukumela nlattu wo woova. Khayanhimenrye ntthu itthu ile nlattu wo woova.
Nonwelenle, wicisu aya nihuku noopacera isumana, Yesu ahonkhumelela woopacera Mariya Mantalena, yola ankumihilyawe macini saapa.
Uyo ahorwaa wacuweliha ale yakhanle ni Yesu, yeetta acukulaka ni yiikhupanyaka.
Ale nanso, wiiwa waya wiira Yesu ri nkumi, ni Mariya ahomoona, khayaakupanli.
Wahoolo aheeconeha nnanna nkina wasilopwana eeli yeetta ni iphiro, arwaaka umawaani.
Ayo yahoturuwa wiira yacuwelihe akhwaya, nanso na ayo khayaakupanli.
Wahoolo waya, ahaakhumelela owiitthuca awe khumi na mmoca alyaka, ni ahaakuphula nlattu wohikupali ni uturumala waya nrima, kontha khayaakupanli ale yamoonne nonwelenle.
Ni aheerela: Murwee ilapo yothene mwaalake atthu othene ni Nhupi Wooreera.
Ntthu nohala ukupali ni upatisiya naahala woopwa, nanso ntthu hinhala ukupali, naahala uhukhumwiya.
Ikanyero cinhala waatthara atthu ookupali phi nnya: Mwancina naka, ankowomola minepa coonanara, ankowuuluma moolumo oonaanano;
ankovara inwaa, ni yawuryaka itthu yowiiva, khinhala wapanka itthu; ammowathatela matata aretta, na ale anaahala uvona.
Vano, Apwiya Yesu anoolumanne owiitthuca awe yahakheleliya wirimu, ni ahonkoma moono nlopwana wa Nluku.
Vano arumeyi yahokhuma ni yahorwaa ulaka mapuro othene ni Apwiya yahaakavihera, yoneehaka nuulumo na Apwiya ni ikanyero cavelenle.



























































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































Mi Yakopu, ipottha ya Nluku ni ya Apwiya Yesu Krisitu, kinasalameeha mahimo khumi na meeli, amwareenle mwilaponi mothene.
Asunnaka, nkhalane utteeliya cinene wophwanyakani ukati woottehattehiya,
ncuwelaka wiira nroromelo ninyu nno nalawihiyaka phinkhalanaya nlipihero.
Nlipihero nihaana nivaraka nteko woomalela wiira nyuva nkhale oomalela, weeyiintthu ni wohihaleela itthu.
Wakhala wiira haawo hirina ankhili, anlepele Nluku, navaha atthu othene woohimatthepwa ni nawaakawa.
Nanso alepele nuuroromela woohaakanyaca; kontha ule nakanyaca ri toko mawimpi ompharyaa, ankusiya ni wuutuwanyinya ni iphyoo.
Uyo huupuwele wiira nawaakhela itthu ya Apwiya,
maana ri ntthu oohilakela ni oohilipelela iphiro cothene cineettawe.
Munnihu oothwennya atteeliye nlattu wowuunuwihiya,
ni oopuha atteeliye nlattu wowiiyeviha, kontha nacuwela wiira mahuku awe ari vakani toko ithutu contakhwani.
Ncuwa noopaka ni nivihaka, yowaaliya inawuuma, ni ithutu aya inanyaala ni ureera waya unaamala. Ciicammo, mayoopuha naakhala oonyaala mphironi mwawe.
Horeeriya ntthu noovilela waphiyaka ukati woottehattehiya; kontha, alawihiyaka, nowa uvahiya ikhwerempa yookumi, yeeyo Apwiya yaroromelihilyaya ale anafenta.
Hikhale neera, attehattehiyaka eeraka: Nluku phinkitteha. Kontha khanlamuliya uttehattehiya ni itthu yoonanara ni uyo khaawo nonttehawe.
Uhiya commo, khula ntthu nottehattehiya ni wunlela wawe citthu, vano wunlela wawe nwo wantepelaka unamooryaca.
Vano wunlela nwo wanttokotthelaka untothola itaampi; ni itaampi iyo inontothola nookhwa.
Asunnaka oofentiya, nhithepiye.
Khula ivahiya yooreera ni khula itthuvo yoomalela inkhuma wirimu, cikhuruwaka wa athumwanaya waarya, ahinrukunuwa toko mitthuuci cihirina nipuro noweemela.
Ni wootthuna wawe, ule honipattusa ni nuulumo neekhweeli, wiira nikhale nlipu nokhiyumpe cawe.
Asunnaka oofentiya, nkiiwe: Nyu ncuweleke nnya citthu nnya: ntthu phi ntthu nolamuliya ukhala owaakuva wiiwa, oohipuphela wuulumaca, ni oopica uviruwa;
kontha uviruwa wa ntthu khunphwanyiha isariya ya Nluku.
Phimaana, nhiye unyala winyu nwo ni coonanara cimpankenyu nnyo, nkuse ni imaani nuulumo niphatteeliyenyu nno, nenno nihaana ikuru cowoopola iroho cinyu.
Vano, nkhale oweettela nuulumo, nhimakele wiiwa paahi, mwithepyaka veekhenyu.
Kontha, ntthu eewaka nuulumo nno ni heettelaka, nolikana toko ntthu neewehera waloolani, oonaka ikhove awe yeephattuwelo.
Wahoolo neewehenrene naathama, ni wowaakuvyaca naaliyala weenryaya ikhove awe iyo.
Nanso ule nohelelela aviriyanaka nlamulo noomalela, nlamulo nowoopola, akhanyereraka weettela, wohiira wiiwa nuuhiya, nanso woorya uvarela nteko, ula ntthu ula nokhala ooreerihiya mpaka ni nteko umpankawe uyo.
Ntthu eehelaka ukhala nattiini, ahiyaka ulokiha nlimi nawe, nanso phiithepyaka, ittiini awe iyo iri yo mahala.
Ittiini yomaana ni yeekhweeli inoncivela Nluku Athumwanihu, phi ila: Waathotola akhwaacuni ni minankhwele ukati unhuvaaya ni wiisunka omwaneene woohinyala toko cineettiyaya ntuniyani.
Asunnaka, nakupaliki Apwiya ehu Yesu Kirisitu aneene uttitthima, nihaahiyaniheke atthu ayo.
Phimaana, awaaka ntthu mapuro anthukumanenyu, oonwara nnela owooru mmakokhoni mmo, nawaracile ikuwo comaana, wahoolo phikelaka tho ntthu nkina oohuva ni oothaaleliya,
vano phaahawulanihaka wowaakhelela vaa, ni phimwiirelaka oowaraca ikuwo comaana uyo: Nyu vaa, mmweke mowunkomeke va nipuro noolemela nuuphwanenleeni. Vano oohuva uyo phimwiirelaka: We, weemeleke vaa, atthuna uweke wawonkomeke waryaka va.
Mwapankaka ciicammo nheehawulaniha ayaayoru ni nheepanka mayahukhumu owuupuwela coonanara.
Nkiiwe, asunnaka oofentiya: Nluku haathanla atthu owooninya uhuva mwilaponi wiira akhale athaaciri muukupalini ni akhale mayoophwanya umwene wo wirimu waalupelenlyawe ale anonfenta.
Nanso, nyu akina vaa, nnawannyohola mayoohuva. Khaanakhala athaaciri phinootulumuni? Khaanakhala yaayo phinoorwanani upwaroni onoolumiya milattu?
Khaanakhala yaayo phinnyohola ncina nomaana ninromoleliyeenyu?
Nyu mweettela malamulo o omwene wa Nluku, mwanapanka toko cinhimyaya cowantikhiya: Unfente nkhwaa toko cineefentaa umwaneene, unapanka yooreera.
Nanso, mwaahiyanihaka atthu nnopanka itaampi, ni nnaahala uhukhumwinya ni malamulo toko mayootthekaca.
Ule noorya weettela malamulo othene, nanso phivonyanihaka nipuro nimoca, nalikeleliya ukosera othene.
Phimaana, ule eenre: Nheette uluva, ciicammo holamula eeraka: Nhiive. Vano, waheetteke uluva, nanso unawiiva, unkhala ntthu oovonyiha nlamulo.
Toko cineerenyu ni cinoolumacenyu, mpankeke ciicammo ncuwelaka wiira nnohala uhukhumwinya ni nlamulo nowiithawala.
Kontha ule hirina ikiriri naahala uhukhumwinya wohi ikiriri. Ikiriri cinatthema ihukhumu.
Asunnaka, nohala uphurani ntthu neera: Mi kihaana nroromelo nanso woohivarela nteko? Unoona wiira nenno nroromelo nno khaninoopola.
Akhala wiira mwamunninyu atthuna mwanrokorinyu hothaaleliya atthuna hovoliya itala yo khula nihuku,
ni mmoca wa nyu phimwiirelaka: Urweke ni mpuha, wawareke ni walyeke womaana, wohinvaha imphavelawe; mpankileni yooreera?
Ciicammo, nroromeloru paahi, noohivareliya nteko, ninkhala nookhwa.
Vano haawo nohala wiira: We uhaana nroromelo, ni mi kihaana miteko. Ukithoonyere nroromelo naa noohimiteko ni mi kinawuthonyera nroromelo naka ni miteko caka.
We unakupali wiira ri Nluku mmoca paahi. Wahoreera! Ciicammo asotwani anakupali ni anattettemela!
We, oomphuku! Khuncuwela wiira nroromelo noohivareliya nteko khanirina icaayira?
Aparahamu athumwanihu ookhalayii, khayaavahiye isariya nlattu wo miteko waanvaherenraaya mwanaya Isaki wanipuroni noosataka.
Vano wooneke wiira nroromelo ni miteko cineetta wamoca, ni nroromelo nimaliheriya ni miteko.
Coo phitthariheleliyaya yowantikhiya yiiraka: Aparahamu honkupali Nluku ni hoheeliya ukhala nasariya, ni uyo heehaninya mpwanawe Nluku.
Mooneke wiira ntthu novahiya isariya nlattu wo miteko, woohikhala nroromeloru.
Wanlikana toko puuta Rahapi; waavahiyawe isariya nlattu wopanka yooreera, aavahaka nipuro atthu oohottela ni wathonyera iphiro ikina.
Ciicammo irutthu yohiroho inkhala yookhwa, philikanaya nroromelo nohikhalana coopankiya ninkhala nookhwa.
Asunnaka, nhunlele ukhala othene mayoosomiha, maana nhocuwela wiira hii, nineetthuciha, phi hii ninkela utepa uhukhumwiya.
Othene ninakosa wo mananna oovirikana. Ntthu aahikoseke nlattu wo wuulumaca, uyo ri nttuntthu, ciicammo nawoorya usunka irutthu awe yothene.
Nahelelaka iyuma malaku okhavalu wiira ciniiwelele, ciicammo ninawoorya weettiha irutthu aya yothene.
Nthonyero enyu ukhale wokalawa; cinookhalaru cuulupale ni cittinkihiyaka ni iphyoo cuulupale, cineettihiya ni ileemi yankani cinene, toko cintthunawe nocika.
Ni ciicammo phinlikanaya, nlimi waryaya itthu yankani iri mwiirutthuni, ninawiittottopa nlattu woopanka citthu cuulupale. Nkoonani, itakhwa yuulupale impariheliyaya ni mooro mwankani.
Phi ciicammo, nlimi nihu niri mooro; nlimi niri ituniya yotaampi. Ninaheliyeene iriyari yorutthu ihu ninaannanariha irutthu yothene, ninaparihela makhalelo ookumi, ni mpaka ni nno ninapariheliya omooroni.
Phimaana ikhapila cothene conama, coovava, cowiipurula ni compharyaa cinasinnttiya ni cinsinnttiya na atthu,
nanso nlimi khaawo ntthu noorya usinntta. Niri noonanara woohimala ni noocara nrette wo wiiva.
Ni nenno, ninanttitthimiha Pwiya Athumwanihu; ciicammo ninawaalapha atthu, apattusiye oolattana ni Nluku.
Malaku mamoca yaayo paahi, inakhuma iparakha ni ikilapho. Asunnaka, khavanreera wiira citthu nnya cikhaleke coo.
Uhopaca woona waluusi akhumaka maasi oociva na ayo ootumpurya nipuro nimoca nenno?
Asunnaka, nrale uhopaca wiima maphepu atthuna mphepu wiima nrale? Hata vakani, khawanoorya iluusi yo maasi ootumpurya ukhuma maasi oociva.
Tipani iriyari inyu ri aankhili ni oocuwelaca? Aathonyihere makhalelo omaana nuupisa nrima wa ankhili.
Waahikhaleke commo, munrimani mwinyu mmo nhaana urama wootepa ni wiihelela, vano nhiittottope ni nhoothe nveehaka ikhweeli.
Ala ankhili ala, khaankhuma wirimu, nanso ari omwiilaponi moomu; khaanakhala o munnepani, nanso asotwani.
Phimaana nipuro niri uramana ni wiihelela, ciri iporonka ni coonanara cinci.
Nanso ankhili ankhuma wirimu ari ooreera, osalaama, onnema, eemaani ni oocara ikiriri, ookumiha mihokorokho comaana, oohihawulaniha ni oohiithepya.
Ni wosalaama phinwiihaya isalaama ale anaala nhokorokho wosariya.
Cinkhumelela vayi ikhotto nnyo ni waanaca winyu ayaayoru nwo? Cinkhuma nkhwiluni cinaana mwirutthuni mwinyu mmo.
Nnakhalela nttima ca akhwinyu ni khannophwanya. Nnawiiva ni nnarama nanso khannophwanya. Makhalelo enyu ari owiiva ni waana ikhotto. Nnavekela nanso khannakhela, kontha khannovekela ratta.
Nnophavela mwaphwanyaka nrihakaceleke nkhwiluni mwinyu mmo.
Nyu mayooluva, khannocuwela wiira upatthanana ituniya unkhala mwiinani awe Nluku? Ule nophavela ukhala mpwana awe ituniya, neepanka mwiinani a Nluku.
Atthuna nnoona wiira waari wopure cihimilyaya cowantikhiya ciiraka: Nnepa univahilyawe wiira ukhale ni hii uhaana ihace?
Nanso uyo nanivaha nnema nuulupale. Phimaana cowantikhiya ciiraka: Nluku nawaarusanana owiittottopa nanso nawaavaha nnema oowiyeviha.
Phimaana, mmwiiwelele Nluku. Munkhottele sotwani ni uyo phinhalawe wuutthawani.
Mphiyeke wa Nluku, ni uyo phinhalawe wuuphiyerani! Anataampi, nnyaweke ni nrapiheke nrima, nyu anamirima miili.
Ncukuleke ni muunleke. Mwakakhaniheke uthyaa ni wunla, utteeliya ni ucukula.
Mwiiyevihe wa miithoni wa Apwiya ni ayo phinhalaya uwunnuwihani.
Asunnaka, nhaapanane. Ule nomwaapa munnaawe atthuna unhukhumu munnaawe, noolumacera yoonanara ni nohukhumu malamulo. We wamakelaka uhukhumu malamulo, khuneettela, nanso wiyeesile ukhala mayoohukhumu.
Nlamuli ni hukhumu ri mmoca paahi, yoole noorya woopola nuukwanyula. Vano we, tipani oonhukhumu nkhwaa?
Vano nviriyane, nyu nneeresa: Ilelo atthuna meelo, ninaarwa iparasa yonese, ni ninkookhala mwakha mmoca nimweettaka nakoso nuuphwanya nhakhu.
Nyu khancuwenle itthu inhala wuukhumelelani meelo. Ukumi inyu uyo unookhala isiyani? Nyu nri toko itthapwe inkhuma ni ukati vakani inamwaryaca.
Uhiya wuulumaca commo, fatari wiira: Apwiya yatthunaka ni anivahaka ukumi, ninapanka ila ni ile.
Nanso, nna, nnasamela citthu cinoopuwelenyu upanka. Wiisamiha toko coo inkhala itthu yoonanara.
Phimaana muupuwele ratta: Ule nocuwela wiira nolamuliya upanka yooreera, pihipankaka, naakosa.
Vano nviriyane, nyu mathaaciri! Ncukule ni munle mwanlattu wo mahuviho anhala wuphwanyani.
Mihakhu cinyu nnyo, ikuwo cinyu ni coolya cinyu, cihontta ni ciholiya ikuttihi.
Iwooru inyu ni ipheeta enyu cihonyela urenci. Vano urenci uyo phinhala ukhala saahiti owuuttonkani ni wuulalihani toko waneerihaya mooro. Nyu nhothacirera mahuku oomalela.
Mooneke. Ncurukhu wa ananteko yoorula mmattani mwinyu ayo, nhaalivaka, unakhuwela wuttonkakani nyenyu vaa. Wiikhupanya wa anakanyari uhophiya mpaka mmanyaruni mwa Apwiya a anakhotto.
Nyu nheetta mpuhaka ni nhovolela ikhwilu cothene cucivenleni vathi va. Nhorittimalihera mirima cinyu nnyo nihuku noohitiya.
Nnanhukhumu nuumwiiva nasariya, wohiwiirihani itthu.
Phimaana asunnaka, nkhale oovilela, mpaka wanhalaya uwa Apwiya. Kinawoona mayoolima navilela awehereryaka yoolya yo mmattani, mpaka wammwaya ipula coopacera ni coomalihera.
Ciicammo nyu nkhale oovilela ni oolipa nrima, kontha uwa wa Apwiya uri wakhiviru.
Asunnaka, nhittokuttani ayaayoru wiira nhihukhumwinye. Hukhumu uyo ri wankhora!
Asunnaka, niwehere minapiyu coolumaca mwa ncina na Apwiya, ciinryaya woohuva nuuvilela.
Kinawoona nineerela ahoreeriya ale yiisunkile ni uvilela. Nnawiiwaka uvilela wa Yopi ni nhoona yaceenryaya. Apwiya ari oocara uthunku ni ikiriri.
Asunnaka, hata mwiirihiye cani, nhilupele nromolaka wirimu, atthuna vathi va, ni hata itthu phi itthu iheliye nhilupelele. Yakhalaka khweeli, mwiireke khweeli, yakhalaka mena, mena, wiira nhihukhumwinye.
Wariyari winyu vaa haawo nohuva? Aswaliki. Haawo tteeliye? Eepeke icipo coolemeliha.
Wariyari winyu vaa haawo nowerennya? Arume urweliya ahooleli okereeca, wiira yoonswalele ni anttikitthele makhura, mwancina na Apwiya.
Iswali yowaamini navona nretta ni Apwiya anaanwusa; ni wakhala wiira nookosa, naleveleliya.
Phimaana, nlaphulule itaampi cinyu nnyo waakhwinyu ni nswalelaneke wiira nvonihiye. Ulapa wa nasariya uhaana ikuru yoolipa.
Eliya aari ntthu, oolikana makhalelo ayo toko hii. Ule ahoswali venci wiira ihirupe ipula, ni khweeli ilapo yothene khayaarupile ipula mpaka umala myakha miraru ni nuuso.
Ahaakulela tho uswali, vano irimu yahovaha ipula vathi nuumela mihokorokho.
Asunnaka, wariyari winyu vaa akhalaka ntthu hiile ikhweeli, vano aturuselihiyaka ni nkhwawe,
ncuwele wiira ule nonturusiha nataampi warukurerya cawe, nawoopola iroho awe wuukhwani ni cinakhuneelya itaampi cinci.
